  • Chapter 1950 - The Indestructible Lord has added you as a friend

Eight bee-sized bundles of light danced on Song Shuhang’s palm, twirling happily around his fingers.

Fairy Blue Phoenix had put a lot of thought into these “common” gifts, making sure that they would match each other well—the cultivation technique with the pills, and the gemstone fruit seeds with the little monster beasts.

All of these four things were things that Song Shuhang needed.

The only thing he was feeling rather regretful about was that there were no spirit stones.

Of course, Song Shuhang was still satisfied with the gifts that Fairy Blue Phoenix had prepared and given him.

“I like these treasures very much. It can even be said that each of them are things I’m in urgent need of.” Song Shuhang showed a sincere smile, and after thinking about it, he added, “Fairy Blue Phoenix, if the pandemic in the Beast Realm becomes too grave such that the medicinal liquid and the infection mitigation plan are no longer sufficient to handle it, then you can gather people together and call me. I’ll make a trip to the Beast Realm and try to cure as many of them as possible.”

The fat ball had cast a wide net over the Beast Realm, infecting a lot of people with the evil energy of the Netherworld. However, while this might be a headache for the Beast Realm, they were all treasures for Song Shuhang.

The evil energy of the Netherworld in the infected bodies came from the fat ball, so it was extremely pure. Extracting it through the lotus projection and transferring it into the Inner World to convert it into pure energy should allow the Inner World to level up.

More importantly, when each patient came for treatment, he could ask them to come with a medical fee. This was how Song Shuhang had collected most of the materials for his Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure.

“Really?” When Fairy Blue Phoenix heard his words, an elated expression emerged on her face. “In fact, those with severe symptoms have already been gathered together so that we may attend to them more easily. If Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song has the time... Why don’t you make a trip to the Beast Realm now? Or else, we can transfer those patients to a secure independent space for Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song to go to.”

The Beast Realm had been researching ways to purify the evil energy of the Netherworld recently-however, it had quickly become apparent to them that the evil energy that they were dealing with was different from before, and this was because the evil energy of the Netherworld that appeared in the Beast Realm had come straight from the fat ball. As such, the methods that the Beast Realm had previously used in dealing with the evil energy, such as magical techniques and medicinal pills, were much less effective this time around.

During this period, they had gathered together some of the more seriously infected patients into specific areas...

There were nearly 1,000 such camps in the territory of the Divine Phoenix Nation, which was where Fairy Blue Phoenix was situated.

“Now?” Song Shuhang scratched his head. He had been planning to head to the scholarly faction.

Su Clan’s Sixteen pondered for a moment, and then said, “Shuhang, why don’t you try to create a ‘transfer station’ in your Inner World, and let Fairy Blue Phoenix and those from the Beast Realm transfer the patients directly to your Inner World?”

Song Shuhang nodded, and said, “Good idea, let me try that.”

He sent his consciousness into the Inner World, and contacted the Inner World Assistant.

The Inner World Assistant immediately responded, “Good afternoon, Mr. Tyrannical Song. What are your orders today?”

Song Shuhang relayed Sixteen’s suggestion to the Inner World Assistant.

After considering the suggestion for a short while, the Inner World Assistant replied, “No problem, Mr. Tyrannical Song. Please wait a moment.”

After a few minutes, the Inner World Assistant and the virtuous lamia came to a consensus.

Afterward, the Virtuous Palace was extracted and placed in a corner of the Inner World to be used as a transit station.

The virtuous lamia did not care about her Virtuous Palace at all. In fact, she had not returned to her Virtuous Palace until now. For some reason, she kept on feeling like avoiding her own palace, but she did not know why.

The Inner World Assistant replied, “The structure is complete, Mr. Tyrannical Song. Next, you can open an entrance to the Virtuous Palace’s location. The defense mechanism of the Virtuous Palace will be activated, effectively preventing any of the patients from escaping the palace and damaging the Inner World.” Ever since the Inner World Assistant came to his Inner World, the place had become tidier and more organized by the day. In the past, when he was operating the Inner World, he would have to use his consciousness to control everything. Now, with one command, the Inner World Assistant could do what he wanted to be done perfectly.

This kind of “small world assistant” was a must-have treasure for every big shot who had their own private world!

Song Shuhang said, “You’ve done well.”

The Inner World Assistant replied, “For the service of the people.”

“...” Song Shuhang. What’s with that answer?

Song Shuhang’s consciousness exited the Inner World.

Fairy Blue Phoenix and the two girls behind her looked at him expectantly.

Song Shuhang nodded slightly, and said, “Fairy, let’s go look for a suitable place first. After that, I’ll give you some spatial coordinates, and you can transfer the patients in batches. How many of your patients are in urgent need of treatment?”

“The number is very large,” Fairy Blue Phoenix replied. “The ordinary methods of purifying the evil energy of the Netherworld have a very limited effect on the patients. Also, the number of patients is only increasing.” Song Shuhang said, “Then let’s start with those who are severely ill. You can transfer those patients who are about to fall and become demons first. At the same time, Fairy, you can distribute the medicinal liquid and the method over in the Beast Realm.”

His strength had improved a lot compared to when he had last gone to the Beast Realm. Moreover, the Inner World had also been upgraded once since then. As such, his efficiency at drawing and absorbing the evil energy of the Netherworld would be much faster this time.

After some thought, Song Shuhang asked, “By the way, will transferring the patients over cost a lot?”

Spatial teleportation was the ability of Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcenders. If one did not have the help of a Tribulation Transcender, it would be necessary to use a teleportation formation to move across space, and a teleportation formation was something that consumed a lot of spirit stones.

If it would take a lot of spirit stones, then Song Shuhang felt that he should go to the Beast Realm to save on spirit stones.

When a person was lacking spirit stones, they would naturally try to save as much as they could.

Fairy Blue Phoenix said, “We can open a temporary spatial passage between the Beast Realm and the Earth. With that, we can transfer patients rather stably, and the price will not be that high.”

Song Shuhang said, “Then, while I still have some time, we can try something else first. We can try transferring the patients directly to a palace I prepared.”

Song Shuhang, Sixteen, and Fairy Blue Phoenix rode the Divine Lobster’s Chariot to the suburbs of the Jiangnan area. They went to this sparsely populated area so as to avoid disturbing people.

Song Shuhang opened the Inner World, and opened an entrance to the Virtuous Palace.

Fairy Blue Phoenix contacted the members of Beast Realm’s Divine Phoenix Kingdom, and told them to construct a temporary spatial passage linked to the entrance of Song Shuhang’s Virtuous Palace.

The Beast Realm operated extremely quickly.

Half an hour later, the first batch of severely infected people was transferred over through this temporary spatial passage.

These infected people were of various races, and there were about 200 of them in total.

Affected by the evil energy of the Netherworld, their bodies were already showing signs of demonization. The Netherworld’s evil energy twirled around their bodies, and each patient’s eyes were red. Their sense of reasoning was also close to collapsing. In their ears, there was a hushed voice corrupting their minds.

The patients looked like they would fall and demonize at any moment now.

As soon as they appeared, they were scratching and tearing their own throats as they began to roar.

But before they could completely roar, a suction force was generated in the Virtuous Palace, and all the demons fell into the palace like dumplings.

After the first batch of patients was transferred, Song Shuhang closed the exit of the Inner World.

Song Shuhang said, “Sixteen, you stay here with Fairy Blue Phoenix and the others. I’ll go in first. I’ll be back shortly.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen nodded. “Okay, be careful.”

Song Shuhang smiled, and said, “Don’t worry, in my world, I have complete control.”

After saying that, he entered the Inner World.

The defense of the Virtuous Palace was fully activated, firmly trapping the infected patients inside it.

Because the power of virtue had a certain restraining effect on the evil energy of the Netherworld, after being locked inside the Virtuous Palace, the infected patients became restless and kept on roaring.

Song Shuhang stepped on a black lotus, and arrived on top of the Virtuous Palace. He then raised his right hand, and summoned a giant lotus projection. “Maximum power.”

He wanted to test out how many of the infected patients he could cure at once.

With the urging of his thoughts, thousands of lotus roots emerged from the giant lotus projection and drilled into the Virtuous Palace. The lotus roots then penetrated into the bodies of the infected patients with great precision. It had already been a long time since the Inner World had last had a meal, so when it began absorbing, it did so avariciously, fattening itself up in one go.

After about 10 breaths of time...

As the evil energy of the Netherworld in the bodies of the patients was drawn out too quickly, the infected patients had been sucked dry like a mummy. They were dry and skinny, lying on the ground as they gasped for air.

Song Shuhang was taken aback, and his consciousness quickly swept over the over 200 infected patients.

Fortunately, although they were currently in a weakened state, they were all still alive.

Once they went back and ate some supplements, they should be able to return to their peak condition.

The roots of the lotus projection slowly receded from the infected. At the same time, the Inner World started operating quickly, transforming the large amounts of pure evil energy into its own energy.

After the evil energy was transformed, it was separated into four portions.

A portion of the pure energy was set aside for the evolution of the Inner World; another portion was turned into the spring water of the Living Spring; another portion was turned into spiritual energy that filled the Inner World; and the last portion was sent back to Song Shuhang

With the pure spiritual energy being fed back to him from the Inner World, the seven small Spirit Lakes in Song Shuhang’s body unceasingly expanded and strengthened themselves.

A refreshing feeling overcame his entire body. He felt as if he were drinking a cold beverage on a hot day as he felt comfortable all over.

Song Shuhang guessed, “At this rate, after absorbing dozens of batches of this equally pure evil energy of the Netherworld, perhaps my small Spirit Lakes can move on to Laketop Life Wheels?”

Meanwhile...

After being supplied with energy, new spring water unceasingly emerged from within the Living Spring

Rich spiritual energy, centered on the Living Spring, spread out across the entire Inner World.

The monster beasts called that were accompanying Song Shuhang cheered as they continuously conveyed their thoughts to him.

They hoped that Song Shuhang would allow them to plant the gemstone fruit seeds.

If possible, they wished to plant the gemstone fruit seeds near the Living Spring. There was an area there that the Inner World Assistant had set aside for the future planting of spirit plants.

The spirit plants transplanted from the Black Dragon World occupied less than one-tenth of this fertile land. In addition, since a lot of the spirit plants that had been acquired from the Black Dragon World required special terrain or conditions, most of them were distributed all over the Inner World. Everything had been slowly done by the Inner World Assistant, Lady Onion, and Senior Turtle. When Chu Chu came to the Inner World from time to time, she would help out as well.

Song Shuhang relayed the idea of the little clusters of light to the Inner World Assistant.

The Inner World Assistant nodded quickly, and replied, “No problem, Mr. Tyrannical Song. That plot of land is currently idle and wasting away; if there are any spirit plants that can be planted in that area, then that will be a great use for both the plants and the land.”

“Great! Alright, little guys, follow the instructions of the Inner World Assistant. It will designate where you can plant the gemstone fruit seeds.” Song Shuhang waved his hand lightly and transferred the box of seeds into the Inner World.

The little clusters of light danced happily around his fingers, and entered the Inner World along with the box. After that, they began working hard, picking up the seeds and flying to the fertile, spiritual-energy-filled land.

Earlier, Fairy Blue Phoenix said that the gemstone fruit was a spirit plant with great adaptability, and that it could survive in most environments. However, the stronger the spiritual energy in the area where it was planted, the faster it would grow, and the more fruit it would bear.

Now, after absorbing the evil energy of the Netherworld from the over 200 infected patients, the spiritual energy around the Living Spring was so rich that it was almost as thick as mist.

The eight little clusters of light planted the seeds of the gemstone fruit. After a short while, little sprouts emerged from the ground.

The little clusters of light did not plant all the seeds in one go. They stopped after planting 80 of them.

As there was only a limited number of them, they would have a difficult time managing them if they planted them all in one go. If Song Shuhang wanted them to plant more gemstone fruits in the future, he would have to wait for their population to increase first.

Afterward, they started watering and fertilizing the plants.

The water they used was a mixture of the water from the Living Spring and from five of the Heavenly City’s fragments. As for the fertilizer... They used what was available in the Thirty-Three Divine Beast Department’s toilet.

This toilet, which had been idle for millions of years, had finally come into use again.

Updates by . com

Song Shuhang could see that the invisible sword insects that Senior White had brought into the Inner World, as well as his invisible saber insect, had gone down to guide the magical beasts and spirit beasts with lower intelligence, neatly arranging them into teams to go to the toilet.

There were jet-black three-eyed canine magical beasts, two-headed orangutan-shaped magical beasts, strange magical beasts with sheep and lion heads, winged flying snakes, and bull-like magical beasts with bodies trickling with lightning. There were also some docile spirit beasts that would neatly arrange themselves into groups, entering the toilet one at a time.

As for the magical beasts and spirit beasts with relatively higher intelligence, they would take the initiative to enter the toilet through another entrance.

In the end, this magical treasure that was the Divine Beast Department’s toilet was activated, and large amounts of fertilizers were produced every few hours.

The entire process was very efficient.

Back in the era of the Ancient Heavenly City, the toilet’s function was to provide fertilizer for the Heavenly City’s spirit plant garden.

Under the guidance of the Inner World Assistant, the little bee-sized clusters of light came back with bags of fertilizer to fertilize the spirit plants. While the bee-sized clusters of light were small in size, they were actually quite strong

The two sides cooperated exceptionally well.

With the irrigation of superb water and fertilizer, the gemstone fruit trees grew rapidly. Green branches and buds began to emerge on the trees at a speed visible to the naked eye.

“Unfortunately, once a cultivator or monster cultivator reaches a certain realm of strength, they would no longer need to rid themselves of any waste,” Song Shuhang muttered as he pinched his chin. Otherwise, if Senior Turtle went to the toilet, then wouldn’t they be able to acquire Immortal-level fertilizer? That would definitely be exceptionally effective, right?

And there’s also Pavilion Master Chu...

Cough, forget that, she only has a head right now, and maybe some parts of her collarbone and shoulders.

“Mr. Tyrannical Song, these little spirits and I are very compatible.” At this time, the Inner World Assistant floated to Song Shuhang’s side. It actively praised the eight little clusters of light. “Compared with the invisible sword insects, they are much better trained.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

He had initially thought that the invisible sword insects had gone to work on their own initiative, but they had actually been trained by the Inner World Assistant?

The Inner World Assistant asked, “Mr. Tyrannical Song, before you find spirit plant masters and beast taming masters, can you let these eight spirits stay and help me?”

Song Shuhang smiled slightly. “These eight spirits have come to help with growing the gemstone fruits. They will be living in the Inner World from now on, so they can help you if needed, just try not to tire them too much.”

The Inner World Assistant nodded. “Order confirmed.”

“Then, while there’s still some time, I will store up some more energy in the Inner World.” Song Shuhang’s thoughts shifted, and he transferred the over 200 beast cultivators who had been drained of evil energy out of the Virtuous Palace and out of the Inner World.

The over 200 skinny beast cultivators were transferred to China, in the main world.

Song Shuhang’s figure immediately appeared before them.

In the air, Sixteen and Fairy Blue Phoenix sat on the Divine Lobster’s Chariot, but the two girls who were behind the fairy maiden earlier were nowhere to be seen. They had probably gone back to the Beast Realm with the medicinal liquid recipe and the infection mitigation plan.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, is the treatment over yet?” Fairy Blue Phoenix gently jumped off the chariot. “I’ve already expelled the evil energy in their bodies. Now, they only need to be supplemented with some nutrients, and they should soon be back to normal,” Song Shuhang replied, and added, “In addition, while the spatial passage is still here, you can transfer the next batch of patients. We need to make use of this time when I’m in a great condition to cure as many of them as possible.”

Fairy Blue Phoenix said, “Thank you, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.”

Under her lead, the second batch of patients was transferred in the same way.

At the same time, the first batch of beast cultivators was transferred back to the Beast Realm.

The second batch of patients was in an even worse state than the first.

When they were transferred to the main world, several of them even began to struggle, and tried to escape.

Song Shuhang frowned slightly. After thinking for a while, his left eye suddenly lit up... The Expert’s Appraisal landed on the person who was the rowdiest.

“Aaaaah-” The infected patient let out a miserable scream.

He was not immune to Expert’s Appraisal.

Along with that scream of pain, he fell into the Virtuous Palace.

While he was falling toward the palace, he let out another heart-wrenching scream. “T-Tyrannical Song!”

With this scream, the infected who were roaring violently seemed to recall a painful memory in their minds. Instantly, all of them calmed down.

In the next moment, they obediently jumped into the Virtuous Palace one by one.

“Eh?” Su Clan’s Sixteen, who was on the chariot, suddenly let out a soft sound.

Her eyes fell on a petite figure with an armor-like carapace. The petite figure seemed to have sensed her gaze and turned her head to look at Sixteen.

ee

After a while, the petite figure suddenly moved. Just before she was about to fall into the Virtuous Palace, she rushed out, and a bone sword emerged from her hand.

Holding the sword with both of her hands, she swung it fiercely at Sixteen.

“Come back!” Song Shuhang stretched out his hand. He urged his psychic energy, and was about to forcibly pull the petite figure back.

Su Clan’s Sixteen said, “Shuhang, wait... Leave her to me!” Sixteen seemed to recognize this petite figure.

Su Clan’s Sixteen said solemnly, “I’ll deal with this quickly.”

After saying that, she jumped off the Divine Lobster’s Chariot. The baseball cap she was wearing on her head flew off, revealing her little dragon horns; arcs of lightning flickered on them.

Above her head, a black cloud silently condensed.

Behind her, her life-bound treasured saber took the initiative to leave her and slash at the petite figure.

Boom~

The saber was accompanied by violent explosions of lightning as it flew through the air. A bolt of lightning descended from the dark cloud above, landing on Su Clan’s Sixteen’s sword. The lightning bolt flickered and wrapped around the treasured saber like a snake while loud crackling sounds echoed.

The power of lightning combined with the saber light, creating a giant, five-meter-long saber qi, which then went on to fiercely slash at the petite figure.

The petite figure did not show any fear. She firmly grabbed the huge bone sword with both of her hands, and then slammed it straight toward the lightning saber.

The lightning from the saber coursed through her body, but any damage that it would have done was blocked by the carapace-like armor that covered her skin.

Clang!

When the bone sword collided with Su Clan’s Sixteen’s treasured saber, a clanging sound that one would hear when metal collided with metal rang out.

Su Clan’s Sixteen shouted, “Imperial Saber!”

On her life-bound treasured saber, a hidden power suddenly burst out.

The petite figure let out a smothered cry, and was sent flying backward.

She quickly tucked herself in the air so that she could tumble and reduce the impact on her body.

However, the saber had no reason to wait for her to accomplish what she wanted. The saber sent her smashing toward the ground, creating a huge pit in the ground.

With how big the pit was, it was likely that Senior White’s Ground Leveling Spell would be needed in order to return the ground to its original state.

This was the first time that Song Shuhang had seen Sixteen launch a full-on frontal attack. She was unexpectedly fierce!

Her saber technique had been handed down by Seven, and it was not very suitable for females to practice. However, as it was performed by Sixteen, who had awakened her dragon bloodline, it suited her pretty well. She could unleash considerable might when she used it.

A few moments later, the petite figure jumped out of the pit. The jet-black carapace-like armor that covered her body was in tatters, revealing patches of white skin underneath. Meanwhile, the huge bone sword in her hand was now missing some pieces, and was charred completely.

“Ptui.”

It seems like she spat just now. But wait, since she was wearing a helmet, if she really did spit, did she spit in her helmet...?

She reached out and grabbed the shattered carapace around her body, then ripped it off, tossing it to the side.

Underneath the carapace, she was wearing a thin coat.

She had a flat-chested physique.

At this time, Elder Sister White Dragon gently floated over to Song Shuhang’s side.

Song Shuhang said curiously, “Eh? Elder Sister White Dragon, why did you come over here?”

Elder Sister White Dragon should be in a similar state to that of the virtuous lamia, and logically speaking, she was a part of Sixteen’s body. Sixteen said that she did not want anyone to interfere, and Elder Sister White Dragon was a part of her, so why did she run over here?

Elder Sister White Dragon said slowly, “Don’t worry, I’m not going to intervene.”

Song Shuhang asked, “What’s the background of this flat-chested little girl? Does Sixteen know her?”

/

As soon as he said that, the petite girl and Sixteen froze.

At this time, one should have seized the weakness shown by the opponent to immediately launch an attack. Unfortunately, both Sixteen and the petite girl were stiff, so the opportunity was missed.

“You should go to the Virtuous Palace and treat the infected patients. I can keep watch of Sixteen,” said Elder Sister White Dragon gently—she felt that it would be better for Song Shuhang to leave for the moment.

Song Shuhang said, “It’s fine. There’s no need to go through so much trouble for that.”

The Inner World was his territory.

He only needed to transmit a thought to summon the lotus projection above the Virtuous Palace. Afterward, with another thought, he could have the lotus projection send countless roots to penetrate the bodies of the second batch of patients and quickly drain the evil energy infecting their bodies.

When they saw the transparent, tentacle-looking roots penetrate their bodies, the infected patients struggled fearfully.

However, there was nowhere for them to hide. They were inevitably pierced by the millions of lotus roots that extended into the Virtuous Palace and filled the entire venue.

The infected patients watched on in despair as the tentacles entered their bodies. As the evil energy was sucked from their bodies, they were greatly weakened.

They became so weak that they could not even utter a groan.

In the end, even their consciousness became faint, and they all fell unconscious.

The only exception was the infected patient who had been hit by the Expert’s Appraisal. While he also wanted to pass out, his mind was in a very sober state—the pain of childbirth prevented him from falling unconscious, only adding to the despair he was feeling.

Similar to the previous time, after the evil energy of the Netherworld was extracted from the batch of patients, all of the energy was separated into four portions.

A steady surge of new spring water emerged in the Living Spring, while the Inner World became even more filled with spiritual energy. Along with that, the growth of the gemstone fruits and other spirit plants sped up once more.

The small Spirit Lakes in Song Shuhang’s body also grew a bit more.

Elder Sister White Dragon could not help but shift her gaze and look at Song Shuhang...

He’s just standing still, yet the energy in his body has begun to rise sharply once more. Is he going to increase his realm again? Elder Sister White Dragon thought to herself—she always felt that Song Shuhang was running a race when it came to raising one’s realm. It felt as if it would be too late should he be lagging behind by a step in increasing his cultivation.

Just what was he chasing, though?

Elder Sister White Dragon shook her head slightly again—honestly, there was probably nothing forcing him to increase his cultivation at such speeds.

“Aah~ How refreshing~” Song Shuhang spat out a long breath.

This feeling is addictive.

I just wonder whether this feedback of energy from the Inner World or the ❮Saber-Nurturing Technique❯ feels better...

At the same time, he silently circulated the ❮Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique❯, enhancing the effects of the small Spirit Lakes. He had already become used to his strength skyrocketing.

Every time the energy in his body increased, he only needed to circulate his cultivation technique a few times, and he would quickly be able to adapt to his newfound strength.

He stretched out his hand and waved lightly. With that, the second batch of patients was transferred out of the Inner World.

Fairy Blue Phoenix, who was right next to him, cooperated with him, and sent the batch of patients back to the Beast Realm while transferring the third batch of infected patients over at the same time.

The third batch of infected patients emerged from the spatial passage.

As soon as they appeared, Song Shuhang turned his head sharply, and fixed his eyes on the tallest and strongest among them. Without hesitation, he used the Expert’s Appraisal.

When a group of troublesome people came before you, if you immediately dealt with the strongest person among them, then there was an over 50% chance that it would be enough to act as a deterrent and suppress the entire group... Unless the strongest among them was a poser.

The reason why Song Shuhang chose to do this was because it worked very well.

Amidst terrified screams of people shouting and crying out “T-Tyrannical Song,” the third batch of infected patients also quickly became obedient just like the previous batch, and silently lined up to jump into the Virtuous Palace.

It was a simple and efficient system.

❄️❄️❄️

Song Shuhang shifted his gaze back to the battlefield, and watched the battle between Sixteen and the petite girl.

The two petite figures constantly moved around and clashed with one another.

Sword and saber lights flashed, while lightning and flames constantly exploded. The speed of the two figures who were in an intense duel kept on speeding up. They would clash with one another, then move away from each other, and then repeat while sending out a constant bombardment of techniques toward their opponent.

In just a few minutes, the two had clashed nearly a thousand times.

Around Sixteen’s body, more and more electric arcs had appeared, and the electric arcs had begun to gradually condense into the figure of a true dragon behind her.

As for the petite figure she was fighting, she had somehow already condensed nearly 100 smaller bone swords.

“Ptui!” The petite figure spat again. This time, her saliva could be seen spewing out from the broken part of her helmet’s chin.

Afterward, she stretched out her hand and waved it. With that wave of her hand, the 100 or so bone swords shot toward Sixteen.

Song Shuhang sighed and said, “This move is something I used to dream of being able to do.”

He just imagined stretching out his hand to which several hundred swords would respond and fly and attack his opponents. All the while he simply stood there casually as if it wasn’t even a big deal. Just how cool would he look?

“❮Heavenly Saber Burying the Starry River❯.” Su Clan’s Sixteen held her saber with both hands, and swung it down gently. The lightning dragon behind her attached itself to the treasured saber, and moved with the saber.

The lightning dragon let out a thunderous roar. This saber slash was that of an emperor.

Behind the lightning dragon saber qi was a magnificent phantom of a starry river.

This saber move was a watered-down version of Su Clan’s Seven’s ❮Heavenly Saber Burying the Starry Sea❯ that Sixteen had adapted. However, with the combination of the lightning dragon and her own saber qi, this move was still undoubtedly powerful.

As the ❮Heavenly Saber Burying the Starry River❯ moved, the saber qi that spread caused the 100 bone swords sent out by the petite figure to shatter into smithereens.

The lightning dragon saber qi’s aura continued unabated toward the petite figure.

A loud bang could be heard, and the petite figure was swallowed by the explosion.

After a while, inside the dazzling light of the explosion, a figure was thrown out and fell toward Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang subconsciously reached out and caught her.

It was as if she was weightless.

The figure was soft and boneless, and hung softly from Song Shuhang’s arm.

Boom~

Her damaged helmet fell off, revealing short, dark-silver hair and a delicate face.

“Sixteen?” Song Shuhang stared at the little face, and was stunned for a while.

In the upper left corner of the small piece of paper, there were two marks that looked like fingerprints. Upon closer inspection, one would be able to see that these two fingerprint-looking markings were the figures of peerless powerhouses.

The left marking was the Almighty Merchant, who was huddled up inside a sheet.

The right marking was Fairy Almighty Seller, who was curled up into a ball under a sheet.

There was a contract written on the piece of paper in the language of the ancient era.

This was a new project that had been launched by the Almighty Merchant and his beloved disciple, Fairy Almighty Seller. This project was a life insurance business of sorts.

Having an insurance ticket was akin to having a single-use life-saving method with the Almighty Merchant and Fairy Almighty Seller as the guarantors.

No matter where you were, as long as your life was in danger, the two peerless powerhouses would be able to sense it instantly through the ticket. Then, depending on the level of danger, they would divide the work and send assistance.

This was an item that was almost comparable to a resurrection magical treasure.

It was especially useful for cultivators at and above the Sixth Stage.

The Sixth Stage could be considered a watershed, a pivotal stage of sorts. After reaching the Sixth Stage, the soul of a cultivator would undergo a process of sublimation. Because of this, ordinary resurrection magical treasures would no longer work on them.

Resurrection Gold Coins, Resurrection Crosses, and other similar resurrection magical treasures could only be used by cultivators at and below the Fifth Stage; they were useless starting from the True Monarch Realm.

If a Sixth Stage True Monarch wanted to be resurrected, they would generally need to prepare a huge formation in conjunction with complex procedures and a large number of precious resources, spiritual veins, and spirit stones.

More importantly, the means of resurrection of Sixth Stage True Monarchs needed to be bound. Once it was bound to a certain person, it usually could no longer be transferred to others. This made transferring this type of resurrection to another person extremely difficult.

In short, there were many complications and requirements involved in the resurrection of a True Monarch. The cost to prepare a means of resurrection for them was millions of times greater than that of a Spiritual Emperor.

Knowing this, the Almighty Merchant had considered many ideas over countless years, and finally settled on launching a life insurance service.

“Keep it. As long as you have that, even if you encounter a Ninth Stage-level danger, you can still keep your life,” said Song Shuhang softly. After saying that, he carefully embraced Sixteen and lifted her up.

In addition to the ordinary lightning tribulation, the five-element tribulation, and other major tribulations, there were also the pill tribulation, item tribulation, heart demon tribulation, and some curse tribulations.

A curse-type attack is also a kind of tribulation.

If there’s a curse on my body, one that is from the ruler of the Netherworld at that, I wonder if I can cook it through Demon Emperor Hezhi’s Life Menu...

Curses should be quite similar to inner demons, just that they are a bit more neutral in nature. Senior White Two should not be disgusted with them, right?

In addition, I don’t know why, but I’ve always felt that curses are more of a good thing. After all, if I managed to extract the curse, it could be very useful... For example, I could use it to feed my ghost spirit.

The fat ball’s curses were ineffective on the Inner World.

Am I actually missing something important? And could this important thing be something that Senior White Two cares quite a bit about?

Again?

Was that not it?

Have I come across something along those lines recently?

What did I overlook??He always viewed himself as a relatively cautious person, especially when he was in a calm state, as he would prepare extensively before doing things or seeking death.

Under normal circumstances, an uncultivated gemstone fruit would be quite small, only about the size of a fingernail, and it would look like a miniature spirit stone. As long as one has enough spirit stones, even a First Stage cultivator should be able to use it. As long as there were enough spirit stones, even a First Stage cultivator could use it. The ability to enter a dreamland was Song Shuhang’s most powerful innate ability. Every time it triggered, the reasons behind it would be different; it was an especially willful ability.

Every time he entered a dreamland, Song Shuhang would gain some experience. Even during the time that he had had to live through many years as Lady Onion, he had at least gotten to hone his will, laying the foundation for his will to become as firm as steel.

In recent times, Song Shuhang had gotten in contact with a lot of big shots, items, and even the heavenly tribulation. The number of things that could allow him to enter a dreamland was not small. As such, he had already prepared himself for something like this happening.

Eh? It’s actually our Ancient Sage Speech.?Song Shuhang thought to himself.

Young Master Hai was his enemy, and if the enemy held resentment toward him, it should be a good thing.

Normally, I should be the one filled with resentment and looking to trouble him!

7:00 a.m. Tuesday. November 19, 2019.

Sixteen said, “No wonder.”

Behind him, Senior Turtle and Lady Onion also emerged from the Inner World.

Sixteen asked, “Are we heading to the scholarly faction today?”

“Mm-hm, I’ll make an appointment with Senior Eternal Fire in a bit.” Song Shuhang nodded and said, “By the way, have you seen the gemstone fruits in the Inner World? You should try some, they taste great. When you eat them, just remember to put the fruit pips aside. They can still be used.”

“The Inner World Assistant brought us a batch, and we all got to taste a few.” Lady Onion giggled. “After eating, I feel that my strength has improved a little.”

“It’s great that you enjoyed it. Sixteen, you can bring a few back with you and let Senior Seven have a taste as well,” Song Shuhang said.

At the same time, his consciousness swept across the floor as he prepared to contact Senior Eternal Fire.

Song Shuhang said curiously, “Eh? Senior White’s clone and Senior Eternal Fire aren’t here?”

Where did the two seniors go?

Lady Onion suggested, “Maybe they went out for breakfast?”

“I’ll call them and ask.” Sixteen took out her phone and called True Monarch Eternal Fire—she was not sure if Senior White’s clone had his phone on him, so she decided to contact True Monarch Eternal Fire instead.

The call quickly connected.

Su Clan’s Sixteen said, “Good morning, Senior Eternal Fire, where are you and Senior White?”

“Fellow Daoist White made a mistake, and sent us both to Mars,” True Monarch Eternal Fire replied in a helpless tone.

“There is still a signal on Mars? Is this a new version of the magic-modified phone?” Song Shuhang asked while leaning over to Sixteen’s phone.

True Monarch Eternal Fire replied, “No, we’re currently in Fellow Daoist White’s secret base on Mars. There’s only a signal in the specified part of the base. We should be returning to Earth at noon. Fellow Daoist White is just carrying out some experiments.”

Sixteen replied, “Okay, Senior. See you at noon, then.”

“Just what kind of mistake did Senior White make that caused him and True Monarch Eternal Fire to be sent to Mars?” Song Shuhang did not know whether to laugh or cry at the peculiar event.

Sixteen put away her phone. “What should we do until then?”

Song Shuhang pinched his chin. “Hm, let’s go and find Young Master Hai while we still have time.”

Senior Turtle asked, “Young Master Hai? Who’s that?”

Lady Onion explained, “He’s Song Shuhang’s mortal enemy, and he should be at the Fifth Stage Spiritual Emperor Realm.”

Senior Turtle rolled its eyes.

Song Shuhang said, “It’s the demonic cultivator who received Demon Emperor Hezhi’s inheritance. His strategic ability is amazing, but his luck is not very good.”

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “You’re really going to go and bully that demonic cultivator, eh?”

Song Shuhang responded, “I have a hunch that he’ll be giving me a surprise.”

Song Shuhang might just be able to get the inner demon tribulation he’d been looking for through Young Master Hai’s body.

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “Shuhang, do you know where Young Master Hai is?”

Song Shuhang said, “Hehe, I got to dream of his life yesterday when I was sleeping, so I got some information.”

Sixteen nodded, and said, “Then let’s go and find him. It’s seven o’clock now, we have to hurry up. Senior White and Senior Eternal Fire will probably be back by 11 or 12 o’clock.”

“I’ll pack some things before we leave.” Song Shuhang opened the storage box in the room, and then placed one gemstone fruit, a portion of stone milk from the Black Dragon World, and 10 Saber Intent Condensing Lotus Seeds inside.

“Huh? Why are you leaving these things inside the storage box? Why don’t you just let me eat them instead?” Lady Onion asked.

“These are reserved for Little Cai.” Song Shuhang flicked Lady Onion’s onion tip.

He then sent a text to Little Cai, telling her that he had left her a treasure in Medicine Master’s building, and that she should come over.

Little Cai had been secretly protecting his parents, keeping watch on them and seeing if there were any malicious fellow daoists who tried to approach them. So far, no abnormalities had occurred.

??????

When everything was prepared, Song Shuhang picked up the shrunken Senior Turtle, stuffed Lady Onion into his pocket, and left Medicine Master’s building with Sixteen.

As soon as he stepped out of the house, Song Shuhang saw a couple who looked like students not far from Medicine Master’s building; they seemed to be arguing.

The man said seriously, “Little Zi, you have to believe me. That other woman and I were just acting out a scene. The only person I love is you.”

Ptui, it was actually a love affair.

Also, which TV show was that line from??Song Shuhang almost thought the virtuous lamia had come out to snatch someone’s lines.

Sixteen suddenly said, “Hm... I beat this guy up before. He changed his hairstyle, and I almost didn’t recognize him.”

Song Shuhang smiled lightly, recalling his first meeting with Sixteen.

At this moment, the man happened to see Sixteen beside Song Shuhang, and his expression changed slightly. He then immediately said to his girlfriend in a serious tone, “I only have you in my heart. Believe me. I will never let you down. If there are other women in my heart, may the heavens strike me down with five bolts of lightning!”

“That guy is lying,” said the master of psychology, Senior Turtle.

Song Shuhang asked, “Then, should we cooperate with him?”

He rubbed his fingers lightly, and used the Lightning Drawing Technique of the Lightning Chapter of the Heavenly Master’s Righteous Techniques, and summoned a single lightning bolt.

Boom~

Lightning suddenly struck down from the skies.

Song Shuhang took this opportunity to hold Sixteen’s little hand, and walked away, not bothering to steal the limelight.

Su Clan’s Sixteen pursed her lips and chuckled. Then, she also pinched her fingers to cast a lightning technique.

Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom!

In the sky, four more deafening lightning strikes descended, fulfilling the five-bolt request that the guy had asked for.

When one decided to help another person, they should always try to do their best.

Since the guy asked for five lightning bolts, then, of course, they had to give him the right number.

After Sixteen’s adding four bolts to the one bolt that Song Shuhang had cast, Sixteen and Song Shuhang turned a corner and disappeared.

This only left the man standing on the spot with an absolutely dumbfounded face.?What just happened? The heavens striking down with lightning can’t be real, right?

“A coincidence! That has to be a coincidence!” The man tried to explain desperately.

The girl did not say anything. Instead, she just wiped her tears before standing on tiptoes to slap her boyfriend in the face and then running away.

??????

Meanwhile, Young Master Hai’s clone slowly floated up from the bottom of the sea.

He coordinated it such that the attire and magical treasures of this clone matched those of his main body. In addition, to make everything seem even more authentic, this clone also carried a certain amount of spirit stones and medicinal pills.

If the plan went well, all of these spirit stones, medicinal pills, and magical treasures would become Tyrannical Song’s loot. Either that, or they could be consumed in battle or just wiped out.

The price that he was paying this time was not small.

However, as long as this “Tyrannical Song Tribulation” could be dealt with, all of this would be well worth it.

Young Master Hai took this tribulation very seriously, treating it at the same level of importance as a heavenly tribulation.

Actually, in his opinion, this Tyrannical Song Tribulation was even more troublesome than a heavenly tribulation.

Young Master Hai said softly, “Now, time to figure out a way to draw Tyrannical Song’s attention.”

He knew Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s current location to be somewhere in the vicinity of Heavenly Field Island.

If his only objective was to attract Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s attention, then what he had to do was very simple... He needed to rush in front of Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, provoke him, and he could draw his ire in a few moments.

But with someone doing this, anyone who had a modicum of intelligence would feel that there was something off. If Young Master Hai made it too obvious, then he would not be able to transcend this tribulation.

He needed to make everything seem like a coincidence. He had to try and construct a scene where he had something to do in the vicinity, or show up and “accidentally” attract Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s attention.

At that time, it would be best if he let Profound Sage Tyrannical Song take the initiative to come to him.

The entire event had to seem as natural as possible.

Young Master Hai’s mind entered planning mode.

After a while, the outline of a plan took shape in his mind.

Young Master Hai murmured, “This is my first time constructing such a grand plan where I’m sending myself to die.”

On a cultivator’s path, there would always be setbacks.

The path of cultivation was very long, and temporary gains and losses were nothing. Whoever could step out onto their path and become an Immortal first was the one who would have the last laugh.

At present, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song was several realms ahead of him, but who could say that it would still be so in the future?

“After I succeed in feigning my death, I will be as free as a bird in the wide sky. When that time comes, it will be when I can enter a state of rapid growth.” Young Master Hai gently stroked the robes on his body, and returned to his confident and elegant self.

The corners of his mouth curled up into a charming smile.

“Anyway, I should head to Heavenly Field Island now.” He patted his body and circulated his spiritual energy; his wet body quickly became dry. Afterward, he brought out the Limitless Demon Sect’s standard flying sword, and turned it into a sword light.

Just as he was about to leave, his phone rang.

It was his personal phone, the one that only Demon Monarch Anzhi and Zheng Neng could contact.

Young Master Hai stopped flying and took out his phone.

The caller ID was Demon Monarch Anzhi’s number.

He knew that Demon Monarch Anzhi’s phone was currently in the hands of Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.

At first, he thought that the person who captured Demon Monarch Anzhi was an old enemy of theirs, but later, after probing the other party several times, he determined that Demon Monarch Anzhi had been captured by Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.

Young Master Hai secretly thought to himself,?If it’s Tyrannical Song, then it’s just as I intended.

This was the reason he had kept the phone all this time.

And so, he reached out and answered the call.

“Hello, Fellow Daoist Young Master Hai.” On the phone, it was surprisingly not Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s voice that sounded, but rather a woman’s cold voice.

He quickly recognized this voice to be the voice of Su Clan’s Sixteen, the junior of his close “friend,” Su Clan’s Seven.

Young Master Hai said slowly, “Hehehe, little Sixteen, I haven’t seen you for a few months. Listening to your voice, you seem to be in pretty good shape.”

He began to adjust his state, trying to take control of the conversation.

Though abrupt, Sixteen’s call perfectly fitted his script. With this, the script had already started unfolding, and what he needed to do now was to take control of the flow and make sure everything went as planned.

“How could I not be? After all, Fellow Daoist Young Master Hai, you’re still alive and well,” Su Clan’s Sixteen said slowly. “So anyway, shall we meet?”

“Hahaha, I’d rather not. I really don’t want to see Seven or you right now.” The corners of Young Master Hai’s mouth curled up into a smile.

It was perfect! Everything was going according to his plans.

Su Clan’s Sixteen suddenly said, “I’m afraid it’s not something you can decide.”

Young Master Hai frowned slightly.?What does she mean?

He got a bad feeling that the plot was going to go off-script.

Su Clan’s Sixteen said softly, “It’s already dawn. Why don’t you take a look up at the sky?”

In the next moment, Young Master Hai felt an ear-splitting sound come from above his head.

He immediately activated his sword light, and rode on his flying sword in a rush to escape.

Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom!

In the sky, several golden rays of light slammed down into the sea, causing large waves to form.

The golden rays of light were all powerful magical treasures, crashing down from the air to attack.

Vaguely, Young Master Hai could see that there were a saber, a sword, a spear, a crossbow, spikes, a fist, and even a horn among the rays of light.

Each of these magical treasures was at the Eighth Stage level, and exuded a terrifying pressure.

Young Master Hai looked up to the sky.

In the air, a golden chariot slowly emerged.

His “Tyrannical Song Tribulation” had his arms crossed as he stood on the chariot. Beside him was Su Clan’s Sixteen and a big turtle whose strength he could not see through.

“Long time no see, Young Master Hai,” Profound Sage Tyrannical Song said slowly. “As expected of my mortal enemy, you were able to evade my attack.”

“...” Young Master Hai.

He was really flattered. He did not expect to have such a high status in Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s mind. A Sage actually considered Young Master Hai his mortal enemy!

The progress of the script was much faster than he originally planned, and it had directly skipped to the finale.

Fortunately, the result had not changed. Although he had no idea how Profound Sage Tyrannical Song had found his location, as long as the plan did not derail, it would be fine.

In the air, Song Shuhang gave a mental order.

All of the magical treasures shone brightly as they returned to Shuhang’s side. They were mostly parts of the Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure, and the primordial treasure Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber was also in the mix to make up the numbers.

Unfortunately, Shuhang could not use the ?Divine Weapon Appraisal? that had been developed by Slow-Witted Song.

Otherwise, he could have retrieved his magical treasures using spatial means rather than having them return in such a low-class way like flying back.

Song Shuhang just imagined being able to retrieve the Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure and other weapons he shot out through Slow-Witted Song’s ?Divine Weapon Appraisal?, then sending them out again, and creating an endless cycle. It was simply a beautiful thought.

It was a pity that he did not have the spatial means to do so. And while the virtuous lamia could leave a mark on treasures, she could not recover them. Song Shuhang really felt that it was a great pity.

Meanwhile, below them.

Young Master Hai stood above the sea. He raised his head to look at Song Shuhang and Su Clan’s Sixteen—even if the script had suddenly skipped most of the plot and directly went to the finale, he would go through with it.

At the very least, he could not let Profound Sage Tyrannical Song see any flaws.

Therefore, he could not regard himself as a clone now. Instead, he had to treat this clone as his real body, and put an end to Young Master Hai’s life.

If it were his real body in this situation, what would he do if he encountered Profound Sage Tyrannical Song?

The first thing he would do... would definitely be trying to escape.

If he fought Profound Sage Tyrannical Song head-on, it was almost certain that the battle would end in his defeat in a mere 10 seconds. Regardless of whether he was fine with it or not, the other party could easily kill him if he really wanted to.

However, Young Master Hai had a variety of bizarre means of escape—no matter if they would prove useful against Profound Sage Tyrannical Song or not, he should at least use them first. Otherwise, if he let himself be hacked to death by Profound Sage Tyrannical Song without doing anything, it would arouse suspicion from the other party.

While Young Master Hai was in thought, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song said, “Although I really want to have a duel with you in an upright manner in order to break the karma between us, such a thing really isn’t suitable for the two of us now. As such, I’ll give you a choice.”

Young Master Hai asked, “What choice?”

While speaking, he was secretly casting an escape technique. In the shadows under the soles of his feet, his clone began to escape quietly, leaving only an empty shell in its place.

“For the karma that exists between you, me, and Su Clan’s Sixteen, Sixteen will represent me and her in severing that karma today,” Song Shuhang said. “As long as you can keep your life after fighting against Sixteen, I promise that I won’t trouble you for at least one year.”

“...” Young Master Hai.

Su Clan’s Sixteen is going to have a duel with me to sever the karma between us? But Su Clan’s Sixteen is only at the Fourth Stage Realm. What is Profound Sage Tyrannical Song thinking? What is he planning?

“In 20 seconds, the duel will begin,” Song Shuhang said. “It’s already late. Sixteen and I still have to go home for dinner at around 11 o’clock. So... Don’t run away. Fight like a man.”

After saying that, Song Shuhang’s left eye suddenly lit up.

He suddenly launched the Impregnating Gaze!

Pa!

This ray of light, also known as the Expert’s Appraisal Technique, passed directly through the shell that Young Master Hai left on the surface of the sea, and landed on his clone that was right below it.

A familiar light, familiar feeling, familiar pain.

The pain of pregnancy was simply something especially unbearable for men who never even had the function of becoming pregnant.

Young Master Hai’s clone gritted his teeth, endured the pain, and emerged from the bottom of the sea.

In the sky.

Song Shuhang looked at Su Clan’s Sixteen, and asked in a hushed voice, “Do you want me to weaken him more?”

Su Clan’s Sixteen said gently, “No, this is enough.”

The Impregnating Gaze had already weakened Young Master Hai’s combat power by at least 30%. Moreover, the longer it lasted, the stronger the weakening effect would be.

She gently took off her hat, and placed it on Song Shuhang’s head. Afterward, she raised her treasured saber and rode on it, prepared to descend.

Song Shuhang knew that Sixteen was protected by Sister White Dragon, but he still reached out and patted Sixteen lightly.

A saber intent fell on Sixteen’s body, and it remained on her body.

This saber intent actively cooperated with Sixteen’s saber qi, and transformed into a set of exquisite armor on her body.

Saber intent armor, besides being a mismatch in terms of style, could be said to be perfect in all other aspects. It would actively morph into the most suitable armor shape according to whoever or whatever it attached itself to.

Su Clan’s Sixteen pursed her lips and chuckled. She slid her feet and began her descent.

At the same time, there was the projection of a white dragon that condensed behind her... The white dragon’s little claws were holding a pair of chopsticks, and then the white dragon fed Sixteen a block of food that appeared to be filled with traces of lightning.

Below, when the pregnant Young Master Hai saw this small block of food, a strange feeling flooded his heart. He sensed the aura of the heavenly tribulation from the small cube. He had just transcended the Fifth Stage heavenly tribulation, so his impression of the heavenly tribulation was still particularly clear.

Eh, the Braised Heavenly Tribulation??Song Shuhang also saw this scene, and wondered when Sister White Dragon had hidden a batch of Braised Heavenly Tribulation.

After Su Clan’s Sixteen bit down on the small block of Braised Heavenly Tribulation, electric arcs crackled on her body.

The little dragon horns above her head began to draw the energy between the heaven and earth.

Boom!

Above Sixteen’s head, dense clouds appeared and claps of thunder sounded as violent lightning brewed. At the same time, a large wave suddenly broke out on the originally calm sea.

Summoning wind and calling rain, as well as overturning the rivers and seas, was a talent that had originally come from dragons.

And the sea was the home of dragons.

Fighting in such a location, Su Clan’s Sixteen’s combat power received a great boost.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

After a series of muffled thunder, a thick lightning bolt fell on Su Clan’s Sixteen, and merged into her saber and body, wrapping around her. At the same time, a faint strand of lightning with the aura of the heavenly tribulation escaped from her body, and merged with the lightning attached to her body.

At this moment, she was like a goddess of war who could manipulate thunder and lightning.

“Heavenly Saber Burying the Starry River!” When Sixteen made her move, it was the low-end version of Seven’s move.

A starry river of saber intent condensed, merged with lightning dragon saber qi, descended from the sky, and slashed Young Master Hai.

The formidable power of this saber move was no longer at the Fourth Stage Realm, even many ordinary Fifth Stage cultivators would not be able to send out such an overbearing and powerful attack.

Young Master Hai’s clone sighed. When he looked at the petite figure in the sky, he seemed to see the figure of Su Clan’s Seven. The members of the Spirit River Su Clan who had numbered daoist names were all masters of battle, and their combat prowess was outstanding... Every one of them more or less had a record of battles where they defeated those above them in cultivation.

From his observations, Su Clan’s Sixteen could definitely fight head-on against those Spiritual Emperors with two or three dragon patterns, and perhaps even defeat them.

However, I am different.

I am not like those ordinary two or three-dragon-patterned Spiritual Emperors.

Even if he was a pregnant clone, he would not be defeated by a saber attack of this level.

Young Master Hai endured the severe pain in his abdomen, and made a hand seal.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Five demonic god pillars emerged from behind him. These demonic god pillars were all projections that were directly condensed by spiritual energy.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

The front of the demonic god pillars went on to block the Heavenly Saber Burying the Starry River.

The corners of Young Master Hai’s mouth rose.

I’m not going to lose?that?easily.

At this moment... A dragon claw suddenly ignored the defense made of demonic god pillars, directly moving past them to grab Young Master Hai. Afterward, the dragon claw exerted a large amount of force, and threw him into the sky.

A female voice shouted, “Seismic Toss!”

“???” Young Master Hai.

What’s going on with this dragon claw?

What’s with this power?

When he was caught by the dragon claw, he could not resist at all. He felt like an ant that had been pinched by a human hand... Perhaps he was even worse than an ant.

It was such a plain toss, but he could not resist at all as he was thrown up into the air.

Is this dragon claw the reason why Profound Sage Tyrannical Song dared to let Su Clan’s Sixteen duel me on her own?

What is this dragon claw? Is it a materialization of virtue? The soul of a divine beast? Or a dragon possession?

“Step!” Young Master Hai, who was thrown into the sky, made a hand seal with one of his hands, and quickly cast a magical technique to free himself. Under his feet, a bridge made of demonic energy appeared.

Young Master Hai stepped on this bridge, and forcibly stabilized his body.

But just when he managed to stabilize his figure... Su Clan’s Sixteen suddenly appeared right in front of him.

So fast!

Her speed was so fast that his clone could not even react.

Immediately afterward, Su Clan’s Sixteen’s feet stepped on a layer of light, and she swung her petite fist right at him—she did not even use her saber. On both of her fists, electric arcs crackled, accompanied by a faint sound of a dragon’s roar.

Every one of her punches carried the trajectory of fate, rendering those it targeted clueless on how to even go about avoiding it.

This was an extremely esoteric fist technique... In terms of the fist technique’s level, it was probably even above Su Clan’s Seven’s Heavenly Saber Burying the Starry Sea.

Didn’t Su Clan’s Sixteen follow in the footsteps of Su Clan’s Seven in learning the saber? When did she master such a powerful fist technique? Why do I feel like the entire world has changed over the span of the short few months that I spent in seclusion?

Thud! Thud! Thud!

A series of drum-like sounds spread from their clash as Su Clan’s Sixteen sent fist after fist at Young Master Hai.

In the blink of an eye, Su Clan’s Sixteen and Young Master Hai clashed countless times.

In the next moment, the defensive magical techniques and magical treasures that were protecting Young Master Hai exploded. In addition, four fist prints were charred on the clothes on his abdomen.

Sixteen had sent out 16 punches over that short span of time.

12 punches had been enough to smash apart Young Master Hai’s defenses, and the last four punches hit him without reservation, striking his abdomen.

Young Master Hai’s face was pale, and his mouth was wide open in shock. A painful cry got stuck in his throat, but because he was in so much pain, he could not squeeze the cry out of his throat.

The pain he was experiencing now was even more intense than pregnancy and childbirth... After all, he had been hit right in his stomach while suffering the pain of pregnancy and childbirth.

Meanwhile, the saber intent armor on Su Clan’s Sixteen body had also slightly dimmed. When she had been quickly attacking Young Master Hai, Young Master Hai had managed to get in two counterattacks.

However, these two blows were completely blocked by Song Shuhang’s saber intent armor. While the saber intent armor seemed to have dimmed, it was actually just silently accumulating power for a counterattack.

Sixteen touched the saber intent armor lightly, turned around, then opened her small mouth, and roared at Young Master Hai, who was currently experiencing so much pain that he could not even utter a sound.

During a battle, one had to seize every moment. One could not give their enemy time to catch their breath.

Boom!

A cannon of light, which was filled with a mix of draconic energy and lightning that had traces of the heavenly tribulation’s aura, shot out a dazzling attack.

Young Master Hai, who was already in so much pain that he could not even stand upright and whose defenses were broken, could only use his body to endure the blow. As the attack hit him, he was sent flying and somersaulting in the air.

On the Divine Lobster’s chariot, the black-skinned Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “Beautifully done. Sixteen fought wonderfully.”

“What fist technique did Sixteen use?” Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

Senior Turtle replied, “Don’t even think about it. That’s the fist technique of the ancestral golden dragon. Without the blood of the dragon clan, no matter how well you copy the moves, you won’t be able to display the same defense-breaking effect and the dragon’s roar.”

Song Shuhang remarked, “That wasn’t what I was hinting at, I just thought that it was really cool.”

“This is definitely a common problem of the Chinese people. They instantly feel that any move that has a relationship with dragons becomes handsome, while any move that has a relationship with turtles becomes comparatively lowly,” Senior Turtle said. “This is a huge flaw in your psychology.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

At this time, the black-skinned Scarlet Heaven Sword slowly said, “You focused on the wrong thing. In the short confrontation just now, the most important thing to note was the four punches that Sixteen sent at Young Master Hai’s abdomen—this made it such that the Impregnating Gaze’s effect was maximized. Shuhang, this should be part of your considerations when you develop your combat style in the future. After casting the Impregnating Gaze on your enemy in the future, it would be an excellent choice to rush up and strike them where it hurts most.”

“That’s simply too inhuman,” Senior Turtle commented. “Such a battle is too brutal, and will completely ruin any accord.”

Song Shuhang said, “It’s the Expert’s Appraisal Technique.”

Just thinking about attacking someone’s abdomen after hitting them with the Impregnating Gaze felt terrifying.

On the other hand, to hit an enemy’s abdomen after hitting them with the Expert’s Appraisal Technique sounded a lot more normal. At that point, the other party’s abdomen would be the weakest part of their body, and it would indeed be good to take advantage of that.

??????

Meanwhile, Su Clan’s Sixteen stepped on a layer of light, and continued bullying Young Master Hai.

The saber light of the white dragon projection flickered repeatedly, while punches accompanied by a dragon’s roar were repeatedly thrown.

Su Clan’s Sixteen’s fingers appeared as sharp as a dragon’s teeth. The little dragon horns on her head constantly drew the energy between the heaven and earth.

Whenever Young Master Hai tried to break free, a white dragon claw would appear and grab him before bringing him back into the fight.

Sometimes, when Young Master Hai seized an opportunity to fight back, a dragon’s tail would suddenly appear and knock him down.

Young Master Hai had a look of utter desperation on his face.

Although this clone was intended to die according to the script he had in mind, being defeated and beaten in such a way by Su Clan’s Sixteen without having any chance to resist still caused Young Master Hai to feel very aggrieved.

While the conclusion of the script was fine, the process felt very uncomfortable.

This clone of his even substituted the data of his main body into himself, and after simulating the event in his mind, he discovered that even if it were his main body that was here at this moment, the outcome would probably not be much different.

The white dragon behind Su Clan’s Sixteen was simply an incomprehensible existence.

At least for Young Master Hai who was at the Fifth Stage Realm, there was absolutely no way to deal with this white dragon.

That was unless he could draw the power of Demon Emperor Hezhi, and use it to fight against this white dragon.

In that case, it would be king against king, general against general, and he would be able to fight a proper one-on-one duel against Su Clan’s Sixteen and have a chance of winning.

Just as this idea just surfaced in Young Master Hai’s clone’s mind, demonic qi suddenly churned in his body.

This clone was made by Young Master Hai through a method he learned in Demon Emperor Hezhi’s inheritance. He made use of the shell of his old body and a portion of his soul impurities, along with a demonic god pillar refinement technique, to create this clone.

Is it the power of Demon Emperor Hezhi??Young Master Hai’s clone frowned, and fell into thought.

Sure enough, there were always some backdoors within the methods in the Demon Emperor’s inheritance.

The power of the Demon Emperor came just in time.

Young Master Hai smiled lightly.

He took the initiative to let go of the clone’s imprisonment, allowing the demonic qi to do whatever it wanted. He even relaxed the consciousness of his own clone in order to allow the power of the Demon Emperor to dominate his body even faster.

He allowed the final scenes of Young Master Hai’s death to be left in the hands of the Demon Emperor’s power.

With the active cooperation of Young Master Hai’s clone, the violent demonic energy that surged in his body soon began to “take over” his body. As the demonic energy surged, violent emotions emerged in Young Master Hai’s clone.

At the same time, Young Master Hai took the initiative to withdraw his consciousness to the depths of his soul to act just like an audience, enjoying the end of this ❮Young Master Hai’s Death❯ drama.

“Aaah~” Young Master Hai let out a bestial cry. The demonic energy in his body spiked, and began emerging from every pore on his body, forming demonic black mist around him.

This demonic mist made Young Master Hai’s clone feel a “warm” feeling, just like a fish returning to the sea and being enveloped in warm seawater.

Su Clan’s Sixteen slashed three slashes in a row, but when her attacks reached the demonic mist, they disappeared.

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “Rampage?”

Sister White Dragon responded, “He should be using a berserk skill. This is the main field of expertise of the demonic forces.”

If a demonic cultivator did not have several berserk skills, then they would probably be too ashamed to talk to other people.

After saying her piece, Sister White Dragon swung her claw Young Master Hai again.

Bam~

The demonic mist covering Young Master Hai’s body was smashed away immediately, revealing Young Master Hai’s body, which was covered with bulging blue veins. Immediately afterward, Young Master Hai’s body was sent into the sea.

As Young Master Hai fell into the sea, huge waves surged once more as a result.

Senior Turtle commented, “The splash was too big when entering the water, minus one point.”

Under the sea’s surface.

While Young Master Hai’s body struggled, a large swath of demonic mist reappeared around his body. At the same time, violent emotions surged within him again.

Strange, is this really it? Young Master Hai’s consciousness deep in his mind wondered.

If this really was the back door left by the Demon Emperor in his cultivation technique... then shouldn’t the Demon Emperor’s power have gone a step further at this time, and directly projected a strand of his consciousness into this body?

Could it be that this was not a back door of the Demon Emperor, but rather a berserk seed opportunity especially left by the Demon Emperor for his inheritor?

Or... Could the Demon Emperor’s main body have met with an accident, and so was unable to use this back door?

Just as Young Master Hai was puzzled, the demonic mist around him condensed a projection of a demonic god pillar.

[My inheritor, do you want power?] This projection of the demonic god pillar conveyed a thought to Young Master Hai.

Young Master Hai’s consciousness replied, “Yes, lend me your power, great emperor.”

[Then, are you prepared to pay the price?] The projection of the demonic god pillar once again conveyed his thoughts.

Young Master Hai thought for a while, and then replied, “Yes.”

This clone had been originally meant to face this tribulation for him anyway, so there was nothing that could not be given up when it came to this clone.

[Accept my power and experience the might of the Demon Emperor.] After conveying this thought, the demonic god pillar projection directly integrated with Young Master Hai’s clone.

In the sky.

Su Clan’s Sixteen stood on the tips of her toes on a layer of light as she looked at the calm sea below her. “He still hasn’t come out.”

“Don’t worry, he can’t escape.” Sister White Dragon had locked on to Young Master Hai, preventing him from escaping. “It looks like his berserk seed is about to completely develop. After it does, the real battle begins.”

“That’s exactly what I want,” said Su Clan’s Sixteen. What she currently needed was a suitable opponent to stimulate her and allow her to raise her realm.

Boom!

A huge explosion appeared on the sea, and an inflated version of Young Master Hai emerged.

His figure had swelled in size, and blue veins covered his entire body. His style had completely changed from a handsome man to a muscular man. Moreover, his originally already swollen abdomen now even seemed to be leaking.

This inflated version of Young Master Hai let out a strange laugh, and said, “Let’s see. Who’s my opponent?”

His eyes swept over to Su Clan’s Sixteen, and then over to Song Shuhang who was standing on the Divine Lobster’s chariot.

As soon as the inflated version of Young Master Hai set his eyes on Song Shuhang, he froze, his body stiffened for a moment, and even the demonic mist that was flowing around him stopped.

“???” Young Master Hai’s consciousness.

“Tyrannical... Song!!!” The inflated version of Young Master Hai let out a hoarse cry.

There was endless resentment in his voice.

If every bit of resentment in his voice was transformed into a brick, then the resentment he held was enough to create a second Great Wall of China.

Song Shuhang looked at Young Master Hai, and for some reason suddenly remembered when Senior White Two had blurted out “Egg thing?”.

The inflated version of Young Master Hai took a deep breath, and his body slightly bent over. “One day, I will unscrew your head with my own hands.”

“Oh,” Song Shuhang replied calmly.

The inflated version of Young Master Hai said savagely, “I’m going to hang your head on my demonic god pillar and insert it in the most conspicuous place in my Demon Empire.”

“Eh, this tone... You’re not Young Master Hai, are you?” Then, Song Shuhang’s eyes suddenly lit up. “Demon Emperor Hazie?”

He stretched out his hand, and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword leaped into his hands. At the same time, the virtuous lamia emerged and wrapped herself around his body, while Fairy Creation also emerged, and began to play the pipa.

The 49 Holy Apes also emerged one after the other behind Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang exclaimed, “There’s no need to wait for ‘one day,’ how about I take you and hang you in my Inner World.”

Senior Turtle remarked, “Pay attention to what you say. You should be gentler. Don’t yell at others like some villain.”

“You’re already here, so there’s no need to move about. How about you just let someone behead you? That will be a lot more convenient.” Song Shuhang corrected himself when he realized his mistake.

“...” Senior Turtle.

The inflated version of Young Master Hai used all his strength, and shouted, “The next time I see you will be the time you die!”

After roaring out loud, Young Master Hai’s body shrank like a leak...

The demonic energy in his body dissipated, the violent thoughts dissipated, and even the small strand of Demon Emperor Hezhi’s will dissipated.

Young Master Hai stood blankly in the air, dumbfounded.

The demonic mist was still around him.

But at this time, the patch of demonic mist no longer brought him the same warm feeling as it did a while ago...

This patch of demonic mist that used to be warm was now as cold as ice.

It was only November, but Young Master Hai felt as if the harsh winter had come early.

In his mind, he recalled a scene.

That day, in the Demon Emperor’s inheritance space. The young-looking Profound Sage Tyrannical Song stood suspended in the air of the inheritance space, and said calmly, “Demon Emperor Hezhi is very powerful and terrifying. It was only with the combination of the right timing, the right setting, and the right people that we were able to tear him apart.

Tear him apart...

Apart...

Demon Emperor Hezhi had been torn apart...

At that time, he thought that it was only an illusion, a trial of the inheritance secret realm, a test of his inner tenacity.

But now it seemed that it was not a trial at all, but rather a nightmare called Tyrannical Song Tribulation.

Demon Emperor Hezhi had really been torn apart and defeated by him.

Otherwise, when the Demon Emperor’s consciousness possessed his clone’s body, it would not have carried such heavy resentment and retreated right after cursing at the other party.

Within Young Master Hai’s heart, an unprecedentedly large shadow cast down upon him.

His goal in life was to become the second Demon Emperor Hezhi. Even if he did not have the aptitude to defy the heavens like some of those people with nine dragon patterns, he still wanted to rely on his own efforts to step out onto a path of immortality and become the Demon Emperor.

However, just as he was beginning to make progress on the path he had decided upon, his dreams were shattered.

No, I should stop thinking in such a way.?Young Master Hai quickly stopped his thoughts.

If he were to continue with that line of thinking... He was afraid that inner demons really would appear in his heart.

After this incident was over, he had to take a break for a while and stabilize his mental state.

Young Master Hai silently thought to himself,?Even though Demon Emperor Hezhi is my goal, he is also someone I want to surpass. The future I want is not limited to what has been achieved by a Demon Emperor. My aspirations are much greater.

Moreover, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song had not relied on his own strength to defeat Demon Emperor Hezhi. He had done so by relying on various factors.

From the fact that Demon Emperor Hezhi was clamoring to take revenge, it could be seen that Demon Emperor Hezhi was not afraid of Profound Sage Tyrannical Song. It was very likely that he had been taken advantage of, or Profound Sage Tyrannical Song borrowed the power of other big shots.

Young Master Hai was quickly able to calm himself down.

A person like him would not easily be beaten or knocked down. Even in a desperate situation, he would survive tenaciously as long as he was still breathing, and make a comeback one day.

“Alas, Demon Emperor Hezhi ran away,” said Song Shuhang. Afterward, he returned to the Divine Lobster’s Chariot.

But it’s fine that he ran away. To be honest, if I really were to fight a Young Master Hai possessed by Demon Emperor Hezhi, I’m not certain what the outcome would be.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword had left, and Song Shuhang was currently only left with the black Scarlet Heaven Sword. And the black Scarlet Heaven Sword had no way of cooperating with Song Shuhang to slash out the Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique. Compared with back when he was in the Black Dragon World, Song Shuhang was lacking a lot of his trump cards.

He looked at the black Scarlet Heaven Sword that was in his hands, and then suddenly gestured.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, “What?”

Song Shuhang said, “I was just thinking, should I learn the sword-swallowing skill? I always felt that when Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword’s main body was still with me back then, while it would express its resistance to the action with its words, it never really resisted the virtuous lamia’s sword-swallowing performance.
