Senior, do you actually enjoy the process of being swallowed?”

The virtuous lamia tilted her head and blinked.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword warned, “If you dare to perform sword swallowing with me, I will fight you. I will definitely pierce your guts!”

Senior Turtle remarked, “It is an inner demon, after all. Some of its hobbies are probably the opposite of its main body.”

“That makes sense,” said Song Shuhang. After saying that, he moved his hand and used the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? on the black Scarlet Heaven Sword.

“Aaaah~ How refreshing.” The black Scarlet Heaven Sword felt extremely comfortable.

Song Shuhang remarked, “But there also seems to be some things that are still the same.”

“...” Senior Turtle.

Sister White Dragon said, “It looks like Young Master Hai doesn’t have much strength left.”

The berserk effect that he had gone through just now had consumed much of Young Master Hai’s power.

And Demon Emperor Hezhi’s will had even retreated when it had been in the middle of possessing his body. At this time, Young Master Hai’s power was nearly depleted.

Su Clan’s Sixteen said, “This will be the last move.”

She looked at Young Master Hai’s clone, and said, “If you manage to survive after this move, then you can live. If you are unable to endure it, then you die.”

Young Master Hai raised his head and looked at Su Clan’s Sixteen.

Sixteen stood on one foot on a layer of light, having already assumed a graceful punching posture...

Her words showed that her strongest move at the moment was not a saber technique, but rather a fist technique.

“Phew~” Sixteen slowly exhaled. Around her neck, several dragon scales made of spiritual energy emerged. The dragon scales looked like they were made of crystals, which made them look very valuable.

Behind Sixteen, a series of visual phenomena emerged.

Violent lightning enveloped her body, a true dragon wrapped around her arm, and a formation composed of ancient runes appeared on the soles of her feet.

A “starry river” composed of countless stars appeared behind her elbow. This projection of a starry river stretched out for nearly a kilometer.

In the starry river, there were hundreds of true dragons swimming amongst the stars.

The river surged forward. The force that came with the flow of the water and the hundreds of dragons all acted upon Sixteen’s elbow, pushing her arm forward.

Gulp.

Song Shuhang swallowed.

The special effects of this punch looked absolutely brutal. It really made one feel that regardless of who would be hit by this punch, they were bound to die.

“Heh, I didn’t expect Sixteen to have been able to learn this punch as well,” Senior Turtle said. “The ancestral golden dragon used this move to knock Slow-Witted Song from the eastern end of the Ancient Heavenly City to its western end in one hit. It caused him to shed a tear the size of a bean. It was truly spectacular.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

Another dark part of Slow-Witted Song’s history when he got beaten and cried?

Boom!

Sixteen threw the punch with everything she had.

When she swung her fist, the environment changed—heavy rain poured down from the sky, and the waves roared and crashed, setting off even larger waves.

Young Master Hai did not avoid the attack.

It’s time to end this,?he thought.

There was no need to move about anymore. There really was not much power left in his body. In this way, even if he died, he would be able to put a proper close to the play.

And so, the fist hit him.

As soon as it touched him, Young Master Hai felt like his bones were being crushed.

His body was sent flying, but then the terrifying punch passed through his body, blasting out a huge vortex in the sea.

Young Master Hai’s body was like a skipping stone, bouncing on the sea surface up and down repeatedly.

In the end, his body stopped skipping on the water, and he lay floating on the sea, motionless.

I actually didn’t die?

What a tragedy.

He would rather die immediately to end the play where his clone was meant to die anyway.

Young Master Hai recalled Sixteen’s punch just now. At the last moment, her punch passed through his body and slammed into the sea. This was obviously not an operational error, but an intentional one.

Damn, does Tyrannical Song want to capture me alive?

Not good.?Young Master Hai frowned.

If he was captured alive by Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, then the other party might be able to discover that he was a clone.

While he was in thought, he saw two figures descend right by him.

It was Sixteen, as well as Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, whom he least wanted to see.

Song Shuhang reached out, took off the hat on his head, and put it back on Sixteen’s head. “You’ve worked hard, Sixteen.”

Sixteen said regretfully, “Mm-hm, it’s a pity that this battle was not that enjoyable.”

“There will be a chance for you to enjoy yourself in the future.” Song Shuhang smiled slightly, and squatted beside Young Master Hai. “Don’t you think so? My mortal enemy, Fellow Daoist Young Master Hai.”

Young Master Hai closed his eyes and pretended to be dead, trying to figure out a solution in his mind.

Song Shuhang said, “Next time, you should let Sixteen have a proper battle with your main body.”

“!!!” Young Master Hai suddenly opened his eyes.

Song Shuhang continued, “This clone of yours is very realistic. If I had not known your plan from the very beginning, perhaps I would have been deceived by you.”

Young Master Hai asked, “You... knew my plan?”

How is that possible? I’m the only one who knows of my plan! I did not tell anyone!

“Indeed. I knew it from the very beginning,” Song Shuhang said. “I’ll tell you a little secret. I know of everything that you’ve done, experienced, and felt in the past month.”

Young Master Hai only felt an unspeakable feeling in his heart as madness surged within him.

It was an inner demon.

An inner demon had been born within his heart.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “I can smell an inner demon.”

Both of them were inner demons, so when an inner demon was born in Young Master Hai’s clone, it had immediately been able to sense it.

When he heard this, Song Shuhang suddenly put on a serious face, clasped his palms together, and began to silently recite words from his mouth.

Senior Turtle asked curiously, “What are you reciting?”

“I’m praying to Senior White,” said Song Shuhang. During this trip, not only did he manage to find Young Master Hai’s clone, but he also got himself an inner demon out of it!

“...” Senior Turtle.

Song Shuhang asked, “Speaking of which, how do I extract the inner demon from his clone? There isn’t a method on how to extract inner demons inside the ?Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet?...”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said “As a saber... Ack, as a sword, I don’t have much knowledge of things that are not related to fighting.”

Elder Sister White Dragon added, “So far, the only method I know that can forcibly extract an inner demon from a person is Soft Feather’s inner demon clone technique.”

Ever since the ancient era, inner demons had always been one of the most troublesome things for cultivators. How to extract inner demons from a cultivator was a difficult problem to tackle.

“You should capture him for now, and ask a big shot later,” Senior Turtle said. “I’ll contact the Great Northern Emperor, and see if he has any input on this.”

Lady Onion reminded Shuhang, “You can also ask Pavilion Master Chu. She has done quite a bit of research on inner demons.”

“I almost forgot about Pavilion Master Chu.” Song Shuhang gently patted Lady Onion’s green onion sprouts.

When Pavilion Master Chu was at the Sixth Stage, she had gotten herself entangled with an unkillable inner demon. That inner demon stuck with her throughout her whole life, all the way to the Ninth Stage Realm. Moreover, this inner demon later stepped out onto its own path of immortality, and became Pavilion Master Chu Two.

Song Shuhang looked at the weakened close of Young Master Hai, and said, “I’ll send him to Pavilion Master Chu and see if she knows of any way to deal with the inner demon.”

Young Master Hai’s clone slowly closed his eyes, not daring to look at Song Shuhang. In the entire universe, except for real peerless powerhouses, nobody truly dared to look directly into Tyrannical Song’s eyes.

Song Shuhang looked down at Young Master Hai, and said after some pondering, “Young Master Hai, you’ve suddenly become so weak. This really makes me feel quite unsettled.”

“...” Young Master Hai.

As he faced the Young Master Hai, Song Shuhang clearly felt how quickly his strength and realm had been progressing.

He usually hung around the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, who were his seniors. As such, Song Shuhang had always considered himself their junior, and this had not changed even as his strength increased.

But as he looked at Young Master Hai now, the difference in strength between them was truly big.

He could still remember how powerless he had been when he had been resisting the joint forces of Young Master Hai and Demon Monarch Anzhi not too long ago, but now he felt as if Young Master Hai was too weak.

He had always regarded Young Master Hai as someone akin to the final boss of a dungeon. This was how deep of an impression Young Master Hai left on him half a year ago.

“Senior Tyrannical Song, are you having fun?” Young Master Hai’s clone said in a hoarse voice. “You’re a dignified Eighth Stage Profound Sage, yet you’re saying that I’ve suddenly become weak. Surely, you must be joking.”

Song Shuhang paused, and then smiled slightly. “Not at all. It feels quite boring.”

He did not bother explaining to Young Master Hai that he was a fake Profound Sage, or that he was at the Sixth Stage Realm, and was only a small cultivator at the Foundation Establishment Realm half a year ago.

There was no need to explain, as there was no point to it.

“...” Young Master Hai.

Song Shuhang said, “My obsession with you has come to an end.”

Senior Turtle asked, “Are you not going to kill him and sever the karma between you two?”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword also asked, “Aren’t you going to end this and put everything behind you?”

“If I do end up running into his main body, it won’t be too late to kill him at that point. This is a problem between him and Sixteen and me.” Song Shuhang reached out and sent Young Master’s clone into his Inner World.

The only difference from before was that the obsession he had toward Young Master Hai was gone.

“Mm-hm.” Sixteen nodded.

Song Shuhang took out his phone and checked the time. “It’s almost time. We should head back now. Senior Turtle, we’ll have to trouble you again.”

Although Senior Turtle’s strength had been sealed, it could still perform short-distance spatial teleportation.

Previously, it was the one who had brought Song Shuhang and his whole party from the Jiangnan area to this stretch of sea.

Senior Turtle said suddenly, “By the way, you hit me twice in the face before and did me dirty once. My heart is in pain.”

“???” Song Shuhang.

When did I do such a thing?

“I’m not happy.” The Senior Turtle stood up, and began to dance out of nowhere.

Lady Onion quivered on its turtle shell.

Song Shuhang blurted out, “Uh... sorry?”

He had always been a man who recognized his mistakes and corrected them, unless it was something outside of his control.

Senior Turtle said, “That’s so insincere. And if apologies were useful, what would be the point of having the police?”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword interjected, “Fellow Daoist Turtle, that line is too old-fashioned. It isn’t even popular anymore.”

Senior Turtle said, “Scarlet Heaven Sword, please don’t rend my heart any further. My heart is very fragile today, maybe my period has come.”

Song Shuhang was surprised. “Senior Turtle, are you a female turtle?”

“Can’t a male turtle also have a period?” Senior Turtle rolled his eyes. “Your Expert’s Appraisal can even make men pregnant!”

Elder Sister White Dragon interjected, “If it’s a male turtle, maybe it’s not a period, but rather bleeding hemorrhoids.”

Senior Turtle sighed. “How stifling...”

Song Shuhang smiled, and said, “Alright, there’s no need to talk in such a roundabout manner. Senior Turtle, is there something you want?”

Senior Turtle said, “I want to set up an amusement park in your Inner World... Some time ago, when I was watching TV, I saw a roller coaster where people would go upside down and scream. It looked really exciting.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

“We can set up the upside-down roller coaster a bit higher so that it doesn’t interfere with other things. You buy the materials, and I’ll build the amusement park and ensure that it’s exciting. In addition, we can also make various other fun rides,” Senior Turtle continued.

The Inner World was ultimately Song Shuhang’s domain, and Senior Turtle was merely a guest. If it wanted to make something, it needed to get Song Shuhang’s consent first.

Senior Turtle then added, “In addition, if this amusement park is well made, in the future, we could charge fees to those who go on the rides and earn spirit stones!”

“Sounds good,” Song Shuhang quickly agreed. “Since Senior Turtle is interested in making an amusement park, I’ll talk to the Inner World Assistant and let her allot a suitable plot of land for you.”

“Then it’s settled.” Senior Turtle happily opened a spatial gate. “Let’s get moving. By the way, what are we having for lunch today?”

“Boiled turtle soup,” Song Shuhang said. “But since we haven’t bought any soft-shelled turtles yet, we can just use sea turtles instead.”

“Kid, you’re courting death!” Senior Turtle growled.

“Actually, the sea turtle soup does not taste that good. Let’s make soup using other seafood,” said Lady Onion—she and Senior Turtle were good friends, so she spoke up for it.

Using other seafood?

Hearing this, the gazes of all those present shifted to Elder Sister White Dragon.

“Haha.” Elder Sister White Dragon smiled gently. “White Dragon Soup is actually not bad.”

Elder Sister White Dragon did not look angry. It seemed like she was in a good mood.

If Shuhang had not heard that the ancestral golden dragon had once punched Slow-Witted Song from the eastern end of the Ancient Heavenly City to its western end, he might have really taken the opportunity to make a remark.

But now, his strong desire to survive told him that doing so might just really bring about his death. Not everyone could simply shed tears as large as beans!

Song Shuhang shook his head desperately as he thought to himself,I don’t dare poke that beehive.

Moreover, with how powerful Elder Sister White Dragon was, who could even make her into soup? Perhaps he could get a pot of Elder Sister White Dragon’s bathwater, but that was the limit.

??????

After going through the spatial gate that Senior Turtle opened, Song Shuhang and the others returned to Medicine Master’s building in Jiangnan University Town.

All of them safely descended to the ground.

Song Shuhang said, “Speaking of spirit stones, I suddenly remembered something.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked curiously, “What? Do you need spirit stones?”

“No... I remembered that after treating the batches of patients that Fairy Blue Phoenix sent over, I didn’t charge them any of it.” Song Shuhang pressed his right hand to his chest, grief-stricken.

Yesterday, he had gone to Fairy Blue Phoenix to receive some guidance on the ?Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique?. At the end, when his Inner World was full, the two of them bid goodbye to one another.

At that time, he had forgotten to collect his fee in spirit stones.

Sixteen laughed, and said, “Well, you didn’t say that you were going to be collecting spirit stones for a fee in the first place.”

Song Shuhang replied, “Yeah, that’s why I feel that I’ve lost big time.”

Now, he did not have even a half of a spirit stone on hand. This was especially problematic with the constant improvement of his strength and realm as he now had numerous places where he needed to use spirit stones.

Firstly and most fundamentally, when a normal cultivator practiced, they usually could not do without spirit stones.

When normal cultivators bought items in the world of cultivation, they also needed spirit stones.

The Time City in his Inner World was in an inactive state. In order to reactivate it, he needed to provide it with an astronomical amount of spirit stones. The only exception was if he could acquire a high-power core for it like he did for the puppet maiden.

There was also the Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure. If he were to lift its seals all the way to the Eighth Stage, it would begin consuming astronomical amounts of spirit stones.

Besides those, he also had the God Slaying Mother-Child Cannon. If he had enough spirit stones, the shots of the cannon could even reach the level of an Eighth Stage attack.

In addition... He was also planning to build a set of training equipment in the Inner World, such as a gravity chamber, a pain tolerance trial, a death trial, a 12-step trial, and so on. All of this equipment that would help with his and his disciples’ cultivation required money, which, in the world of cultivation, was spirit stones.

And, once again, this was exactly what he was lacking at the moment.

Song Shuhang sighed and said, “If I once again receive a request from the Beast Realm to cure the patients stricken with the Netherworld’s Evil Energy Infection, make sure to remind me to charge them.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen replied, “Okay.”

None of the others responded to Song Shuhang.

“Sixteen is still the best,” said Song Shuhang.

Lady Onion blinked and changed the subject. “Senior White and Senior Eternal Fire haven’t returned yet.”

Song Shuhang said, “How about I go to the vegetable market to buy some ingredients first? After that, I can show all of you my new skills.”

He now possessed Demon Emperor Hezhi’s demonic chef heart, which gave him experiences and records on cooking and making demonic dishes. Logically speaking, he should be able to make pretty good home-cooked dishes now.

Ding, dong~

While he was speaking, the doorbell of Medicine Master’s building began ringing.

The aura of three strange cultivators appeared at the door, and they remained standing outside quietly.

Song Shuhang looked out the window.

At the door were two women and one man. They were all young and dressed in modern clothes. It was impossible to tell which cultivation system or force they belonged to.

Song Shuhang asked, “I don’t know them. Sixteen, do you know them?”

Sixteen shook her head.

“Are they here to cause trouble?” Song Shuhang asked—he had been attacked a lot by big shots recently, so he felt a little nervous.

Lady Onion guessed, “They probably came to see Senior Medicine Master.”

Song Shuhang said, “I’ll go down and have a look.”

He then opened the window and jumped out...

As he was halfway through his jump, he stopped abruptly and jumped back up again.

Senior Turtle asked, “Why did you jump back up?”

“Jumping out of the window is a disease that needs to be cured,” said Song Shuhang. After saying that, he opened the door and went down the stairs.

“...” Senior Turtle.

Isn’t jumping out and then jumping back up while mid-air even a worse disease?

Su Clan’s Sixteen leaned against the window, and took a look at the area below.

Elder Sister White Dragon, Senior Turtle, and Lady Onion all huddled against the windows and looked down as well.

Song Shuhang ran to the door and opened it.

“S-Senior Tyrannical Song.”

“S-Senior Tyrannical Scholar.”

“S-Senior Tyrannical Dragon.”

There were three different voices that sounded, and three different names that were called out. The only thing that was the same was that the three young fellow daoists all trembled like little quails. They all lowered their heads, not daring to look at Song Shuhang directly.

“...” Song Shuhang.

Am I really that scary? When I first started cultivating, the seniors in the Nine Provinces Number One Group said that I had a kind-looking face.

“Fellow Daoists, you don’t need to be so nervous. Why have you come here?” Song Shuhang tried his best to keep his voice as gentle as he could make it.

“This junior is from the Drifting Starlight Sect, Xi.”

“Fairy Naiqi.”

“Ding Gan.”

“We greet Senior Tyrannical Song.” The three young fellow daoists bowed respectfully to Song Shuhang again. Their emotions were a mix of fear and joy.

They were afraid because the person before them was Senior Tyrannical Song, but the reason for their joy was the exact same—this was Senior Tyrannical Song, the first Sage in 1,000 years!

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “You guys came for me?”

“Yes, Senior Tyrannical Song.” The young man who looked the youngest out of the three stared at Song Shuhang with a look of reverence.

Fairy Naiqi said, “We were ordered by our master to escort our junior brother to the Jiangnan area for his tribulation-transcension. Therefore, we came to greet Senior Tyrannical Song.”

Naiqi and the girl named Xi were both in the Fourth Stage Realm.

As for the young man named Ding Gan, he was at the peak of the Second Stage Realm, about to reach the Third Stage Realm.

“I see.” Song Shuhang smiled slightly.

After his name as Profound Sage Tyrannical Song became known across the universe, some well-informed cultivators and forces already knew that he often appeared in the area around Jiangnan University Town.

The news that the Jiangnan area was Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s domain had already spread among a small circle of cultivators.

Therefore, if a disciple of any force wanted to transcend their tribulation in the Jiangnan area, they first had to go and pay a visit to Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.

Song Shuhang smiled, and said, “Have you already found a good place to transcend the tribulation?”

Xi replied softly, “Yes, we have already prepared a location.”

“Alright, I wish little fellow daoist a successful tribulation.” Song Shuhang patted the young man as he spoke.

What a coincidence, a Third Stage heavenly tribulation... Should I go with them and collect the Third Stage tribulation lightning and use it to make a dish?

“Thank you, Senior Tyrannical Song.” Ding Gan was very happy to receive Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s well wishes. Finally, he brought out a small box, and said, “This is a small gift that my master asked me to bring to Senior Tyrannical Song. I ask Senior Tyrannical Song to accept it.”

Song Shuhang wanted to refuse, but as Ding Gan handed over the small box to him, he could smell the fragrance of spirit stones inside the box.

[This young man has an inner demon.] From behind his waist, the black Scarlet Heaven Sword sent him a voice transmission.

[It seems that this little fellow daoist and I have some fate.] When he heard the reminder from the black Scarlet Heaven Sword, Song Shuhang immediately had such a thought in his mind.

The Third Stage tribulation lightning and the inner demon tribulation were both great things.

It was just that they were rather troublesome to acquire.

For the tribulation lightning, he needed Senior White to come and seal it for him. Currently, Song Shuhang could only knead the lightning, and he did not have the ability to seal it. He was still in the middle of learning how to seal it from Senior White.

As for the inner demon tribulation, so far, there was no method in the universe—or at least one that he knew of—to forcefully extract an inner demon from another person.

“When is little fellow daoist Ding Gan going to transcend the tribulation?” Song Shuhang asked with a smile.

Profound Sage Tyrannical Song actually cared about the date of his tribulation! Ding Gan felt slightly flattered, and replied, “Reporting to Senior Tyrannical Song, junior is going to transcend his tribulation on November 22.”

Song Shuhang said, “Mm-hm, a good day.”

Ding Gan said happily, “This junior thinks so as well.”

After saying that, he put the gift in both hands and looked at Song Shuhang, hoping that Profound Sage Tyrannical Song would accept their gift.

Song Shuhang smiled slightly. He reached out and tapped on the gift box lightly, sending it into the Inner World.

S-spatial means? Or was it a spatial magical treasure??This was the first time that Ding Gan had seen spatial abilities. He had only heard of such abilities from the words and stories of his senior brothers and sisters in the sect.

“Senior Tyrannical Song, we three juniors will be taking our leave now.” Fairy Naiqi bid goodbye to Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang said, “Three little friends, please wait a moment.”

Hearing this, the three little cultivators stopped and looked at Senior Tyrannical Song in confusion.

Song Shuhang said, “Just wait a moment, I’ve got to ask my senior about something.”

He decided to bring the three little fellow daoists into the yard and let them wait there for a while.

Afterward, his consciousness sneaked into the Inner World and went to the Living Spring.

There, Young Master Hai’s clone lay weakly by the pool, with a seal on each of his limbs, completely immobilized.

In fact, even if there were no seals on his limbs, Young Master Hai’s clone would not dare to move—the fairy in the spring was simply too terrifying. While staying next to this fairy, he felt that it was difficult for him to even breathe. He sensed that the fairy in the spring was a terrifying existence in a realm similar to Demon Emperor Hezhi.

Pavilion Master Chu’s head bobbed up and down in the spring, and a strand of hair would stretch out from time to time and poke at Young Master Hai’s clone. With every poke, a miserable cry would shoot out from Young Master Hai’s mouth.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior Chu, is there a way to extract the inner demon from Young Master Hai’s body?”

Pavilion Master Chu shook her head—she had grown her shoulders and collarbone now, and could finally shake her head properly. “At this time, I can only create a projection of his inner demon through a magical technique; it’s like looking at the inner demon through a mirror. However, it’s very difficult to extract an inner demon from someone’s body. This process is like pulling someone’s reflection straight out of a mirror, and it’s very difficult. I’m taking notes from Soft Feather’s inner demon clone technique. However, I have yet to figure out anything substantial.”

“Senior Chu, you got this,” said Song Shuhang—he was thinking that if Senior Chu did have a way to extract inner demons, then he could help Fellow Daoist Ding Gan by extracting his inner demon. This could be considered repayment for the gift they brought when visiting him.

What a pity.

“But, I do have an idea,” Pavilion Master Chu said. “Under the heavenly tribulation, the form of an inner demon would change. When an ordinary inner demon transforms into an inner demon tribulation, there is an instant in which the inner demon takes a physical form. If we were to combine my means with Soft Feather’s inner demon clone technique, perhaps we could extract the inner demon tribulation. However, this needs some experimentation. The next time you transcend a tribulation, we can try it out if an inner demon is born.”

Song Shuhang said, “Oh, there’s actually a little fellow daoist who is about to reach the Third Stage and is currently with me. He has the seed of an inner demon inside him, but his inner demon is lurking deep within him. He probably hasn’t discovered it yet.”

Pavilion Master Chu asked, “Is he about to transcend his tribulation?”

Song Shuhang nodded, and said, “He plans on transcending the tribulation on the 22nd. I was wondering if there was any way to help him get rid of his inner demon.”

Pavilion Master Chu said, “Let me take a look. Give me a hand.”

“Sure, Pavilion Master Chu. If we can, let’s help this little friend. These three little fellow daoists are very polite,” Song Shuhang added.

Everybody liked polite kids.

??????

Song Shuhang’s consciousness returned to his body.

The space above his head fluctuated, and long black hair drilled out of the Inner World and “grew” directly out of Song Shuhang’s head.

This hair was so long that if it were allowed to fall, it could probably fill an entire room.

However, the long black hair did not fall, and after it was extended, it began to flutter about.

From the perspective of the three little fellow daoists, Senior Tyrannical Song’s hair grew wildly until reaching a length of around seven or eight meters. The long hair then fluttered upward, ignoring gravity.

The state that Profound Sage Tyrannical Song was in was akin to a demon king descending upon the world.

The three little fellow daoists trembled silently. They weren’t frightened by Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s appearance, but rather the terrifying pressure that emanated from the long hair. The pressure made them breathless, and they could not help but want to immediately curl up on the ground.

This was the pressure brought about by a huge gap in power—and this was with Pavilion Master Chu restraining the aura she was releasing as much as she could. If Pavilion Master Chu directly released her Immortal Light Wheel, these little guys’ eyes would not be able to handle the sight of the laws, and would directly go blind.

Pavilion Master Chu’s sweet voice sounded. “Are these the three little fellows?”

Song Shuhang said with a smile, “Yes, they are. They’re very polite kids.”

Pavilion Master Chu’s long hair sensed the state of the three little fellow daoists, and then she said to Song Shuhang, [Very polite kids? Well, you’re a rude and rough kid who has no courtesy.]

“...” Song Shuhang.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword laughed. “Hahahaha.”

Pavilion Master Chu’s voice transmission was not blocked from its ears.

[Who is the little fellow daoist who has an inner demon?] Pavilion Master Chu asked again through voice transmission.

“This is little fellow daoist Ding Gan.” Song Shuhang then pointed at Ding Gan.

Ding Gan lowered his head and slowly approached Song Shuhang.

Pavilion Master Chu stretched out one strand of her long hair and gently touched Ding Gan.

“Ah~” A scream sounded from Ding Gan’s body.

“???” Ding Gan.

I didn’t scream, who screamed?

Pavilion Master Chu went straight to the point. “Little fellow daoist, you have an inner demon.”

“An inner demon?” Ding Gan looked confused.

Pavilion Master Chu said, “Shuhang, bring me some water.”

Song Shuhang’s psychic energy moved, and he opened the faucet in the small courtyard. Afterward, a stream of clear water was brought over using psychic energy, falling in front of Pavilion Master Chu’s long hair.

Pavilion Master Chu’s long hair lightly touched the clear water, and the clear water turned into a mirror that reflected Ding Gan.

In the mirror, a bunch of squid-like tentacles appeared.

Pavilion Master Chu said, “Look, this is your inner demon.”

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “What type of inner demon is it?”

Pavilion Master Chu said slowly, “This is love.”

Senior Chu, I haven’t cultivated for that long, but don’t lie to me. How can love be this mess of warping tentacles?

Senior Chu transmitted her voice, and said, [Why would I even lie to you? This group of twisting tentacles is undoubtedly ‘love,’ it’s the inner demon of love.]

It was precisely because this type of love was taboo and twisted that it had to be avoided. This type of love was not the same as normal love, and it was this type that could produce an inner demon.

If it had been a normal type of love, it would have been very difficult for the cultivator to have gotten an inner demon—because they generally had immunity to such things.

Love was a very important emotion in the life of a young cultivator, and it could give birth to strong emotional fluctuations.

Love was a double-edged sword. It could make a person burst out with outstanding potential, but it could also dampen their dao heart.

Therefore, when it came to the aspect of love, every major force had special courses on it.

The psychology of love had been an important subject in the cultivation world since ancient times.

Improving one’s character, developing one’s dao heart, and cultivating the heart before cultivating immortality.

At present, in some proper cultivation forces, there would usually be seniors who would deliver lectures for younger cultivators. Occasionally, there would be lessons in these lectures on how to correctly view the concept of love, how to view one’s dao companion, how to resolve a lovelorn state as quickly as possible, how to deal with heartbreak, and many other topics concerning love.

There were also some forces who would teach their disciples to look down on love. They would frame it such that as long as you were strong enough and lived long enough, you could fall in love and have a 20-year-old dao companion even when you were 1000 years old.

A portion of the old-fashioned forces would even publicize the statement that “only the strong are worthy of love.”

??????

Ding Gan frowned at the sight of the tentacles in the water mirror.

An inner demon?

Love?

Fortunately, I came to see Profound Sage Tyrannical Song this time... Otherwise, I would not have even known that I had an inner demon. If I wasn’t careful, I might have gone astray and died.

He looked closely at the tentacles in the mirror, and began to think about the reason for the birth of this inner demon.

??????

[Taboo love?] Song Shuhang, Pavilion Master Chu, and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword entered a small-scale group voice transmission state.

Pavilion Master Chu also involved Su Clan’s Sixteen, Senior Turtle and the others who were watching from upstairs in the scope of the group voice transmission.

Scarlet Heaven Sword said, [Love is such a troublesome thing: it will bring people hope and strength during times of despair, but it can be the one to bring despair and make people lose their desire to live... This is why it’s better to be a sentient weapon like me.]

[However, it seems that little fellow daoist Ding Gan doesn’t even know about his inner demon. Does he not know about such a taboo or twisted love in his heart?] Song Shuhang asked curiously. [If it is related to love, what kind of love was it for it to have turned into an inner demon? Does it have something to do with a person he loved? Or does it have more to do with himself?]

The black-skinned Scarlet Heaven Sword reminded Shuhang, [Don’t go around calling everyone little fellow daoist, call him big brother.]

Su Clan’s Sixteen, who was watching from upstairs, could not help but laugh.

Song Shuhang habitually used the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique?.

“Aaaah~ Good~~” the black-skinned Scarlet Heaven Sword mumbled, its voice cute and crisp.

The three little fellow daoists facing them were dumbfounded.

Pavilion Master Chu transmitted her voice, and said, [That’s because his heavenly tribulation is imminent. When one’s heavenly tribulation is imminent, some minor emotions in the cultivator’s heart will emerge. As long as there are loopholes in their heart or mind, sometimes even small loopholes that they do not notice would be magnified during such periods and transform into an inner demon tribulation. This is why the inner demon tribulation is the most hated tribulation of cultivators.]

In other words, little fellow daoist Ding Gan’s loophole was one he did not even know of.

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, [But there normally isn’t an inner demon tribulation in a Third Stage heavenly tribulation, right?]

Some time ago, Su Kongjun had transcended his Third Stage heavenly tribulation. Normally, the inner demon tribulation only began appearing in the Fourth Stage heavenly tribulation.

Senior Turtle replied, [Regardless of which heavenly tribulation it is, if the cultivator has an inner demon before their heavenly tribulation, there is a chance of it transforming into an inner demon tribulation.]

Pavilion Master Chu remarked, [Even if you are lucky, and your inner demon does not transform into an inner demon tribulation during the heavenly tribulation, your inner demon will undoubtedly grow larger... If you aren’t careful, you can still end up experiencing cultivation deviation.]

“Senior Tyrannical Song,” Ding Gan said, “is there a way to resolve my inner demon?”

“At present, if you want to deal with your inner demon, you can only rely on your own dao heart to resist it,” Pavilion Master Chu answered in Song Shuhang’s place. “Now that you already know that you have an inner demon, and that it is related to love, you can be prepared for it when it comes.”

As long as one had precautions in their heart, and their dao heart was firm enough when the time came, then they would not have a problem resisting such a weak inner demon.

His inner demon was nothing serious. In fact, it was even so weak that he, himself, did not notice it.

Scarlet Heaven Sword added, “If you can know what your inner demon is related to, then simply strengthen your mental defense in that regard.”

Song Shuhang and the others all looked at Ding Gan with some curiosity.

What was the love that caused the young man to form an inner demon?

Such gossip could always arouse people’s curiosity.

“Actually, even I have no idea in that regard.” Ding Gan smiled wryly after sensing everyone’s curiosity.

Senior Turtle jumped down from upstairs, and asked curiously, “You are at that phase when the feeling of love would be overflowing within you. Have you never fallen in love with someone else?”

Song Shuhang said, “Senior Turtle, you need to deal with that disease of jumping down from windows. Next time, you should take the stairs.”

Senior Turtle waved its forelimbs, and said, “It’s fine. I’m a turtle, not a human. Isn’t it normal for animals to jump out of windows? Cats, and all those other animals, they all go out through windows, don’t they?”

“...” Song Shuhang.

Ding Gan said embarrassedly, “Actually, I already have a dao companion, and our relationship is very stable. Our relationship should not have had the conditions to foster an inner demon.”

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “If it’s not your fault, it’s Shuhang’s fault.”

“???” Song Shuhang.

What does this have to do with me? What did I do? I have no fault in this.

At this moment, the virtuous lamia swooped out from behind Song Shuhang, and said, “What is love!”

Fairy Creation followed right after, and said, “What is filial piety!”

The two fairies floated beside Song Shuhang on his left and right, flaring out their arms like white cranes as they stood on one leg like a golden rooster. Their eyes then stared straight at Song Shuhang’s shadow.

After a while, the black-skinned Soft Feather shyly emerged from his shadow, and assumed the same pose before saying, “Do you know the greatness of maternal love?”

On the opposite side, Ding Gan’s face suddenly turned pale.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said slowly, “Exactly.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

“No, it can’t be this. I’m sure of this, and I don’t have any psychological problems when it comes to maternal love.” Ding Gan waved his hands again and again.

Pavilion Master Chu pondered for a moment, and then she suddenly plucked a hair from the top of Song Shuhang’s head.

Then, she placed the hair in Ding Gan’s hands. “Take this strand of hair, it might bring you a little luck.”

“Thank you, Senior.” Ding Gan happily accepted the strand of hair.

This is Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s hair, it should definitely work as a protective amulet, right?

??????

Pavilion Master Chu put away the water mirror.

The three polite young cultivators bid their goodbyes to Song Shuhang and took their leave.

“Senior Chu, does my hair have a lucky effect? ??Can it really defend against inner demons?” Song Shuhang asked curiously. If there was such a function, he could grow it... He had the ?Hair Growing Technique?, and he could get rich just by selling his hair.

Pavilion Master Chu shook his head, and said, “No.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

Pavilion Master Chu said slowly, “However, after all, it is the hair of the first Sage in a thousand years, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song. Moreover, it was a cultivator of my level who endorsed it. As long as I say that it brings good fortune, ordinary little cultivators will definitely believe it.”

In the case of this peerless expert’s endorsement certification, what was fake could be made real.

Pavilion Master Chu continued, “As long as he believes, there will be a sort of ‘hint’ in his heart. Even if he encounters an inner demon, with the strand of hair in hand, he will subconsciously think that it can help him resist the inner demon and boost his confidence. It’s a small trick, but sometimes it’s practical.”

“So that’s the case.” Song Shuhang raised his posture, and wrote this action down in his notebook—in the future, when his disciples Chu Chu and Little Cai transcended their tribulation, he could invite a peerless expert to appear to consecrate them with blessings as a “protective amulet,” boosting their confidence in transcending their tribulation.

The seniors truly are worthy of being seniors. There is still a lot for me to learn from them.

Pavilion Master Chu continued, “In addition, I placed a ?Divine Weapon Appraisal? mark on the strand of hair. When this young man transcends his calamity, we can watch him from a distance. Perhaps we can crack the mysteries of his inner demon and extract it.”

Whenever they made a move, reliable seniors truly were impeccable.

Song Shuhang still had a long way to go before becoming a reliable senior such as that.

Song Shuhang said, “Then let’s wait for the 22nd.”

He could not provide little fellow daoist Ding Gan with help. The little fellow daoist had to overcome his tribulation on his own.

??????

Seeing that it was still early, Song Shuhang prepared to go to the vegetable market to buy some ingredients to try out and show off his cooking skills.

Sixteen got ready to go with him.

The other seniors stayed at home.

Song Shuhang opened the door, and stepped out of the building.

Suddenly, the sound of loud rumbling filled his ears.

In the next moment... a normal immortal shuttle suddenly emerged from the void.

It was an imitation of the [Universe-Piercing Flying Shuttle].

Before becoming enlightened, the sixth Wielder of the Will possessed the fastest flying shuttle in the world... Now, this flying shuttle was in the hands of Senior White Two.

Later on, the current Senior White and Senior White Two exchanged some technology, and he acquired an imitation. However, it was not much worse than the real one.

The shuttle appeared in an instant, stopping right as it reached Song Shuhang’s stomach.

“Aaah~ Ah~” Song Shuhang screamed four times, and was knocked back and fell into the yard.

“Shuhang, are you all right?” Su Clan’s Sixteen ran beside him.

Song Shuhang got up from the ground, and touched his stomach. “Ugh... I’m fine.”

...When the flying shuttle appeared, it had immediately stopped by the entrance. While the force from the impact might have seemed like it was a lot, in fact, it did not even harm a single strand of hair on his body.

True Monarch Eternal Fire hurriedly jumped out of the immortal shuttle, and said, “Little friend Shuhang, are you okay? When we left, I set the immortal shuttle’s navigation destination to the entrance. I wasn’t able to stop in time... It was simply too fast.”

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “Senior Eternal Fire was the one driving? Where is Senior White?”

True Monarch Eternal Fire smiled bitterly, and said, “Fellow Daoist White was indeed the one driving it initially, but as we were flying back, the immortal shuttle stopped on a meteoroid, and he began to go into a daze. Therefore, I had no choice but to take over in driving the immortal shuttle back. By the way, it’s already about time. Let’s go to the scholarly faction. Who wants to drive the car? This immortal shuttle is a bit too fast for me. I feel uncomfortable driving it.”

Sixteen shook her head, and said, “I’ve never driven an immortal shuttle.”

Senior Turtle said, “I’m much more accustomed to just using spatial passages to travel. In addition, my turtle form isn’t suitable for driving a flying shuttle.”

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “By the way, Senior Turtle, what is your human form like?”

After a monster cultivator reached the Fifth Stage, it could take on a human form. Since Senior Turtle was a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm existence, it should have long acquired a human form.

Senior Turtle chuckled. “You want to see my human form?”

Song Shuhang said, “Well, I am a little curious.”

Senior Turtle said regretfully, “Unfortunately, you are not beautiful enough.”

Song Shuhang responded, “Huh?”

“I only show my human form to those who I think are beautiful enough.” Senior Turtle covered its face shyly with its forelimbs, and said, “I will only show the best side of myself to the person I like.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

Su Clan’s Sixteen smiled and patted Shuhang lightly, comforting him, “Shuhang, you’re actually quite attractive.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “While you are worth a second look, you look quite plain at first glance.”

Song Shuhang looked up at the sky—this time he did not use the ❮Saber-Nurturing Technique❯ on the black Scarlet Heaven Sword.

This was because he realized that the black Scarlet Heaven Sword seemed to have been looking for opportunities to pierce his heart recently, piercing it in all kinds of manners.

Afterward, it would trick him to use the ❮Saber-Nurturing Technique❯.

At this time, Sister White Dragon said calmly, “Don’t listen to Fellow Daoist Turtle’s nonsense. Its cultivation technique is very special. It makes it difficult to show its human form. When it reveals its human form, it bursts out with its strongest power.”

“That sounds cool,” Lady Onion said.

Song Shuhang could not help but say, “Senior Turtle, isn’t your cultivation technique set in reverse? For normal monster cultivators, don’t they show their true combat power only after they show their true forms?”

“Who said that?” Lady Onion immediately said in disagreement. “My human form’s pure combat power is higher than that of my true form.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

True Monarch Eternal Fire carried the shuttle into the yard and sighed. “Little friend Shuhang, the topic jumps so quickly even when you guys chat offline? Anyway, let’s get back to the main topic. Who’s going to drive the immortal shuttle?”

Song Shuhang stood up, and he quietly reached out to touch his waist—his waist was perfectly fine.

He then opened his mouth, and said, “I’ve only driven an immortal boat once. It was a version modified by Senior White, so driving it didn’t feel much different from driving a normal car. In other words, I’m quite sure I can’t drive an ordinary immortal shuttle.”

After saying that, Song Shuhang turned his head and looked at Fairy Creation, the virtuous lamia, and the black-skinned Soft Feather. Did any of these three fairies know how to drive?

The little heads of the three fairies tilted to the right in unison, and they all looked at Song Shuhang cutely.

It looked like they were acting out a play.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “I know how to drive it, but my second form has no feet, and can’t drive it.”

“There’s nothing we can do. I guess we can only call a chauffeur,” said Senior Eternal Fire. He then took out his phone, and began swiping on its screen.

At the side, Song Shuhang’s face was calm.

Ever since Song Shuhang had experienced the limited flying swords and the Whizzing Flying Sword APP in the scholarly faction, he was no longer surprised when hearing about immortal shuttle chauffeurs existing in the world of cultivation. It now sounded very natural to him.

Song Shuhang suggested, “Senior, why don’t I just store the flying shuttle inside my Inner World, and then we fly to the scholarly faction on our swords and sabers.”

“Don’t, let’s just call a chauffeur. Anyway, it’s not that expensive to get one,” True Monarch Eternal Fire insisted. “To be honest... Fellow Daoist White’s flying shuttle is very exciting to ride. I feel that if you aren’t the one driving it, riding in it should be very enjoyable. While I don’t want to drive it, I still want to ride in it for a while. An opportunity like this is hard to come by, let’s not miss it.”

Song Shuhang always felt that True Monarch Eternal Fire was pulling everyone into a trap—he had already fallen into the trap himself, so he now wanted to pull a few more people to fall into it with him.

“Come on, a fellow daoist has already accepted the request,” True Monarch Eternal Fire said. “The fellow daoist who took the request isn’t that far from us. They should arrive in 10 minutes at most. Let’s take a break and adjust our states.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “By the way, what about Senior White?”

True Monarch Eternal Fire replied, “He’s still in a daze inside the shuttle.”

❄️❄️❄️

About 10 minutes later.

In the sky, a figure rushed over, and finally landed in front of Medicine Master’s building.

The person who had rushed over did not fly over using any magical treasure or weapon. He had run over solely using his two legs instead.

The man shouted, “Fellow Daoists, are you the ones who needed an immortal shuttle chauffeur?”

His voice was thick and magnetic.

When Song Shuhang listened to this voice, he suddenly remembered the voice of one of his teachers for some reason—it was the type of voice used when reading articles out loud.

“Yes, the door is open, please come in,” said True Monarch Eternal Fire.

After True Monarch Eternal Fire said that, the door opened.

A man with disheveled hair and cyan-colored modern clothes entered the yard.

He was clearly dressed neatly... But for some reason, he gave off the illusion that he was rather rough.

In addition, Song Shuhang also noticed that the shoes on the man’s feet were the other way around, with his left shoe on his right foot, and his right shoe on his left foot.

After the man entered, he stretched out his hand and stroked his messy hair behind his head, revealing a very temperamental middle-aged man’s face. He had a face that would make others inexplicably trust him.

“Eh.” When Song Shuhang saw the man’s face, he suddenly felt that it was very familiar.

There was a name in his heart that he wanted to call out, but when he opened his mouth, he discovered that he did not know the man’s name, and he did not even know who the man was at all.

This feeling reminded him of the senior from the Nine Provinces Number One Group whom he would only remember whenever he checked his phone’s contact list

He silently thought, Is my ‘everything I see feels familiar’ disease acting up again?

“Fellow Daoist, this is our immortal shuttle. Our destination is the scholarly faction,” said True Monarch Eternal Fire—when he saw this man, he also felt a strong sense of familiarity about him. Therefore, he did not even ask for the other party’s daoist name, and simply chose to trust him.

“No problem, the scholarly faction it is then. I’m very familiar with the place.” The man smiled gently.

The door of the flying shuttle opened, and the man swiftly entered the vehicle, “This immortal shuttle is awesome. Come on, everyone. The operation interface is not much different from that of a normal immortal shuttle. I’ll be able to drive it perfectly well.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen, Senior Turtle, Sister White Dragon, and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword all entered the immortal shuttle.

Behind Song Shuhang, both the virtuous lamia and the black-skinned Soft Feather returned into his body.

As for Fairy Creation, she did not completely return into his body, and decided to leave her head silently poking out from behind Song Shuhang’s neck. Because of this, it looked as if Song Shuhang had two heads.

She was quietly looking at the man who was going to drive the immortal shuttle.

As if sensing her gaze, the man turned his head, looked at Fairy Creation, and smiled gently.

In response to this, Fairy Creation was like a naughty student who had been discovered by the teacher in the middle of class, and she hurriedly returned into Song Shuhang’s body with a swoosh.

“Senior, do we know each other from somewhere?” Song Shuhang could not help but ask after stepping inside the flying shuttle.

The man laughed, and said, “I know you. You’re the first Sage in 1,000 years, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song. But you probably don’t know me. In fact, I have a very common face. When you look at my face, do you feel that I look familiar? But then after thinking about it carefully, do you feel that among the friends and people you know, there are many whose faces are similar to mine? Well, that’s because my face is very common. That’s why whenever people see me, they feel that I’m familiar. Hahaha.”

Song Shuhang and Senior Eternal Fire nodded silently.

“Sit down, everyone,” the uncle who was driving said loudly. He then grabbed the control stick of the shuttle, and started up the shuttle with one foot.

Boom~ Senior White’s immortal shuttle rose into the sky instantly.

It soared up vertically at a speed that seemed like something had exploded behind them.

The strong sense of weightlessness made Song Shuhang’s body stiff.

This immortal shuttle really has Senior White’s style... It pursues extreme speed and excitement.

In an instant, the shuttle had risen up high into the sky.

After slightly adjusting the angle, it rushed towards the position of the scholarly faction’s White Cloud Academy.

This flying shuttle was an imitation of the Universe-Piercing Flying Shuttle.

The Universe-Piercing Flying Shuttle was a work made by the sixth Wielder of the Will, and it was known to have the title of reaching the fastest speeds excluding spatial techniques! When it came to short-distance journeys, it was even faster than spatial techniques—spatial teleportation still needed one to open a spatial passage and enter before reaching the other side.

Although the imitation that Senior White had was not as good as the real one, it was a product of the joint efforts of Senior White and Senior White Two, so its speed was only slightly worse than the real one’s.

In its full-speed burst state, it was among the fastest across the entire universe.

Moreover, this uncle, who was driving the immortal shuttle, was clearly an expert at driving flying shuttles. As soon as they rose into the sky, he immediately pushed the shuttle to its fastest speed!

This was definitely a maneuver at the professional level.

Song “Another Life Saved” Shuhang.
