Meanwhile, in the void outside the world.

A figure with slender legs stepped out of a spatial gate. A small sun was rolling as it followed behind her, sending a warm light all around it.

The Heavenly Emperor stretched her waist, and said, “It’s almost time.”

In the current scholarly faction, there were also members of the Heavenly City—to be precise, there were some disciples of the scholarly faction who had once been a part of the Heavenly City.

After the last battle for the position of Wielder of the Heaven’s Will, the scholarly faction met with a dire situation and fell apart. The disciples of the scholarly faction were attacked by the demons of the Netherworld, and they nearly collapsed from this.

After a long period of time, the Heavenly Emperor established the Heavenly City to suppress the universe.

The original Heavenly City was all-encompassing. Whether it was Buddhism, Daoism, the scholarly faction, monsters, or demons, as long as they met the conditions, they would all be accepted into the city. Among them, some disciples of the scholarly faction had joined the Ancient Heavenly City.

After the collapse of the Heavenly City, among the descendants of those who were from the scholarly faction, there were those who returned to become disciples of the scholarly faction.

There was nothing wrong with this group of disciples; they were no different from normal scholarly faction disciples.

However, the former Heavenly City was the path of the Heavenly Emperor.

As long as she joined the Heavenly City, the Heavenly Emperor could collect some information from these scholarly faction disciples through her path.

Once she gathered enough of these bits of information, the Heavenly Emperor could easily acquire the information she wanted.

Information involving things such as the Heavenly City Fragments that were hidden inside the scholarly faction, or the world of the golden lotus that the scholarly faction possessed.

The Heavenly Emperor thought to herself,?I’ll focus on getting information on the Heavenly City Fragments first.

She had no intention of going head-to-head against the scholarly faction—she merely wanted to take back what was hers.

She still had several things in her possession that the scholarly faction would absolutely not be able to refuse—for example, she had the corpses of some of the fallen Tribulation Transcenders who were among the scholarly faction’s 13 Tribulation Trasnceders. She could use them to exchange for her Heavenly City Fragments.

The Heavenly Emperor adjusted her state, and prepared to open a spatial gate.

But just as she stretched out her hand, she suddenly discovered that the space had been locked.

“It seems that my luck today isn’t bad.” A man’s voice sounded.

From within a shadow, a figure stepped out. He was wearing a sheet and looked particularly forlorn.

The Heavenly Emperor said sweetly, “Senior Almighty Merchant, we meet again.”

“Don’t address me like that. I really can’t take you addressing me as senior.” The Almighty Merchant waved his hand, and said, “I didn’t expect the dignified Heavenly Emperor to be like this...”

The Heavenly Emperor giggled, and said, “Cute?”

“...” The Almighty Merchant.

“The fragments of the Ancient Heavenly City were originally mine.” The Heavenly Emperor stretched out her fingers, and said seriously, “I merely want to retrieve my things.”

The Almighty Merchant said, “Those things, I bought them through regular channels. I bought the fragments from the successors of your Ancient Heavenly City, so those fragments are already mine.”

“How heart-stifling.” The Heavenly Emperor stretched out her hand and placed her hand over her chest. “Those prodigal things. I’m going to kill them.”

“Now, hand over the fragments,” the Almighty Merchant said slowly. “If I were faced with the version of you from the ancient era, I would only be able to consider myself unlucky. But now... my fists are harder.”

“Fists are the hard truth. It seems what you previously told me about business having to be carried out reasonably is nothing but nonsense. In the end, you still depend on your strength.” The Heavenly Emperor raised her arms, and said, “Okay, I admit defeat. Then, I will be giving the three Eastern Spring Pavilion fragments to Fellow Daoist.”

After saying that, the Heavenly Emperor threw three pieces of compressed Heavenly City Fragments over to the Almighty Merchant.

The Almighty Merchant had an expression of disbelief when he saw this.

She’s actually returning them?

He pulled out a long golden staff and used it to tap on the Heavenly City Fragments to check on them.

These are actual Eastern Spring Pavilion fragments! They’re the real deal!

But the Heavenly Emperor was too cooperative; she had surely hidden something inside them—if he were to take them just like that, then he should pluck off his head and give it to Almighty Seller to kick around!

“What tricks are you playing here?” the Almighty Merchant said solemnly. He then stretched out his hand and used the sheet on his body to cover the three Ancient Heavenly City Fragments before putting them away.

“Why are all of you business people like this? You’re always full of distrust toward others. When I wasn’t cooperating with you, you said that you had a harder fist than me, and now that I have softened up and decided to cooperate and return your goods to you, you’re stirring up more trouble. What do I have to do to make you satisfied? You’re honestly making things really difficult here.” The Heavenly Emperor laughed, and said, “However, I do like seeing you vexed like this.”

“...” The Almighty Merchant.

The Heavenly Emperor said slowly, “I can assure you that the goods I returned to you are the fragments of Eastern Spring Pavilion. Moreover, I did not secretly exchange them for others, these are the three fragments that you took away from me back then.”

The little sun behind her exuded a dazzling light, setting off her stunning appearance.

“What did you do?” The Almighty Merchant’s heart felt stifled.

For the first time, he found himself extremely uncomfortable when the other party suddenly decided to cooperate with him. He discovered that he would much rather prefer them to fight, and that he would have much more peace of mind if he had just snatched the Heavenly City Fragments back from the Heavenly Emperor instead.

“I’ve already made my move. This is a battle of ability between us. If you can crack what I’ve hidden in the three fragments, then you win. Otherwise, you lose.” The Heavenly Emperor stretched out her hands, revealing a confident look on her face.

“You’re that confident?” The Almighty Merchant clutched his sheet and shrank back into a ball.

“That’s because I am the Heavenly Emperor.” The Heavenly Emperor raised her head slightly.

The Almighty Merchant laughed and disappeared into the shadows.

No matter what the Heavenly Emperor had done to the three Heavenly City Fragments, as long as they were in his hands, he was absolutely confident that he would be able to find out what she had left.

The Almighty Merchant disappeared, and the spatial blockade was lifted.

“Study it well, Fellow Daoist Almighty Merchant.” A slight smile emerged on the Heavenly Emperor’s face.

She then opened a spatial gate, stepped into it, and directly traveled into the vicinity of the scholarly faction’s White Cloud Academy.

Even if Fellow Daoist Almighty Merchant studies those fragments until next year, he won’t be able to find anything. After all, I didn’t leave anything on those fragments.

She could already picture the scene of the Almighty Merchant scratching his head while studying the fragments diligently.

She liked leaving other people in great confusion.

As for why she simply returned the three Heavenly City Fragments to Almighty Merchant?

This was because the thing she needed from the three Heavenly City Fragments, particularly the parts of them that were related to her path, had already been retrieved by her. As such, she would be able to make up for the lack of the three fragments.

In the ancient era, the Heavenly City was often demolished or partially damaged due to various accidents, and the Heavenly Emperor naturally had certain means to repair such damage.

These three fragments were not large in size, so it would not be too troublesome to recreate them.

Last but not least, she knew that the seller of the Eastern Spring Pavilion was little friend Song Shuhang. This gave her a lot more room to play with... She found little friend Song Shuhang a lot more fun to play with. She would much rather spend her time playing with Song Shuhang rather than waste her time with the Almighty Merchant.

“Mm-hm, time is precious.” The Heavenly Emperor’s figure disappeared into the spatial passage.

She was still busy retrieving the Heavenly City Fragments of the scholarly faction.

??????

At the scholarly faction

Senior White’s clone, Song Shuhang, Su Clan’s Sixteen, Senior Turtle, Lady Onion, and True Monarch White Crane were brought by True Monarch Eternal Fire to the entrance of the world of the golden lotus.

The entrance to the world of the golden lotus had not yet been opened.

As Song Shuhang approached, he sensed a faint resonance between his inner world and the world of the golden lotus.

However, during the last accident in the world of the golden lotus, Song Shuhang and True Monarch Eternal Fire had worked together to seal up the passage connecting the world of the golden lotus and the world of the black lotus.

Therefore, Song Shuhang’s Inner World was unable to connect with the world of the golden lotus.

After the two small worlds faintly resonated with one another, they quieted down.

Song Shuhang turned his head and looked at Senior White’s clone, who was beside him.

He was neither suddenly dozing off nor entering seclusion. Senior White’s clone was in a normal state.

Coupled with his decent luck and that there was no darkness in the space between his brows, Song Shuhang felt especially calm.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior Eternal Fire, what are we going to do next?”

True Monarch Eternal Fire responded, “I’ll show little friend Shuhang and Fellow Daoist White something first. When I heard little friend Shuhang mention that he transferred an Ancient Heavenly City Fragment into his small world, I returned to the scholarly faction to prepare and try doing the same. But in the end, it did not go smoothly.”

After saying that, True Monarch Eternal Fire clapped his hands. In the distance, a scholarly faction disciple controlled several pages of scriptures and carried a huge fragment of a public square.

Those texts on the scripture pages were written by the scholarly faction disciple by memory. After activation, 20 scripture pages were able to support the weight of a huge public square.

“The entrance to our world of the golden lotus is relatively large,” explained True Monarch Eternal Fire. “Anything the size of this huge public square can be stuffed through and into the world of the golden lotus.”

Song Shuhang was envious.

With the thousands upon thousands of years that the scholarly faction had been operating, the sect was easily able to make use of the world of the golden lotus. Once the world of the golden lotus was born, it was very huge, and it was a complete small world. They had been able to make great use of it and develop it in a short period.

Meanwhile, Song Shuhang was working on his Inner World nearly all on his own. In addition, the size of his small world was completely incomparable to that of the world of the golden lotus.

True Monarch Eternal Fire said, “Normally, other objects of the same volume can easily be sent into the world of the golden lotus. However, when transferring the Heavenly City Fragments, we are faced with a form of rejection.”

That group of scholarly disciples controlled the Heavenly City Public Square Fragment, and stuffed it into the world of the golden lotus.

With that, the fragment was slowly sent into the world of the golden lotus.

Song Shuhang said curiously, “Isn’t it going quite well?”

As soon as he said that, Song Shuhang’s Inner World sensed the world of the golden lotus producing a throbbing like it was experiencing nausea.

In the next moment, the huge fragment of a public square was spat out.

Whoosh~

Perhaps due to the influence of the Inner World, the Heavenly City Public Square Fragment that had been spat out by the world of the golden lotus shot straight toward Song Shuhang.

“Why was it reflected over there?” True Monarch Eternal Fire said softly—nevertheless, the scholarly faction had already long prepared for this reaction, so there was no need to worry.

“Be careful!” Song Shuhang took Sixteen’s little hand, and brought her behind Senior Turtle to squat down and hide.

Senior Turtle was currently in its three-meter-tall giant turtle form—in this form, it was relatively wide.

Its turtle shell was just enough for Song Shuhang and Sixteen to hide behind.

“Aaah, what do I do?” cried Lady Onion. Since she was too lazy to walk, she was stuck on the enlightenment stone on Senior Turtle’s shell.

If the Heavenly City Fragment crashed down on Senior Turtle’s shell, wouldn’t she be squashed into onion paste?

Senior Eternal Fire smiled, and said, “Don’t worry, we have long been prepared for this. This isn’t a problem at all.”

Boom!

The Ancient Heavenly City Fragment that was spat out hit an invisible barrier before finally falling in front of Senior Turtle slowly.

Senior White’s clone said, “Don’t worry, you have decent luck today. There definitely won’t be a case of you getting squashed by a Heavenly City Fragment.”

With Senior White having said that, Song Shuhang felt at ease all of a sudden.

The black-skinned Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “As it is now, it would at most crash in front of you, but it definitely would not hurt you.”

Song Shuhang suddenly got the urge to move his right hand and use the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique?.

True Monarch Eternal Fire said, “This is what happens to most Heavenly City Fragments. Even if they can fit and are then sent into the world of the golden lotus, they will be rejected and repelled by the world of the golden lotus after a short while.”

Senior White’s clone squatted beside the Heavenly City Fragment. “Are all Heavenly City Fragments rejected?”

True Monarch Eternal Fire said, “Almost all of them are. So far, the scholarly faction has only been able to transfer two very small fragments into the world of the golden lotus. This is why I asked Shuhang to come and have a look.”

Song Shuhang walked forward to the side of the Heavenly City Fragment, and stretched out his hand to feel out the fragment.

He did not feel any difference between this Ancient Heavenly City Fragment and any of the other fragments that he had been in contact with.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior White, what do you think?”

Senior White replied, “I don’t know yet. Let me check it out first. We can enter the world of the golden lotus and take a look at the two Heavenly City Fragments that were able to be moved in and see what’s different with them. What do you think?”

Song Shuhang nodded, and said, “Just now, when the Heavenly City Fragment was sent into the world of the golden lotus, my Inner World sensed that the world of the golden lotus felt nauseated.”

“Nauseated?” True Monarch Eternal Fire looked bewildered.

Lady Onion snapped her fingers. “So you’re saying that the Heavenly City Fragment was not in line with the tastes of the world of the golden lotus, and it found it disgusting and spat it out? If that’s the case, do we have to make the Heavenly City Fragment taste better?”

Song Shuhang chuckled, and said, “For example, sprinkle some fragrant onion oil on it?”

Lady Onion shivered.

“I’m just kidding. You work for me now, and I promised not to take your onion sprouts out of nowhere,” Song Shuhang said seriously. “That is, unless you give me your permission.”

Lady Onion shook her head desperately.

At this moment, Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “Shuhang, since the world of the golden lotus rejects this Heavenly City Fragment, does your small world also reject it?”

Song Shuhang thought for a moment, and said, “Senior Eternal Fire, should we try transferring this Heavenly City Fragment into my small world and see if my Inner World rejects it?”

They just had to be careful when carrying the experiment out lest the Inner World directly incorporated the Heavenly City Fragment into itself.

“No problem, we actually had the same thought,” True Monarch Eternal Fire said.

Song Shuhang was invited by True Monarch Eternal Fire with the idea of ??letting him transfer the Heavenly City Fragment into his personal small space.

They wanted to know whether the problem stemmed from the Ancient Heavenly City Fragments or their world of the golden lotus.

“Then let me give it a try.” Song Shuhang rubbed his hands together, and pressed them on the Heavenly City Fragment. Afterward, he called out, “Senior White, do you have a way to shrink down this Heavenly City Fragment?”

Senior White’s clone replied, “Just cut it. Cut it up into several pieces and put it back together inside.”

“Is there any different way?” Song Shuhang said—after all, this thing was owned by the scholarly faction, so it wouldn’t be good if they broke it.

Senior White’s clone glanced at the size of the Heavenly City Fragment, and after thinking for a short while, he nodded. “Well, I do have a magical technique that might come in handy. Give me a moment...”

After saying that, Senior White’s clone suddenly disappeared.

Seeing Senior White suddenly disappear, Song Shuhang’s heart leaped up!

Could Senior White be leaving to avoid bad fortune again?

The last time that this had happened in the scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus, he had died countless times. As such, Song Shuhang was particularly sensitive to such things.

“Shuhang, are you alright?” When Sixteen saw Song Shuhang’s nervous look, she reached out and patted his back lightly.

Song Shuhang said, “It’s okay. I have decent fortune today, I’ll surely be fine.”

He repeatedly reminded himself that he had a decent fortune today.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword suggested, “If you’re nervous, sing a song to ease the tension.”

Pa!

Song Shuhang’s hand used the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? on the black Scarlet Heaven Sword.

“???” The black- Scarlet Heaven Sword.

It had given him a sincere suggestion this time.

“Aaaah~ This really is the best feeling,” the black Scarlet Heaven Sword said in extreme comfort.

Song Shuhang nodded silently. He was suddenly no longer nervous.

Whoosh!

At this time, Senior White’s clone reappeared.

He was holding a booklet in his hand.

Song Shuhang vaguely saw the words ?Universe-Hiding Sleeve? written on the booklet.

“Hm, first this, then this... And then this hand seal, and then I do this.” Senior White’s clone waved his right hand around while looking at the booklet and making hand seals.

Senior White, are you learning the technique right here right now?

Looking and doing, there is nothing that I can’t do—By: White.

True Monarch White Crane took out his phone, and switched to his petite female human form. It then held the phone while lying on the ground and squirming around constantly as it recorded Senior White’s movements on video.

Squirming and writhing about, it eventually arrived right beside Song Shuhang’s feet.

Senior White Crane said softly, “Shuhang, hurry up and get out of the way.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

He and Sixteen stepped aside.

Then, he said softly, “Senior White Crane.”

True Monarch White Crane said, “I’m busy. Don’t bother me. This is the most important moment of my life, no interruptions are allowed.”

Song Shuhang silently closed his mouth, and stretched out his hand to do a zipping motion over his mouth—he wanted to tell Senior White Crane that its phone was not recording at the moment, but since Senior White Crane had told him to shut up, he had to shut up. As a junior, he respected his seniors very much.

“Almost got it,” said Senior White’s clone. After saying that, he threw the booklet over to Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang caught the booklet with a puzzled look on his face.

Senior White’s clone said, “I learned it already, it’s useless to me now.”

So because of that, you threw it over to me?

“Thank you, Senior White.” Song Shuhang happily opened the booklet.

Eighth Stage magical technique—Universe-Hiding Sleeve.

This magical technique could be cultivated by those who were at the Eighth Stage Profound Sage Realm.

The process of practicing this magical technique was very complicated. One needed to start learning right at the first realm [Touching the Laws] of the Profound Sage Realm.

I am the Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, the first Sage in a thousand years.

Afterward, Song Shuhang silently put away the booklet.

He was still self-aware. While he was the first Sage in 1,000 years, he was a fake. If he really wanted to learn this magical technique, he would have to first wait and cultivate his way up to the Eighth Stage before doing so.

Most importantly, he could not understand the contents.

Although the text in the booklet was written in Chinese, and Song Shuhang could read each character separately, when they were put together in the way that they appeared in the booklet, he could not understand anything it was saying.

He would need to spend some time thinking about it carefully and take advantage of the presence of Senior White, Senior Turtle, Pavilion Master Chu, and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, and get their help in order to understand the contents of the booklet.

Then, he could directly start practicing it when he reached the Eighth Stage.

Next to him, True Monarch White Crane was lying on the ground, staring at Song Shuhang with resentful eyes. At the same time, it was also staring intently at the booklet that Senior White had touched with his own hands.

??????

Senior White’s clone asked, “Fellow Daoist Eternal Fire, do you have clothes with wider sleeves?” The clothes on his clone’s body were not like the myriad changes magical clothing that his main body wore.

True Monarch Eternal Fire smiled, and said, “Fellow Daoist White, please wait.”

After a while.

A scholarly faction disciple came over with a brand-new set of scholarly robes, and handed it to Senior White.

True Monarch White Crane jumped up from the ground, and shouted, “Senior White, you want to change? Do you need any help?”

“No.” Senior White directly put the scholarly robe over his body.

Song Shuhang took out his phone, directed it at Senior White, and started recording a video. Senior White’s clone was about to cast Universe-Hiding Sleeve, so he definitely had to record this for later reviewing.

Yes, it was absolutely for learning.

Senior White’s clone made a hand seal with his left hand, and gently rolled his right sleeve against the Heavenly City Fragment.

A stream of light flashed, and the Heavenly City Fragment disappeared.

“It’s heavy. It also feels like the sleeve is going to get torn at any moment.” Senior White’s clone flicked the sleeve gently, and said, “Hm, when you cast this Universe Hiding Sleeve in the future, make sure to get a better robe or look for another magical technique to use in conjunction with Universe-Hiding Sleeve. Shuhang, open a gate.”

“Here you go.” Song Shuhang stretched out his hand, and opened an entrance to the Inner World.

Senior White trod on air, and entered the Inner World.

Song Shuhang stopped recording on his phone, and nodded with satisfaction. The scene where Senior White cast ?Universe-Hiding Sleeve? was recorded perfectly.

Then, he turned his head to look at True Monarch White Crane lying on the ground and smiled.

True Monarch White Crane asked, “What are you looking at?”

Song Shuhang put away his phone. “I just wanted to tell Senior White Crane that your phone hasn’t been recording this entire time. All this time, you’ve just been dangling your camera at Senior white.”

“!!!” True Monarch White Crane.

It quickly opened its phone and took a look.

After a moment, it froze.

The feathers on the wings on its back stood up one by one.

“Why didn’t you tell me sooner?” True Monarch White Crane lay on the ground, feeling completely drained.

Su Clan’s Sixteen covered her mouth and chuckled. “That’s because Senior White Crane told Shuhang not to bother you with anything.”

True Monarch White Crane burst into tears.

Ding~

At this time, its phone received a message.

[Tyrannical Song sent you a video.]

“???” True Monarch White Crane.

“It’s a video of Senior White casting ?Universe-Hiding Sleeve?.” Song Shuhang smiled slightly.

True Monarch White Crane asked, “Only a snippet? No full version?”

“Of course I have a full version.” Song Shuhang smiled honestly. At this time, he looked especially like the Almighty Merchant.

True Monarch White Crane gritted her teeth, and said, “Bah, even if I have to throw spirit stones into the toilet, I wouldn’t buy a video from you... Tsk, how much is it? You can state your price.”

“I’m just kidding.” Song Shuhang took Su Clan’s Sixteen’s little hand, stepped into the Inner World, and smiled as he said, “I sent you the full version I have.”

He did not have a video creation tool on his phone, and he did not know how to cut a video. So, the version he sent to True Monarch White Crane was naturally everything he had.

True Monarch White Crane jumped from the ground, patted the dust off its body, and rushed into the Inner World.

??????

Inside the Inner World.

The entrance to the Inner World opened by Song Shuhang this time led to the edge of the world.

They were in a large open space. This was new land that had been added to the Inner World after Song Shuhang purified the evil energy of the Netherworld from the patients from the Beast Realm a few days ago.

After the Inner World became full, it began slowly digesting everything it had consumed. Even now, the space was still expanding.

Senior White said, “I’m going to release the Heavenly City fragments.”

Song Shuhang nodded, and said, “No problem, just place it here.”

At the same time, the Inner World Assistant appeared beside Song Shuhang to assist him in handling the fragment. They had to avoid the Heavenly City Fragment directly merging with the Inner World after falling to the ground.

Senior White’s clone flung his sleeve. Then, a light flashed once again.

Boom!

The huge Heavenly City Fragment appeared out of thin air and fell with a boom.

At the moment when the Heavenly City Fragment, the Inner World began operating instinctively.

The soil in the open space turned into mud, wrapping around the base of the Heavenly City Fragment, and the Inner World began trying to integrate it with itself.

“Stop, stop.” The Inner World Assistant waved its little hand again and again, cooperating with Song Shuhang to stop the merging process.

After receiving Song Shuhang’s order, the Inner World finally stopped integrating the fragment.

The mud that wrapped around the base of the Heavenly City Fragment stopped, and did not take any further action.

However, the mud was still wriggling slightly... It was like it was licking the Heavenly City Fragment.

You can’t eat it, so you decide to just lick it instead?

Nevertheless, Song Shuhang let out a breath of relief.

As long as it didn’t consume it, just licking to relieve its craving was fine.

“It seems that little friend Shuhang’s small world does not repel the Heavenly City Fragments.” True Monarch Eternal Fire sighed—this meant that it was their scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus that was the one that had too particular an appetite.

“It’s especially non-repulsive of the fragment. It even looks as if little friend Shuhang’s Inner World is starving,” Sister White Dragon said with a smile.

Song Shuhang nodded, and said, “Senior White, can you take this Heavenly City Fragment first. Otherwise, I’m afraid that the Inner World might swallow it in one bite.”

Senior White reached out toward the Heavenly City Fragment and flung his sleeve again. The light flashed, and the fragment once again disappeared into his sleeve.

The mud on the ground of the Inner World reluctantly receded...

Sister White Dragon’s small claws scratched her face—she got the feeling that when the Heavenly City Fragment was taken back, it was missing something.

Did the mud that was licking the base of the Heavenly City Fragment lick a layer away? Or did it lick away something else?

Am I just hallucinating? Sister White Dragon silently thought to herself.

Compared with the scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus, Song Shuhang’s Inner World was not very picky with its food.

It was fine eating anything or integrating anything into itself.

Sister White Dragon saw all kinds of strange things in the Inner World. For example, inside the Inner World, there was a forest, which seemed to be a secret realm filled with murderous intent that had been cultivated by a powerful cultivator. But in the end, it had been moved into Song Shuhang’s Inner World and become a part of the Inner World.

There were also many different Heavenly City Fragments, which were sorted out by Inner World Assistant little by little and arranged harmoniously together, inside the Inner World.

It felt like as long as you could stuff it into the Inner World, it would be accepted by it.

Song Shuhang asked curiously, “By the way, Senior White, how big is your ❮Universe-Hiding Sleeve❯?”

“It seems to be related to one’s strength and realm. The stronger you are, the more things that the ❮Universe-Hiding Sleeve❯ can hold. If you have some understanding of spatial energy, it would be even easier for you to use,” Senior White’s clone said, and then added, “In my case, I’ve only just learned the magical technique... so not taking into account other factors, if I were to push myself, I should be able to handle a small hill?”

“Then, when Senior White becomes familiar with this technique, would you be able to contain a mountain?” Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

This ❮Universe-Hiding Sleeve❯ was both beautiful and ruthless. Song Shuhang could already imagine containing a mountain inside one’s sleeve, and then suddenly throwing it at anyone who caused him dissatisfaction

/

Senior Turtle easily read what Song Shuhang’s was thinking through the expressions on his face, and it laughed, and said, “It would be better to just refine something like a ‘Wild Mountain Seal’ magical treasure rather than use the ❮Universe-Hiding Sleeve❯ to keep a mountain to smash people with. As soon as you bring a magical treasure like that out, you can immediately make them feel as if a mountain was pressing down on them.”

Song Shuhang said, “Mountains are magnificent. If you don’t like the quality of the mountain, you can choose to keep a meteorite instead, and use that to press down on others.”

“Is it cool to hit someone with a meteorite?” Senior Turtle blinked. It suddenly realized that there really was a generation gap between itself and Song Shuhang.

It would much rather bring out its turtle shell and refine its shell into a seal, and then throw that.

“Shuhang, open the gate!” Senior White’s clone said. “My sleeve won’t be able to hold on much longer. I’ve only just learned the ❮Universe-Hiding Sleeve❯, and I’m not comfortable using it yet. I still have to simplify it into a style I’m more accustomed to using.”

Song Shuhang quickly opened an exit.

Senior White then immediately jumped out of Inner World.

The other fellow daoists and Song Shuhang followed after him.

Behind him, the Inner World Assistant kept smiling as it waved goodbye.

❄️❄️❄️

Boom!

Senior White flung his sleeve and released that Heavenly City Fragment.

“If only there was a magical technique to make a sleeve stronger.” Senior White’s clone raised his right hand and shook his sleeve lightly.

Song Shuhang blurted out, “Steel Sleeve Technique?”

“That sounds really weak,” Senior White said. “It would be much more logical for the ❮Universe-Hiding Sleeve❯ itself to have the effect of strengthening the sleeve. I’ll think about it when I have some time.”

Song Shuhang suggested, “Why don’t you just attach some formations to your sleeve to strengthen it?”

“Hm, I’ll do some research on it when I have the time.” Then, Senior White said to True Monarch Eternal Fire, “Fellow Daoist Eternal Fire, let’s go to the world of the golden lotus next. I want to see if there are any differences between the Heavenly City Fragments that the world of the golden lotus accepted and those that it rejected.”

“Okay, Fellow Daoists, please follow me.” True Monarch Eternal Fire nodded, and opened an entrance to the world of the golden lotus.

Senior White’s clone and the group of fellow daoists all entered the world of the golden lotus.

Song Shuhang and Sixteen went last.

Just as he and Sixteen were about to go in, a broad palm suddenly patted his shoulder. “Yo, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, we meet again.”

Whoosh!

Song Shuhang’s protective light of virtue, saber intent armor, the armor of the Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure, turtle shell... Over 10 kinds of defenses rose up around him in an instant.

When the owner of the large palm approached, Song Shuhang had not sensed them in the slightest—and the same went for the virtuous lamia and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword.

If the owner of the palm had not patted him on the back, and had stabbed him with a saber instead, then he would have absolutely not been prepared for it.

A direct stab to the back was the most deadly.

The owner of the palm chuckled, and said, “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song... Your defenses are quite special.”

Song Shuhang turned his head and saw the uncle with a common face standing behind him with a smile on his face.

While the other party could be said to have a common face, this middle-aged man was actually quite attractive: the more you looked at him, the better he would look... Though it would be a lot better if he wore his shoes correctly.

Song Shuhang frowned slightly—this middle-aged uncle looked familiar, and he felt as if he had seen him somewhere, and recently as well. However, his memory seemed to have been affected, and he just could not remember who they were.

This was very strange.

With his current memory as a Sixth Stage cultivator, under normal conditions, he should be able to clearly remember almost everything that he had seen.

The middle-aged man pointed at his face cheerfully, and said, “I was the driver.”

“...” Sister White Dragon.

This guy really went into the scholarly faction.

Song Shuhang asked cautiously, “So it’s Fellow Daoist. Why did you enter the White Cloud Academy?”

“Because I was originally a disciple of the scholarly faction.” The driver uncle smiled. “Actually, I had originally already been intending to head to White Cloud Academy, that was also why I took up your request for a driver.”

Sister White Dragon asked, “May I know Fellow Daoist’s daoist name?”

The driver uncle replied, “Hm, you can call me whatever you want. Anyway, after I tell you, you’d forget about it in mere moments.”

Song Shuhang thought for a moment. “Is it due to the Heaven’s Will’s small black room? Or is it the inheritance of a mysterious senior swordsman?”

“What inheritance of a mysterious swordsman?” The driver uncle looked confused.

“He is a reliable senior.” Song Shuhang patted his chest, and said, “He’s very kind, handsome, and powerful. He is a senior I respect very much.”

“...” Su Clan’s Sixteen.

The driver uncle said, “The state that I am in is similar to when one is inside the Heaven’s Will’s small black room. I’m temporarily able to move around and appear here by relying on a secret technique. I didn’t expect for Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song to know about the Heaven’s Will’s small black room. You’re indeed very knowledgeable.”

Song Shuhang said, “That’s because I was locked inside it in the past.”

The driver uncle looked at Song Shuhang in shock. “You managed to get out?”

Song Shuhang replied, “Well, I was locked inside for a short period of time, and then I was eventually released.”

The driver uncle sighed. “Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s life experience is incredibly rich.”

Sister White Dragon stared at the driver uncle thoughtfully.

“Is there something Fellow Daoist needs from me?” Song Shuhang asked—at the same time, he thought of the statue of the Tribulation Transcender that led the 13 Tribulation Transcenders of the scholarly faction and had its face rubbed off.

After all, this was too coincidental. It felt like the two were undoubtedly connected.

“Hm, I just suddenly had a thought. I came looking for Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song to verify it.” The driver uncle went to the Heavenly City Fragment and gently rubbed it. “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, can you take this Heavenly City Fragment into your Inner World, and then bring it out and move it into the world of the golden lotus?”

“Is there a difference?” Song Shuhang said curiously. “The world of the golden lotus repelled the Heavenly City Fragment. Even if it were forced into it, it would still be spat out, right?”

Unless the cause of the ‘nausea’ that the world of the golden lotus felt was discovered, it would be hard for them to find a solution for it.

“Well, it’s just a small test.” The driver uncle smiled, and said, “Of course, I won’t ask for Fellow Daoist to do it for free. I have a volume of this ❮Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment❯ which is a lost secret technique passed down in the Jingang Temple. How about it?”

Although this ‘giant palm’ was only a secret technique of the Third Stage, it was a secret technique that the outside world had lost, and was incredibly precious.

It was impossible to find this technique anywhere in the world.

If one wanted to learn the true supreme skills of the Jingang Temple, this giant palm was an important stepping stone to do so.

“A lost technique of the Jingang Temple?” Song Shuhang immediately thought of his own ❮Basic Buddhist Fist Technique❯ and Second Stage ❮Demon Subduing Buddhist Fist Technique❯.

But why was this lost secret technique of the Jingang Temple in the hands of someone from the scholarly faction?

“It’s because I happened to meet a great expert from the Jingang Temple recently. His style was something I myself yearned for. It seemed as if the muscles of the whole world had grown into him, and they were especially powerful. He and I exchanged some notes with one another, and I learned quite a bit from him. Eventually, I received this volume of the ❮Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment❯ from him.” The driver uncle possessed the face-reading technique, and was easily able to read Song Shuhang’s thoughts from his expressions.

“When this ❮Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment❯ is displayed, it can trigger a divine punishment-like thunder and lightning type of power. And at the same time, it can condense a giant buddhist palm. It is especially well-suited to Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song who is inclined to the lightning and fire attributes.” The driver uncle glanced at Song Shuhang.

He could see that Song Shuhang practiced three top-tier body-tempering techniques—among them was the ❮Scholarly Indestructible Body of the Buddha❯ from his scholarly faction, and another should be the ❮Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique❯. As for the last one, he could not pinpoint what it was.

Moreover, he had long known that Song Shuhang practiced the ❮Basic Buddhist Fist Technique❯ and the ❮Demon Subduing Buddhist Fist Technique❯, and that these two fist techniques from the Jingang Temple were the foundation of his cultivation.

“So, will Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song cooperate with me and carry out this small experiment?” The driver uncle smiled slightly.

Song Shuhang turned his head, and asked, “Sister White Dragon, what do you think?”

“Well, the cultivation technique is being delivered right to your door, and you don’t have to use much effort to get it, so why not?” Sister White Dragon replied while glancing at the driver uncle.

Could this guy be looking for a successor in the place of his friend from the Jingang Temple? But Song Shuhang’s cultivation is very complicated. If he plans on teaching him in order to have him become the successor of Jingang Temple, I’m afraid he would end up disappointed.

“Alright then, Senior, I’ll cooperate with you.” Song Shuhang stretched out his hand.

The driver uncle stretched out his left hand and shook Song Shuhang’s right hand. “To a happy cooperation.”

“...” Song Shuhang.

After letting go, Song Shuhang said, “I’m going to call Senior White out.”

If he wanted to put this Heavenly City Fragment into the Inner World, he would need the help of Senior White’s ❮Universe Hiding Sleeve❯.

“There’s no need to bother others. I’ll help you,” the driver uncle said. “It just so happens that I have a magical technique that I wanted to try out.”

After that, he stretched out and aimed it at the Heavenly City Fragment. “Buddhist Land in Palm!”

Another unique skill from the Buddhist system?

Song Shuhang stared at the Buddhist power that was coming from the hands of the driver uncle.

Could it be that this uncle from the scholarly faction is a spy from the Buddhist faction?

“Don’t look at me like that.” The driver uncle put away the Heavenly City Fragment and said softly, “If I were to use the scholarly faction’s secret technique, it would cause giant visions to appear in the air. At that time, the entire White Cloud Academy would begin shaking, and it would attract the attention of a lot of people. That isn’t in line with my low-key style.”

Song Shuhang suddenly discovered that his “facial expression library” was not rich enough for this occasion. He had no idea what facial expression he should display in front of the driver uncle after hearing what he just said.

“Come on, open the gate. I’ll send this Heavenly City Fragment to your world.” The uncle driver said while his hand glowed with the power of the Buddhist Land in Palm.

In the miniature Buddhist Land, there were bursts of Buddhist sounds, making it appear like a miniature version of the Western Paradise of the Buddha Amitabha.

“Actually, fellow daoist, when you use these Buddhist abilities, the visual effects are still quite large,” Song Shuhang said as he opened an entrance to the Inner World.

“Nah, this level is still very small.” The driver uncle jumped lightly and entered the Inner World.

Song Shuhang and Su Clan’s Sixteen followed right after him.

They landed at the same open space where Senior White’s clone had placed the Heavenly City Fragment earlier.

Song Shuhang asked, “Fellow daoist, are you going to be placing down the Heavenly City Fragment?”

The driver uncle waved his hand gently and released the Heavenly City Fragment.

Song Shuhang looked at the ground.

The soil of the Inner World turned into mud again, wrapping around the base of the Heavenly City Fragment. As it wrapped around the base of the fragment, it began to lick it.

But this time, after a few licks, the mud shrank back.

[Huh?] Song Shuhang found himself rather curious when he saw this.

The Inner World was clearly enthusiastically licking it just a few moments ago, why did it suddenly lose interest?

This reminded Song Shuhang of some memories from his childhood when he ate homemade popsicles. Whenever he had those flavored popsicles, he would place as much of them as he could inside his mouth and begin sucking out all the sweet flavoring from them... Afterward, what would be left was nothing more than ice, ice that was bland and tasteless.

Could it be that this Heavenly City Fragment had also become tasteless, so the Inner World no longer felt like licking it?

At this time, the driver uncle suddenly said, “Speaking of which, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song. Your vigilance is very lacking.”

Song Shuhang looked puzzled. “Huh?”

“This small world should be your trump card, right?” said the driver uncle. Normally, small worlds like the Inner World were the life-saving trump card of a cultivator.

Song Shuhang nodded—theoretically speaking, it was indeed a trump card of his. However, he did not really get to use it as such most of the time.

“Since it’s a life-saving trump card, how can you let me, a person you’ve barely met, enter it so easily?” the driver uncle said seriously. “If I had malicious intentions, I could have destroyed this small world of yours, causing you to lose a trump card. Don’t underestimate the destructive ability of cultivators, especially cultivators who have grasped the laws of space, it isn’t difficult for such people to break a small world like this one. In the future, make sure to not just let people into your world so casually. This small world of yours is very precious.”

Song Shuhang nodded. “Thank you for the reminder, fellow daoist.”

At the same time, he quietly glanced at Sixteen. Elder Sister White Dragon was still inside her body.

Actually, Song Shuhang had initially been very cautious and strict with letting others enter his Inner World. Other than a couple of seniors who he considered reliable, he did not disclose information about his small world to anyone. He completely regarded the Inner World as his life-saving trump card.

Then one day, the Inner World and Senior White Two’s world of the black lotus became linked, becoming friends of sorts.

A while after that, Song Shuhang’s thoughts about the Inner World changed.

Now, if there was an enemy that was too strong for Song Shuhang to defeat, he would willingly welcome them into his Inner World.

After all, as long as they entered the Inner World, it would be equivalent to jumping right where Senior White Two was.

Moreover, it was Senior White Two’s real body that resided there, not just the projection that he used to walk around the main world.

Song Shuhang was extremely confident in the strength that the ruler of the Netherworld’s real body possessed.

Of course, the driver uncle was in no way wrong with what he said, as there was nothing wrong with being cautious.

After all, there would still be a delay between the enemy jumping in and Senior White Two making a move.

In the past, the Inner World was a mess, and there were no precious things stored inside it, so even if a part of it got destroyed, Song Shuhang would not have felt that bad.

But now, the Inner World was full of all kinds of treasures, and he was cultivating and nurturing all kinds of spirit plants and spirit beasts inside it.

All of these things were very valuable.

It was necessary to take some protective measures in the Inner World—the defense did not need to last all that long; as long as it could last until Senior White Two made a move and prevented the Inner World from being destroyed, it would be enough.

Several ideas quickly emerged in Song Shuhang’s mind.

He looked up at the “sky” of the Inner World. The virtuous lamia was still weaving the Inner World’s Virtuous Dragon Network. When this large network eventually became as complete as the Dragon Network, the Inner World Assistant could begin operating the Inner World’s power like the Dragon Network Assistant, and use that to defend the Inner World.

The Inner World Assistant was originally a replica of the Dragon Network Assistant, so the defensive measures that the Dragon Network Assistant possessed had also been replicated into the Inner World Assistant’s system.

In addition, there were several Ancient Heavenly City Fragments in the Inner World. Those that were still relatively complete had their own defensive measures—such as the Palace of Winter, the Virtuous Palace, the Thirty-Three Divine Beast Department’s Toilet, the Ancient Heavenly City’s Canteen No. 111, and a couple of other ones.

In the era of the Ancient Heavenly City, there had to be a complete defense system that connected the various palaces together. If they were able to refer to that and have the fragments cooperate with the Inner World Assistant, then they would be able to imitate the defense system from the Heavenly City’s era.

Finally, there was also Pavilion Master Chu, who was bored out of her mind and blowing bubbles in the Living Spring. If not, he could ask her for some advice on how to set up defenses and protect the Inner World. If Pavilion Master Chu was interested and willing to join the defense system of the Inner World, it would be even better.

Having an Immortal be part of the defense system would be especially reassuring.

They could also move a couple of dangerous areas inside the Inner World such as the Death Forest that Senior White had transferred in.

At that time, if he were just facing some weaker enemies, Song Shuhang would not even need to waste his time. He could simply grab them all and throw them into these areas.

Inspiration kept on overflowing in Song Shuhang’s mind.

He suddenly discovered that his Inner World was full of potential.

As long as he could think of ways to use the things inside it, the potential of the Inner World was humongous.

“Thank you for the reminder, fellow daoist.” Song Shuhang thanked the driver uncle again.

The driver uncle went silent for a few moments before saying, “I’m getting the feeling that Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song is thinking of something extremely dangerous.”

Song Shuhang said, “I am a peaceful person, the future successor of the motherland.”

The driver uncle: “???”

There really was a generation gap between him and Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.

Even though they were chatting face to face, they did not seem to be on the same page.

[Shuhang, Sixteen, where did you two go? Why haven’t you come in yet?] At this moment, the voice of Senior White sounded in the ears of Song Shuhang and Sixteen.

“Senior White just called,” Song Shuhang said. “We should head over to the world of the golden lotus.”

The driver uncle nodded and said, “Let’s go.”

??????

At the entrance of the scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus.

Song Shuhang and Sixteen headed toward the entrance, but the driver uncle did not follow.

Sixteen turned her head curiously and found the uncle waving at her and Shuhang.

Song Shuhang asked, “Fellow daoist, are you not coming in?”

The driver uncle said, “I have to keep a low-profile. You guys go on. When you’re in there, ask Sage White how to take out the Heavenly City Fragment. I’ll be waiting for the results of fellow daoist’s experiment from here.”

“Fellow daoist, you won’t suddenly disappear on us again, right?” Song Shuhang said—he still hadn’t gotten the promised ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment?.

The driver uncle, who was proficient in reading facial expressions, was immediately able to decipher what was in Song Shuhang’s mind. He stretched out his hand and took out a thick book and threw it at Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang opened it and saw that it was indeed in the style of the Jingang Temple, and there were pictures of a muscular monk in the book. Every few pages, there would also be cultivation chants attached.

The driver uncle said, “This ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? is similar to a flipbook. When you hold this book and flip through it quickly, you will find that the content of this book seems to come alive and start moving.”

Song Shuhang replied, “I see.”

He held the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? firmly in his hand and began flipping through the book. Indeed, the pictures in the book looked as if they had come alive.

“When the time comes, fellow daoist, you can first write down the cultivation chants and then just start flipping through them quickly. After you chant them a few more times, you can start to learn the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment?. It’s very simple and practical. Back then, the Jingang Temple promoted having their disciples learn on their own, allowing them to go at their own pace. Unfortunately, the Jingang Temple’s inheritance...” The driver uncle said regretfully.

“Thank you, fellow daoist.” Song Shuhang put away the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment?. After he mastered this move, he would be able to stretch out his hand and create a giant palm mixed with the power of divine lightning. It sounded especially cool and powerful.

Moreover, when he thought of the combination of Buddha’s Palm and Divine Punishment’s Lightning, Song Shuhang immediately thought of the city-scale Lightning Palm in the Ninth Stage heavenly tribulation. He felt that the two had quite a few similarities.

Song Shuhang and Sixteen turned around and entered the world of the golden lotus.

The driver uncle nervously stood guard outside the Inner World, waiting for Song Shuhang to come out.

He said softly, “I hope the experiment is successful.”

If the experiment was successful, all of the Heavenly City Fragments in the scholarly faction’s possession could be transferred into the world of the golden lotus in one go. In this way, it would be possible to delay the Heavenly Emperor in rebuilding the Heavenly City. Consequently, that would cause the current Wielder of the Will to continue to remain in an incomplete state.

In addition, if the scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus were to acquire many Ancient Heavenly City Fragments and expand through them, that would be very beneficial for its future development...

Inside the world of the golden lotus.

Song Shuhang and Sixteen locked onto Senior White’s aura and quickly rejoined with the rest of the seniors.

“Yo, Shuhang, where did you go with little Sixteen just now?” True Monarch White Crane leisurely looked at Song Shuhang with a teacup in hand. It was not able to help with the Heavenly City Fragments, so it was standing by the side idly.

Song Shuhang said, “We met a fellow daoist at the entrance and we chatted for a bit.”

However, because of that effect similar to that of the Wielder’s small black room, after he and Sixteen entered the world of the golden lotus, they had already forgotten what the driver uncle looked like.

It was only the existence of the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? in his magical bracelet that proved to Song Shuhang that his previous experience was real.

At this time, Senior White was walking in the air, observing a nine-layered pagoda.

This pagoda and the giant stone platform below were both fragments of the Ancient Heavenly City. These two were the only fragments that they were able to smoothly transfer into the world of the golden lotus.

“Come here, Shuhang. Do you notice anything different between the Heavenly City Fragments here and outside?” Senior White spoke to Song Shuhang while seemingly having already found something.

Song Shuhang leaned over and reached out to touch the pagoda.

He said doubtfully while touching the pagoda, “Eh? Why do I feel like there’s something about this pagoda that’s missing compared to the other Ancient Heavenly City Fragments?”

Senior White nodded and said, “Yeah, I felt the same.”

The eyes of True Monarch Eternal Fire lit up. Have Senior White and little friend Shuhang figured out something?

Sister White Dragon also came out and said, “There is indeed something amiss with this pagoda.”

In short, this pagoda was giving her the same feeling as that fragment that had been transferred into Song Shuhang’s Inner World and got licked repeatedly.

“Let me try something and see what exactly might be different with it.” Song Shuhang willed it, and the fingertips of the glove of the Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Combined Magical Treasure on his hand partially receded, allowing his bare fingertips to touch the pagoda.

At the same time, his body scattered as he entered his pseudo-eternity smoke form.

The price required to appraise an Ancient Heavenly City Fragment would definitely be high as it was something from a long time ago. As such, Song Shuhang had already mentally prepared himself.

Sister White Dragon said, “Wait, Shuhang. Before you use your strange appraisal technique, let me tell you some information about this pagoda so that the price you have to pay can be decreased a bit.”

She knew that Song Shuhang had an appraisal technique that would cause him to start spewing blood and bring him mental pain ten times as intense as what he would feel physically. However, the more he knew about the object that he was appraising, the less the appraisal’s cost would be.

Sister White Dragon used to be the ancestral golden dragon of the Heavenly City, so she knew about most of the structures in the Heavenly City. She was especially familiar with this pagoda, which could be seen all over the Heavenly City.

But... She was too late.

When Sister White Dragon spoke, Song Shuhang had already cast the secret appraisal technique and began paying the price.

Large clouds of smoke began scattering out of his body and flowing upwards. A small, black mushroom-shaped cloud soon formed above his head.

Song Shuhang said with a trembling voice, “S-Sister White Dragon, next time, if possible, please remind me earlier...”

As expected, the pain that came with appraising an Ancient Heavenly City Fragment was extremely high. His body was trembling from the pain, and the only thing he could do at this moment was enduring as best as he could.

Sister White Dragon: “...”

Who would think that despite you knowing how painful using that technique is, you wouldn’t even have second thoughts when using it? It honestly even seems like you enjoy using this magical technique!

In the meantime, information on the pagoda had already been fed back into Song Shuhang’s mind.

[A dilapidated Thousand Mile Pagoda. This pagoda was used by the Ancient Heavenly City to monitor foreign foes remotely. It was an integral part of the Heavenly City’s defense system. A total of 80,000 Thousand Mile Pagodas were distributed all over the Ancient Heavenly City to provide absolute security for the city. The prototype of the Thousand Mile Pagoda was the Ten Thousand Mile Sensing Pagoda designed by the ancestral golden dragon. This version was mass-produced with some of its functions taken off. Due to its connection with the Ancient Heavenly City having been cut off, as the years passed, it lost the nourishment of the Heavenly City and turned into an ordinary Heavenly City Fragment.]

Song Shuhang: “...”

He turned his head to look at Sister White Dragon.

As he looked at her at this time, he found her to be full of historical charm.

The big shots around him were all extremely old, and they would quite often inadvertently display the brilliance of their past.

The secret technique that Senior Turtle had copied down, the Heavenly City Fragment from the Almighty Merchant, which turned out to be the old home of the virtuous lamia, and also that ancient tomb he ventured into, which had been created by Senior Seventh Cultivator of True Virtue and was part of the inheritance of the Cultivators of True Virtue...

Now, the very designer of the Ancient Heavenly City Fragment that he had just appraised turned out to be right beside him.

He could only offer his respect to Sister White Dragon.

Song Shuhang asked, “Sister White Dragon, is it expensive to manufacture Thousand Mile Pagodas like this one?”

He was preparing to create a watertight defense in his Inner World. This Thousand Mile Pagoda had been an integral part of the Ancient Heavenly City’s defense system, and the original designer was right by his side. It would be a crime to waste such a good opportunity to make use of what he had available to him.

“No, manufacturing these doesn’t cost that much,” Sister White Dragon said. “Each pagoda only needs 10 Ninth Stage spirit stones at most in order to be manufactured.”

Song Shuhang’s whole body suddenly began trembling. “Ten... Ten Ninth Stage spirit stones?”

He began converting the value in his mind. Ten Ninth Stage spirit stones were equal to 100 Eighth Stage spirit stones, 1000 Seventh Stage spirit stones, 10,000 Sixth Stage spirit stones, or 100,000 Fifth Stage spirit stones.

Spirit stones of the Fifth Stage were the most used ones in the world of cultivation.

100,000 Fifth Stage spirit stones, this was an enormous amount of spirit stones that Song Shuhang could not even imagine having.

Other than the time when he borrowed a spatial magical treasure filled with spirit stones from Senior White, Song Shuhang had never had such a large amount of spirit stones.

Song Shuhang asked, “Are there any discounts?”

Sister White Dragon said calmly, “That’s just the price of the raw materials.”

Song Shuhang said, “I will try my best to make money.”

“You can do it!” Sister White Dragon encouraged. It was a good thing for a man to want to make money. As long as he did not intend to do anything illegal or immoral, it was worth encouraging them.

True Monarch White Crane approached and said, “This pagoda is called ‘Thousand Mile Pagoda’?”

Song Shuhang nodded and began recounting the information he got from the appraisal.

After listening, True Monarch Eternal Fire thought for a moment and said, “That is to say, the difference between this Thousand Mile Pagoda and the fragments outside is that it has lost its connection with the original Heavenly City and something has disappeared from it with the passage of time. Is that why the world of the golden lotus doesn’t reject it and allows it to merge with itself?”

But then what is that thing that has disappeared from it with the passage of time?

“I have a suggestion,” Sister White Dragon said. “How about we bring out that Heavenly City Fragment into the world of the golden lotus and see if it accepts it?”

Senior White nodded. “I agree.”

Apparently, both he and Sister White Dragon were aware of certain details and had made the same speculation.

“I almost forgot about that,” said Song Shuhang hurriedly. “That Heavenly City Fragment is in my Inner World. When Sixteen and I were pulled aside by that big shot fellow daoist, the other party told me to bring a Heavenly City Fragment into my Inner World before testing out if it would be accepted by the world of the golden lotus.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire asked with a frown, “Who’s this big shot you’re talking about?”

Song Shuhang rubbed his eyebrows. “I can’t remember... My memory has been affected.”

“It was the man who drove us here,” Sister White Dragon said slowly. “My memory has also been affected. It seems that that man is under an effect similar to that of the Wielder’s small black room.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire’s heart thumped. When he heard this, he immediately thought of the leader of the 13 Tribulation Transcenders of the scholarly faction.

Song Shuhang said, “Senior White, let’s work together and move the Heavenly City Fragment out first.”

Senior White’s clone said, ??”Alright.”

“Shuhang, open sesame!” The virtuous lamia jumped out all of a sudden, posing like a white crane with its wings spread out behind Song Shuhang—she shouted “Shuhang” using the voice of Senior White, and the words “Open Sesame” using what she heard from a TV segment.

The virtuous lamia was becoming better and better at spouting random lines.

Immediately afterward, Fairy Creation appeared. As she was one step late and had been bested, she stomped her feet in anger. “Song~ Stupid~ Stupid!”

Song Shuhang: “...”

They’ve even begun snatching Senior White’s lines?

Senior White reached out and pinched his chin, feeling amused. “That’s right, open sesame!”

Song Shuhang did not know whether to laugh or cry. Nevertheless, he opened the Inner World.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword suggested, “Fairy, at this time, you should try and imitate the rumbling sound of the opening of a stone gate.”

The virtuous lamia was taken aback for a moment. She had only ever snatched other people’s lines, but she had never recorded the sound effects of a door opening.

“Rumble~ Rumble~” Fairy Creation immediately began manually dubbing the sound.

Although it wasn’t exactly the same, it was better than nothing.

Song Shuhang stretched out his hands and grabbed the two fairies, stuffing them back in his body.

Senior White jumped into the Inner World, and then jumped out again a moment later.

With a flick of his sleeve, the Heavenly City Fragment was transferred out and landed in an open space in the world of the golden lotus.

The Heavenly City Fragment lay where it was quietly.

This time, the world of the golden lotus did not reject it.

Song Shuhang checked the world of the golden lotus through the Inner World and sensed that it no longer felt nauseous.

True Monarch Eternal Fire asked, “Huh? Why did it work this time?”

Just what exactly was the problem?

This Heavenly City Fragment had only stayed in Song Shuhang’s Inner World for a while, but after being transferred out, it suddenly became able to stay in the world of the golden lotus.

Could it be that little friend Shuhang’s Inner World has an authentication function that validates a Heavenly City Fragment, allowing it to be taken in by the world of the golden lotus?

Senior White said, “It’s exactly as I thought.”

Sister White Dragon nodded and added, “When the Heavenly City Fragment was in Shuhang’s Inner World, it seemed to have lost something. And that something was what caused the world of the golden lotus to reject it... After that something was lost, the world of the golden lotus no longer rejected the Heavenly City Fragment in question.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire looked at Song Shuhang in puzzlement.

“Senior, don’t look at me.” Song Shuhang gestured with his hand. “I don’t know anything.”

“Little friend Shuhang, how about we work together?” said True Monarch Eternal Fire.

If it was the leader of the 13 Tribulation Transcenders who had requested Song Shuhang’s help in carrying out the experiment, then the scholarly faction should cooperate with him.

Anyhow, the scholarly faction needed to expand the world of the golden lotus with new Heavenly City Fragments. Even if certain properties were lost during the transfer, the ability of the Heavenly City Fragments to expand the world of the golden lotus did not disappear, and that was enough for them.

“Sure, I have no problem with that,” Song Shuhang said sincerely. “However, according to Sister White Dragon, when the Ancient Heavenly City Fragments are transferred into my Inner World, something is ‘licked away’ from them. We don’t know if that thing might be precious... Seniors, you know, I really can’t afford to lose money.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire laughed.

He knew that Song Shuhang was short of spirit stones recently, so he quickly understood what he was worried about.

True Monarch Eternal Fire said, “We’re fine with losing whatever it is that is licked away.”

Similar to Song Shuhang’s Inner World, if the world of the golden lotus wanted to grow, it would need to absorb pure energy.

Song Shuhang’s Inner World had a good appetite. Whether it was spirit stones or evil energy of the Netherworld—as long as it was pure energy—it was generally open to consuming it and digesting it.

As for the world of the golden lotus, it had a much worse appetite, and it would only absorb evil demons of the Netherworld. As such, the scholarly faction had to hunt demons and use their corpses to nurture the world of the golden lotus.

But this process was very slow. Moreover, evil demons were not wild beasts, and they could even counterattack and hunt down scholarly disciples. It could be said that the expansion of every inch of the scholarly faction’s world of the golden lotus was paid with the blood and lives of the disciples of the scholarly faction.

Because of this, True Monarch Eternal Fire was ecstatic when he learned about the Ancient Heavenly City Fragments from Song Shuhang—the Ancient heavenly City Fragments were very special, when they were forcibly stuffed into the Inner World or the world of the golden lotus, they could be placed at the edge of the small world to expand it.

What the scholarly faction needed at this moment was the ability of the Heavenly City Fragments to expand the area of ??the world of the golden lotus.

Moreover, other than that “something” that was licked away, none of the other properties of the Heavenly City Fragments would go away.

Senior White’s clone reminded, “Fellow Daoist Eternal Fire, how about you first converse with the members of the other academies of the scholarly faction? It would help avoid conflicts arising in the future.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire smiled slightly. He then stretched out his hand and showed a Scholarly Rune—this Scholarly Rune was a rune left by the Scholarly Sage, and it was similar to the Imperial Rune of the Heavenly Emperor.

After several calamities, there were no longer that many Scholarly Runes that had been personally written by the Scholarly Sage in the scholarly faction. Nowadays, they were often used as important keepsakes.

“In fact, before asking little friend Song Shuhang to come over to help, the leaders of the other academies have already given me the greatest authority on the matter concerning the Ancient Heavenly City Fragments and the world of the golden lotus,” explained True Monarch Eternal Fire.

True Monarch Eternal Fire added, “Also, if little friend Shuhang is short of spirit stones, how about I convert your help in this matter into spirit stones?”

The number of Ancient Heavenly City Fragments that the scholarly faction had acquired was quite large, and it would take several days to move all of them.

Hard work was inevitable.

Originally, True Monarch Eternal Fire was still thinking about what treasure would be suitable to reward Song Shuhang with for his hard work... But now, it seemed that something as ordinary as spirit stones was the best option.

“I always had a liking for ordinary things.” Senior Eternal Fire’s words were music to Song Shuhang’s ears.

“What about you, Fellow Daoist White? Is there anything you want?” True Monarch Eternal Fire turned to look at Senior White’s clone.

During the whole process, Senior White would need to provide assistance in many places.

Eternal Fire had the greatest authority in handling this matter concerning the world of the golden lotus. With that being the case, within the scope of his authority, he would naturally prepare the best gifts he could for his friends.

Senior White’s clone thought for a long time, but he found that he really was not lacking anything.

“Then just give me one of the Heavenly City Fragments,” Senior White said. When he got it, he could cut it up and play with it, and when he got tired of it, he could simply throw it into Song Shuhang’s Inner World.

True Monarch Eternal Fire said, “No problem. If Fellow Daoist White sees any fragment that he likes during the moving process, you can feel free to take it no matter how big or small it is.”

Senior White said solemnly, “Then I’ll pick the biggest one.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire asked, “Absolutely no problem. Sixteen, what about you? What do you want for your hard work?”

Su Clan’s Sixteen looked puzzled. “I have a share too?”

Sister White Dragon smiled slightly. “It seems that you have good eyes. Alright, if there is anything that requires my assistance, I will be sure to help you out. Sixteen, just go ahead and choose something you like.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen said, “Then... I also want a Heavenly City Fragment.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire said, “It’s a deal then. I’ll have someone transfer the Heavenly City Fragments over. When they get here, we can begin with the transplanting and get things done.”

“Huh? What about me? What about me?” True Monarch White Crane on the side could not help but say out loud, “Actually, I can also help.”

True Monarch Eternal Fire laughed and said, “Fellow Daoist White Crane, aren’t you just here as a mascot?”

True Monarch White Crane: “...”

Are you trying to test me? Believe it or not, I might just peck at you if you push too hard! Don’t think that you can bully me all you want just because you’re more well-read than I am!

??????

When Song Shuhang and the seniors exited the world of the golden lotus, they found that the fellow daoist whose face they could not remember had disappeared—of course, it was also possible that they had just mixed with the crowd.

Under the command of True Monarch Eternal Fire, the scholarly faction began to use various techniques to move the fragments.

Seeing this scene, the driver uncle did not have to come up to Song Shuhang and ask him about the results of the experiment. After all, the results were right in front of him.

Song Shuhang and Senior White’s clone stood at the entrance of the world of the golden lotus.

The disciples of the scholarly faction began to carry the fragments according to their sizes, starting with the smallest ones.

The small fragments could be directly loaded into Song Shuhang’s Inner World through Senior White’s Universe Hiding Sleeve.

After being licked by the Inner World and getting “authenticated,” the fragment would be sent straight into the world of the golden lotus by Senior White.

The disciples of the scholarly faction would then take the fragment and bring it to the edge of the small world, forcibly expanding the space inside the world of the golden lotus.

When it came to fragments that were too large, the scholarly faction had their own methods to compress their size.

They would first compress these Heavenly City Fragments to a suitable size and allow them to enter Song Shuhang’s Inner World through Senior White’s Universe Hiding Sleeve and repeat the steps above.

The whole process was as smooth as an assembly line.

With everyone’s teamwork getting better, the efficiency of transporting the Heavenly City Fragments also became higher and higher.

Every time a Heavenly City Fragment was authenticated, it was quickly accepted by the world of the golden lotus, becoming a part of it.

A gentle smile appeared on True Monarch Eternal Fire’s face.

Now, the only thing to worry about is Fellow Daoist White...

It was unknown how long Senior White would bear to perform these repetitive and boring actions. If he suddenly became bored...

True Monarch Eternal Fire could only hope for Senior White’s interest to last much longer.

But at the same time, True Monarch Eternal Fire felt a faint sense of guilt—letting Fellow Daoist White keep repeating such boring and repetitive actions felt like a huge waste.

??????

This Senior White’s clone was much more patient than True Monarch Eternal Fire had expected.

The sun set, and the moon rose.

The moon set, and the sun rose.

The morning had arrived.

It was now Wednesday, November 20.

Senior White repeated the boring actions all day long.

True Monarch White Crane asked, “Do you want to take a break?”

Senior White replied, “No, I’m fine.”

Senior White seemed to be having fun carrying the Heavenly City Fragments between the Inner World and the world of the golden lotus.

Song Shuhang squatted silently at the entrance of the world of the golden lotus, holding the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? in his hand and flipping through it over and over again. He was taking this time to learn the giant palm technique.

In the process of moving the Heavenly City Fragments, his role was only to open the Inner World... Besides that, there was nothing else for him to do.

As the Inner World kept licking the Heavenly City Fragments, it underwent a change—the entrance became bigger!

Moreover, it became able to digest the evil energy of the Netherworld much quicker.

The entire Inner World had become more solid. As it was stuffed with more and more Heavenly City Fragments, a certain resonance was created between them and the Inner World.

“Hm, I’m getting more and more clues.” At this time, Senior White’s clone nodded in satisfaction.

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “What did Senior White find?”

Senior White flipped his sleeve lightly and replied, “I’m trying to improve the Universe Hiding Sleeve. From yesterday to now, I improved it 19 times.”

Song Shuhang stared at Senior White with wide eyes, and then he looked down at the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? in his hand that he could barely understand.

He suddenly felt like he was being crushed by Senior White’s talent.

Senior White said, “Also, while improving the Universe Hiding Sleeve and jumping between the two small worlds, I had a new idea for a magical technique.”

After saying that, he pressed his left hand on a Heavenly City Fragment that had not been compressed, and branded a rune onto it.

Suddenly the huge Heavenly City Fragment was stored in his sleeve.

With a rumble, the Heavenly City Fragment that was stored inside Senior White’s left sleeve was directly transferred into Song Shuhang’s Inner World through his right sleeve.

“There should still be some more space for improvement,” Senior White said. “Shuhang, lend me your copy of the ?Universe Hiding Sleeve?. I’ll modify it for you.”

Song Shuhang said, “Senior White, you’re truly amazing.”

“Ah... I forgot to pay attention to that.” He was so invested in improving the technique that he forgot to pick a fragment.

Song Shuhang looked up at the fragment.

It had words of the ancient era written on it.

Sister White Dragon said, “Inner Demon Cave.”

“Inner Demon Cave? Is it a Heavenly City Fragment related to inner demons?” Song Shuhang quickly put away the book with the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment?.

Recently, he had been paying attention to anything related to inner demons.

“It might just have the same pronunciation, and it may not be the kind of inner demon you are thinking about,” said the black Scarlet Heaven Sword. Song Shuhang had become obsessed with getting an inner demon to use as an ingredient, causing it to feel rather anxious.

When his hand was halfway to the fragment, he suddenly stopped.

Song Shuhang turned his head and looked back. “Sister White Dragon, do you have any information about this Inner Demon Cave that you can tell me?”

Human beings were intelligent creatures, and they would usually avoid making the same mistake twice

I’ve already been cheated once because I lacked critical information. This time, I will make better use of my resources and won’t make the same mistake!

Sister White Dragon stretched out her small claws and scratched her face. “I honestly don’t have any impression of the Inner Demon Cave. That’s actually quite strange.”

She was the Ancestral Golden Dragon, and she had impressions of all the famous palaces and buildings across the Heavenly City. She felt like her friends should have mentioned such a place at least once if it had existed.

However, she could not remember any places called “Inner Demon Cave.”

But it was certain that this place was a Heavenly City Fragment.

Sister White Dragon guessed, “It’s possible that a member of the Heavenly City secretly created it, or perhaps the fragments of the Ancient Heavenly City were reprocessed after its collapse.”

“I’ll try appraising it then,” Song Shuhang said—although the Heavenly City Fragment that Senior White randomly selected was not the largest piece, it seemed to be very precious and fit right in with Senior White’s type of stuff.

Song Shuhang took a deep breath and prepared to endure the pain.

His body transformed into smoke, and he stretched out his hand, placing it on the Heavenly City Fragment.

Then, he activated the secret appraisal technique!

The price for the appraisal this time was extremely heavy. If Shuhang had not transformed into his smoky form, the consequences would have been unimaginable.

The scattering of my smoke body was so that I could relieve the pain, and at the same time forcibly end the secret appraisal technique. Sigh~ This thing has a lot of history. I feel that even if I’m willing to pay a serious price, I would not be able to appraise all of its information.”
