It was a great idea, actually.

The price paid by Song Shuhang after performing the secret appraisal technique directly affected his mind and soul.

At the same time, the comfortable and refreshing feeling that was brought by the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? not only acted on the body, but also on the mind and soul.

Perhaps the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? could really alleviate the effects of Song Shuhang’s secret appraisal technique.

Of course, the premise was that Song Shuhang could physically receive the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique?.

“Ahhhh~” A cry of absolute pain resounded in the area; there was no trace of comfort in it.

[Inner Demon Cave: In the ancient era, the Heavenly Emperor studied inner demons in this secret laboratory. As the secret appraisal technique was forcibly interrupted by Song Shuhang himself, the information from the appraisal was incomplete.

In the ancient era, the Heavenly Emperor had studied inner demons. It was very likely that there had been some results to her research as it could be inferred from Soft Feather.

Not long ago, Soft Feather started thinking of extracting her inner demon and making a clone out of it.

According to Soft Feather’s own words, when she was studying inner demons, she obtained a lot of useful information from her ghost spirit. It was with the information she received that she was able to come up with the Inner Demon Clone Technique.

As her ghost spirit had been forcibly borrowed by the Heavenly Emperor, it meant that the information about inner demons that she received most likely came from the Heavenly Emperor.

He had paid such a steep price for appraising it, so there were definitely more secrets to it if he could appraise it further.

Song Shuhang said, “Maybe there are still inner demons hidden inside. Those aged inner demons would definitely taste great.”

After all, fine wine gets better with age.

Pavilion Master Chu’s long hair twisted gracefully above Song Shuhang’s head, swaying with the wind.

She continued, “In addition to being tastier, older things are generally more powerful.”

Behind Song Shuhang, Senior White’s clone’s hands started to get restless. The clone’s eyes were fixed on the long strand of hair swaying above Song Shuhang’s head, and it looked like he really wanted to pluck it.

The scholarly faction and the evil demons of the Netherworld were archenemies, so the two sides constantly hunted and monitored each other.

But this evil demon directly opened a spatial passage that led to the heart of the scholarly faction... Evidently, they were overflowing with confidence. If it was not a momentary lapse of judgment, did it mean that they were sure that they could leave intact?

Its effects were outstanding.

The current scholarly faction was no longer the same as the one during the era of the Scholarly Sage, when it could suppress the entire universe.

The scholarly faction had gone through numerous calamities. Most of the scholarly faction’s 13 Tribulation Transcenders had been killed or were severely injured, and many of its elite disciples had died prematurely, resulting in the emergence of a serious level of power disparity among different generations.

At present, the scholarly faction did not even have the strength to confront this demonic bear. At most, they could resort to using one of the treasures left behind by the Scholarly Sage to resist it.

He had received news from his companions that the survivors of the Ancient Heavenly City were eyeing the fragments in the hands of the scholarly faction and wanted to retrieve them.

Do you really think that my scholarly faction is so weak that it can be bullied by the likes of you? Do you really think that anybody can just step on the scholarly faction?

Sword light flashed, and he directly used his spatial powers to appear beside the demonic bear and attack.

Rumble~

Pain, madness, despair, and unwillingness emerged from the steel giant as it roared toward the sky.

On the top of the giant’s head, seven-meter-long hair came down like a cloak... It was Pavilion Master Chu’s long hair, ready to attack at any moment.

Is this a new move learned by the steel giant?

Pavilion Master Chu’s long hair gathered into a bundle, forming something that resembled a long spear. Then, it stabbed right at the giant demonic bear, breaking through its physical defense and making a hole in its body.

It also had a helper.

Moreover, this time it had directly broken into the heart of the scholarly faction in order to test the loyalty of this new helper.

Small feet that were as white as snow stepped out of the spatial gate. The feet had graceful curves and looked stunning, the toes painted with pink nail polish.

Immediately afterward, a girl in a black dress stepped out of the spatial gate. “Huh... Did I just hear someone say they want to eat me?”

This passage was also opened in the heart of the scholarly faction. When the girl dressed in black stepped out of the gate, she didn’t seem worried in the slightest.

Song Shuhang, who was hidden in the right fist that had been shot out by the steel giant, was left speechless.

The last big shot who dared to talk to me like that was blasted apart by yours truly!

No, wait... Didn’t I already give you Senior Skylark’s head? Are you not happy with your new head? Why do you still want to screw my head off?

This was the virtuous lamia’s way of reminding Song Shuhang of what happened between him and Pavilion Master Chu Two.

What the hell happened to Pavilion Master Chu Two while she was in the Netherworld Realm?

The fist that was shot out could be retracted, of course!

The steel giant entered combat mode.

“I’ll deal with Sage White. As for Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, I’ll leave him to you.” The demon bear then roared, “Kill them— Aahhh~”

All of a sudden, the demonic bear was sent flying again.

This time, it flew even higher and farther.

Its huge body spun unceasingly in the air, black blood spewing out from its mouth and fur falling off its body nonstop. Besides that, there seemed to be a couple of bear teeth that flew out of its mouth.

The scene looked painful even just from watching.

It was Pavilion Master Chu Two who had suddenly attacked the demonic bear.

The black blood of the evil demon dripped to the ground, and the evil energy contained within started corroding the soil. Every drop of blood of a Ninth Stage evil demon was poisonous to the extreme. If it was not dealt with immediately, this patch of land would become a wasteland.

At this time, the world of the golden lotus took action and “roots” similar to those of Song Shuhang’s Inner World flew out from it. These roots then penetrated into the contaminated ground and instantly absorbed the black blood, even packing up and taking the contaminated ground along.

Song Shuhang’s Inner World did not want to lose out. It also extended its roots, taking the bear fur that had fallen to the ground.

The pollution brought about by an evil demon, which was a headache for most cultivators, became nothing but nutrition for the roots.

The demonic bear finally managed to stabilize its body, its eyes fixed on the girl in black.

Its mission of testing its new helper’s strength and sincerity was now half-complete.

While there did not seem to be any sincerity coming from the other party... Her strength was far beyond its expectations.

Her power isn’t at the level of a Tribulation Transcender at all... That strike she launched at me possessed the power of a path and was at the Immortal level. She’s an Immortal.

However, even after it realized this, the demonic bear could not wrap its head around why an evil demon of the Netherworld like her would help a human cultivator.

It just didn’t make any sense.

??????

Song Shuhang’s figure leaped out of the steel giant’s right fist, landing next to Sixteen and Senior White.

Pavilion Master Chu Two yawned. She then went to Song Shuhang’s side, stretched out her small hands, and touched his head lightly. It was as if she was at the supermarket, touching a watermelon to see if it was ripe.

Song Shuhang froze. “Senior Chu, let’s talk about this. How about you don’t screw my head off?”

Pavilion Master Chu Two asked, “Were you talking about eating me just now?”

“Of course not! How could I possibly even think of doing something so cruel?” Song Shuhang replied quickly. He now felt as if Pavilion Master Chu’s main body had been instigating him previously so that he would fall into this trap.

“Hm, well I do have a new head, so I’m not that interested in yours now,” Pavilion Master Chu Two said calmly. She then turned to look at Sixteen who was beside her, and said, “There’s no need to be so nervous.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen was speechless.

Sister White Dragon smiled slightly. “Actually, we weren’t nervous.”

Pavilion Master Chu Two nodded and said to Song Shuhang, “When I was wandering in the Netherworld Realm, I met this bear king. I happened to hear that they were planning on heading to the scholarly faction, and I also heard them mention the words ‘Heavenly City Fragments’ and ‘Profound Sage Tyrannical Song,’ so I decided to go with them.”

As she had been slightly concerned about what the bear king intended to do to Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, she came up with the great idea of going with the bear king to see what it was that it intended to do.

And that ultimately led to the current scene.

The demonic bear said, “As an evil demon of the Netherworld, you’re actually interested in a human cultivator? This is really beyond my expectations.”

It had surprisingly not taken the opportunity it had to leave through a spatial gate, and instead stayed in the scholarly faction. It was truly a wonder as to what the bear was planning.

Pavilion Master Chu Two said, “I switched sides pretty late in life.”

The demonic bear was puzzled.

Pavilion Master Chu Two explained patiently, “I used to be a human... Or rather, an inner demon. Eventually, I managed to gain a mind of my own and because of a little coincidence, I ended up in this state where I’m an evil demon of the Netherworld.”

The demonic bear asked, “So, you and this human are old acquaintances?”

Song Shuhang could not help but say, “Truth be told, native demons of the Netherworld can also become good friends with humans.”

The demonic hamster had a pretty good relationship with him.

The ruler of the Netherworld, Senior White Two, was one of his most powerful helpers—at least every now and then.

The demonic bear said, “Shut up! There can’t possibly be such a shameful evil demon.”

After saying that, it raised its paws and roared, “Come out, Mogal! It’s time to fight!”

[This is bad!] The driver uncle, who was quietly hiding among the crowd, grew worried.

The demonic bear wanted to summon the power of the “demon god” through the parasite in its body. If it were to fuse with the power of a demon god, the situation would become very troublesome.

The demonic bear could not be allowed to summon the parasitic demon god in its body.

Otherwise, its combat power would jump to a level close to the Immortal Realm, making it very difficult to deal with it. The damage it would cause to the heart of the scholarly faction would be tremendous.

It seemed that driver uncle would have to make a move to stop the demonic bear.

At this time, exposing himself was unavoidable.

“Roooaaar, huh?” The demonic bear discovered a big problem after roaring for a short while.

In the past, as long as it willed it, the parasite would immediately begin cooperating with it. But this time, it was as if there was a problem with Mogal. It was not responding to any of its thoughts.

“What happened?” The demonic bear was stunned—this was the first time that it encountered such a situation.

Meanwhile, Shuhang’s side was also confused.

After all, the demonic bear looked like it was about to make a big move from the way it was acting. As such, all of them had prepared their defenses to resist whatever it was that the bear was going to throw at them. However, even after roaring for so long, nothing came from the bear.

Both sides found themselves in a rather awkward situation.

Song Shuhang asked, “Did it fail to use its skill?”

“Perhaps it got influenced by the scholarly faction’s defensive formations?” the black Scarlet Heaven Sword said—after all, they were currently at the very heart of the scholarly faction, the domain of the Scholarly Sage. It would not be strange if the Scholarly Sage, who had been able to suppress the entire universe back then, had left some high-level mechanisms or formations that specifically countered evil demons.

It was also possible that a powerful expert from the scholarly faction had made a move in secret.

Both the demonic bear and Sister White Dragon had faintly sensed a powerful aura within the crowd.

“Rooaarrr~” The demonic bear roared loudly once again. It was frantically trying to summon Mogal, who was inside its body.

“Should we give it a chance? It looks like it’s really trying its hardest...” The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said. “Hehe, just kidding, let’s take this opportunity to kill it!”

As a pure-blooded inner demon, its actions would naturally match its nature. It was someone who loved taking advantage of the chaos to deal with its targets.

“Wait... He was my companion for a while, so let’s at least give it a chance to show what it’s got,” Pavilion Master Chu Two said. “I can guarantee that it won’t be able to do much. No matter how much power it erupts with, I’ll deal with it instantly.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

Are you even an inner demon?

Sister White Dragon said, “Since Fellow Daoist has said so, we have no reason to object. Let’s wait.”

Song Shuhang looked up at the sky.

I now feel as if this demonic bear is really pitiful.

This is exactly why it’s important to choose your teammates well!

??????

After roaring for quite a while, Mogal’s energy inside the demonic bear’s body finally responded to its calls.

However, the energy with which Mogal responded was particularly weak; it was akin to water squeezed from a dry sponge.

The demonic bear asked, [Mogal, what’s wrong with you?]

[I don’t know. My power seems to have left me all of a sudden. I’ve never experienced something like this.] The demon god parasitizing the demonic bear’s body replied weakly.

It felt as if it had died and resurrected.

As a special parasitic-type demonic creature, as long as its host had not died, Mogal could resurrect through the energy of its host.

This manner of existence faintly resembled that of a manifestation of light of virtue.

[How?] A feeling of despair welled up in the demonic bear’s heart.

It lowered its head slightly and looked at Song Shuhang.

Suddenly, it thought of a possibility. “It was you!”

Song Shuhang was puzzled.

The demonic bear pointed at Song Shuhang and said solemnly, “I see now. I underestimated you, first Sage in a thousand years Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.”

Song Shuhang quickly hid his confused expression, and the corners of his mouth curled up, revealing a smile that seemed to show that everything was under his control. Although he had no idea what the demon bear was talking about, he knew that things would work out for him as long as he smiled in response.

As long as he smiled handsomely, there was no need for words.

When the demonic bear saw his smile, it would complete the plot on its own.

“This time around, I accept my loss,” said the demonic bear, “but when I come back, it will be your downfall!”

After saying that, it roared and opened a spatial gate to escape.

This evil demon of the Netherworld did not display reckless bravery.

It must immediately report the scholarly faction’s movements to its master—at that time, as long as it could bring over a strand of its master’s power, it would be able to absolutely trample on Profound Sage Tyrannical Song.

“Seal the space!” Song Shuhang transmitted his voice to several seniors.

“It’s fine to let it escape.” said Pavilion Master Chu Two slowly. “My Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion is waiting for it on the other end of the spatial passage.”

Song Shuhang asked, “You even prepared for something like that?”

While speaking, the demonic bear had already entered the spatial channel and disappeared.

“I’m going to hammer it back.” Pavilion Master Chu Two then spoke to the strand of hair above Song Shuhang’s head, “Head, lend me your power.”

She had mentioned previously that the demonic bear was discussing some plans with several other evil demons of the Netherworld on how they should go about dealing with the scholarly faction. In other words, the demonic bear had other companions.

She needed the help of Pavilion Master Chu’s main body in order to deal with them.

Pavilion Master Chu replied, “I don’t have much energy stored right now. I can only unleash three strikes at most.”

“That’s enough,” said Pavilion Master Chu Two—with her and Pavilion Master Chu’s powers combined, they would be able to unleash their genuine strength. “I can supply the energy for both of us.”

And so on Song Shuhang’s head, two more strands of hair that were seven-meter-long grew out.

There were now a total of three strands of long hair swaying in the air.

Pavilion Master Chu Two stretched out her hand, and the three strands of hair fell into her hands.

She grabbed the three seven-meter-long strands of hair and inserted them into her own head. Afterward, she waved her hand and opened a spatial passage before disappearing into it.

Pavilion Master Chu Two and the demonic bear had come and gone in quite a hurry.

Senior White stretched out his hand and handed the black Scarlet Heaven Sword back to Song Shuhang. Afterward, he said inexplicably, “I’m almost there.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Almost there?”

“I’m almost at my limit. I don’t have much energy left.” Senior White’s clone pointed at himself. “I’m going to save on using energy as much as possible.”

Song Shuhang said, “Senior White, you’ve worked hard. You can leave the rest to us.”

Even when Senior White’s clone had little energy left, he could still function as a good luck charm; he only had to stand there.

Heavenly City Fragment, Inner Demon Cave.

Song Shuhang and the others entered the Inner Demon Cave.

Before being interrupted by the demonic bear, they were just about to enter and check the cave.

Scarlet Heaven Sword, who was suspended behind Song Shuhang’s waist, said. “Brr~ This place makes me feel very uncomfortable.”

The moment it entered the cave, it felt chills that made its heart shiver.

This place was filled with malice toward inner demons.

Sister White Dragon’s gaze scoured the Inner Demon Cave and found nothing of value.

True Monarch Eternal Fire wondered, “Fellow Daoist White, did you find anything over there?”

Senior White’s clone shook his head. “It would be nice if my main body was here right now.”

That way, he could just grab his main body and swing it around. Wherever the main body landed, a treasure would be found.

Although he was very lucky as a clone, he could not act as a human-shaped treasure detector like his main body. After all, his main body was unique.

“Senior White, you’re thinking of abusing your main body again!” said Song Shuhang.?If you do that, you’re going to harm the next clone of Senior White.

Senior White’s clone looked calm. “It’s fine. After all, it’s the next clone that is going to have to face the consequences; that has nothing to do with me.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

The next clone of Senior White is going to cry because of this.

“Anyway, if there’s nothing we can do, perhaps we can just slice this place apart,” said Senior White’s clone. No matter what was hidden in this Inner Demon Cave, as long as it was sliced apart enough times, the things hidden inside it would be revealed.

As this Inner Demon Cave already belonged to him, he did not mind slicing it apart.

Song Shuhang said, “Let’s wait a bit. Even my secret appraisal technique was unable to fully appraise this Inner Demon Cave, so its value is extraordinary. It would be a pity to just slice it up. We should leave that as our last resort.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword suggested, “Otherwise, let’s grab Song Shuhang and throw him around. Doesn’t he have ‘decent luck’ right now? Perhaps that can also be used for finding treasures!”

Song Shuhang waved his hands repeatedly. “I’m not Senior White. I don’t have this kind of power!”

“That won’t work,” said Senior White’s clone calmly. “Song Shuhang’s decent luck expired yesterday. It took us an entire day to move the Heavenly City Fragments; I’m afraid that he no longer has that ‘decent luck’.”

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

I finally got a day of “decent luck” and I didn’t get to use it for anything? It expired just like that? Then what’s my fortune today?

Song Shuhang turned his head and asked, “Senior White, could you do another divination for me?”

Does ‘decent luck’ have a renewal function?

If not, I’m fine with something like “lower luck” or “mediocre luck” as well.

“I’m not in the mood for fortune-telling today.” Senior White’s clone shook his head and said, “There’s nothing that can be done. It seems that there’s only one last method we can use. Shuhang, come here.”

Song Shuhang asked carefully, “Senior, you aren’t going to throw me around, are you?”

Senior White’s clone said calmly, “It’s better to throw yourself than to throw me.”

After saying that, he reached out to grab Song Shuhang, and then took out a bottle filled with dark purple liquid. “Open your eyes.”

Song Shuhang asked, “What is that?”

Senior White’s clone replied, “Eye drops.”

Song Shuhang said, “Senior White, don’t lie to me. There can’t possibly be eye drops that have that color. Who would possibly put that in their eyes?”

Senior White’s clone replied, “You’ve been gouging out your eyes so often, yet you’re afraid of putting a few drops into them?”

Hmm, Senior White does have a point.

Under Senior White’s control, the dark violet medicinal drops dripped into Song Shuhang’s left eye socket—where the Scholarly Sage’s eye was at this moment.

Recently, Fairy Creation had not helped Song Shuhang to replace the eye in his left eye socket. As such, the Sage’s eye was still there.

As the dark violet liquid dripped into his eye socket, Song Shuhang felt a cool feeling, which he enjoyed quite a bit.

At the same time, the Scholarly Sage’s eye was activated.

Under the gaze of the Sage’s eye, there was nothing that could remain hidden.

Senior White’s clone asked, “How does it feel?”

Song Shuhang replied, “I feel like I can now use the Sage’s eye to cast the Twins Impregnating Gaze.”

Senior White’s clone: “...”

I think that it would be better for you to pluck your eye out right now.

“By the way, Senior White, what exactly is that thing in your hand?” Song Shuhang scoured the Inner Demon Cave with the Sage’s eye.

“It’s really just eye drops,” Senior White replied. “This is the secret technique of one of my monster spirit friends... By the way, they are little eyeball-shaped monster spirits; they’re very cute. When the opportunity presents itself, I can introduce them to you.”

Song Shuhang said, “I think I’ll pass on that.”

He was kind of allergic to “eyeballs” now.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, “Did you find anything?”

Song Shuhang said curiously, “Not yet. It’s strange, though. I scanned the entire Inner Demon Cave but found nothing. Is the valuable item the Inner Demon Cave itself, rather than some hidden treasure inside it?”

Sister White Dragon thought for a few moments before saying “Since the treasure is the Inner Demon Cave itself, why don’t you find a few cultivators plagued by inner demons and bring them here?”

Song Shuhang said, “Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword is an inner demon. Also, there’s the black-skinned Soft Feather in my shadow. However, neither of them seem to have had any special reaction to the Inner Demon Cave.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “Actually, I do feel a little something... I feel that this place is full of malice toward me, and I would really like to get out of here quickly.”

“Actually, Fellow Daoist Scarlet Heaven Sword and the black-skinned Soft Feather are mutated inner demons. They are not even afraid of the light of virtue, so they aren’t that reliable when it comes to such things,” Sister White Dragon said. “So, we need to find a cultivator who happens to be haunted by an inner demon. Then, we have to bring them into this Inner Demon Cave and carry out some experiments.”

Song Shuhang said while pinching his chin, “I happen to know a little cultivator who is about to transcend his tribulation, and he’s currently haunted by an inner demon. Before I came to the scholarly faction, he greeted me over at Medicine Master’s building.”

But that little guy is very polite. It really wouldn’t be suitable to use him for an experiment.

Besides that guy...

Oh right, there’s someone else who fits the bill much better.

At the same time that he thought of that, Sixteen said, “Shuhang, we also have Young Master Hai.”

“I was also just thinking about him.” Song Shuhang laughed.

Then, he stretched out his hand and moved over the clone of Young Master Hai from the Inner World.

Young Master Hai’s clone was currently in a coma.

Since it was only a clone, it was pretty much meaningless to kill it. It was more useful alive than dead to Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang remembered that before capturing the clone, he caused the birth of an inner demon in its heart. Now, that could come in handy.

When Young Master Hai’s clone was transferred out of the Inner World, he was immediately brought to the Inner Demon Cave. The clone’s eyes widened, and he shouted, “What is this place?!”

He felt chills all over his body, and the cold seemed to seep all the way through to his bones. The cold feeling made him feel like getting a thick sheet and wrapping it around his body.

Song Shuhang replied, “This is the Inner Demon Cave, a very valuable place.”

At the same time, the Sage’s eye in his left eye socket finally saw something interesting.

Inside the Inner Demon Cave, there seemed to be a kind of energy that enveloped Young Master Hai.

This energy began to form a vortex, creating a powerful suction force.

Then, there was a mass of black mist that was forcibly pulled out from Young Master Hai’s clone.

“It’s the inner demon.” The demonic chef heart in Song Shuhang’s body reacted.

“Crack~”

A crisp sound echoed.

The inner demon that was forcefully pulled out from Young Master Hai’s clone was torn into two halves all of sudden. Afterward, one half of the inner demon was returned to the clone’s body.

It appeared that even the Heavenly Emperor’s Inner Demon Cave could not eradicate inner demons completely. It could only weaken them.

If one wanted to completely defeat and exterminate the inner demons in their body, they would have to rely on their own will.

Even after all the research that the Heavenly Emperor did on inner demons, she was unable to figure out a way to completely exterminate them.

As expected of inner demons, one of the most troublesome existences that cultivators had had to face since ancient times!

However, this is not what I should be focusing on right now.

Song Shuhang’s gaze shifted to the halved inner demon that had been forcibly taken from Young Master Hai’s clone.

The energy of the Inner Demon Cave firmly held the inner demon captive, making sure that it could not extricate itself from its grasp.

However, the Inner Demon Cave did not do anything afterward.

The cave was just a fragment, and it was very likely that it had lost its other features, making it unable to do anything to this inner demon. Either that or it was also possible that after forcefully drawing the inner demon out from a target, it would be left to the Heavenly Emperor to deal with.

“Regardless, this makes things a lot more convenient for me,” said Song Shuhang.

He rummaged through his Inner World and magical bracelet, but he did not find any magical treasure that could store an inner demon.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior White, do you have a way to seal this inner demon and store it somewhere?”

Senior White replied, “I’ll check... But my treasure trove is just too big. I’m not sure that I’m going to be able to find something that has those functions.”

He did not even know how many things were stored in his treasure trove.

After saying that, Senior White went into a daze and began to check his huge treasure trove.

Song Shuhang pinched his chin and looked at the inner demon floating in the air, thinking about how to cook it.

In Demon Emperor Hezhi’s ?Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet?, there were two dishes that were related to the inner demon tribulation.

One was the ?Smoked Inner Demon Tribulation Slices?, which would smoke an inner demon before slicing it up. The smoking process was the same as that of the ?Braised Heavenly Tribulation?, and it required quite a number of steps.

The other one was the ?Inner Demon Tribulation Sashimi Slices?. This dish would have the inner demon placed onto a chopping board and sliced up. Afterward, some seasonings would be added, then it would be ready to be eaten, fresh and tasty.

The ?Smoked Inner Demon Tribulation Slices?’s method was very easy to comprehend, and because of the smoking process, it would allow the inner demon tribulation to materialize and create an incomparably delicious dish.

On the other hand, the ?Inner Demon Tribulation Sashimi Slices? seemed quite difficult to handle, despite how simple it appeared.

Song Shuhang looked at the inner demon in the air.?An inner demon should have a body of pure energy, which makes it intangible. How am I supposed to slice it up? And after that, how is it supposed to be eaten?

Unless it was first transformed into something like the black Scarlet Heaven Sword or the black-skinned Soft Feather, it was quite difficult to picture how to prepare this dish.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, is there a way to transform this inner demon into something like you?”

The black-skinned Scarlet Heaven Sword replied quickly, “Yes.”

Song Shuhang’s eyes lit up.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said proudly, “Let me swallow it. After that, we can take it out of me and it should have a solid body. As an inner demon, I should be able to swallow it.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

Song Shuhang waved his hands. His left and right hands shone brightly as he pressed them onto Scarlet Heaven Sword’s body again and again, giving it ten instances of the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? in a single go.

Normally, Song Shuhang would only use three instances at one time on Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword as it gave it the perfect level of comfort.

As for having used it ten times, that was an accident.

“Ahhhh~ Stop, stop~ It’s too much!” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said weakly. “Actually, I don’t even have the ability to eat. I was just joking with you. I’m only a sword.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword continued, “However, I have a bold idea. Although I don’t have the ability to eat, I can...”

“Bah! Senior, please just shut up.” Song Shuhang fired another ten bursts of the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique?, making the black Scarlet Heaven Sword shut up.

It was truly stupid of me to ask the black Scarlet Heaven Sword such a question.

I’ve even been deceived by Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword to use the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? on it twenty times!

“Sixteen, Sister White Dragon, what do you think?” Song Shuhang looked at Sixteen.

Su Clan’s Sixteen shook her head. “Sorry, Shuhang, I can’t help you with this.”

Sister White Dragon said, “I feel like Fellow Daoist Scarlet Heaven Sword—”

Song Shuhang interrupted, “Sister White Dragon, please don’t be like it.”

“What in the world is in that head of yours?” Sister White Dragon did not know whether to cry or laugh. “Anyway, what I was trying to say was that I feel like we could use Fellow Daoist Scarlet Heaven Sword’s current state as a reference. By following the process by which it materialized, we might be able to do the same for the partial inner demon that was extracted.”

Song Shuhang said, “You have a point.”

Then, Song Shuhang summoned the black-skinned Soft Feather.

“Soft Feather, it’s time for you to shine,” Song Shuhang said.

The black-skinned Soft Feather replied in a gentle and polite manner, “Sorry, Senior Song. I don’t have any way to transform other people’s inner demons into an inner demon clone. The only thing that I can do is to carefully explain the main body’s research on inner demon clones, and then perhaps figure out how to make an inner demon acquire a solid state... However, the actual operation will probably require Senior Song’s help.”

Song Shuhang said, “Then, let’s go to the entrance of the Inner Demon Cave to discuss this.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, “Why go to the entrance of the cave?”

Song Shuhang smiled and said, “To save precious time.”
