Song Shuhang, Sixteen, Fairy Creation, the black-skinned Soft Feather, the virtuous lamia, and the dazed Senior White went to the entrance of the Inner Demon Cave.

Song Shuhang opened the entrance to the Inner World right beside him.

At this time, True Monarch Eternal Fire was still directing the members of the scholarly faction and moving Heavenly City Fragments into Song Shuhang’s Inner World before transferring them to the world of the golden lotus.

Meanwhile, Song Shuhang and several others began to discuss how to modify the inner demon clone technique into something that would allow inner demons to materialize.

This allowed them to work on two things at once, making the most of their time.

The discussion was still at the point where the black-skinned Soft Feather was explaining the principles and details of the inner demon clone technique. During this time, Sister White Dragon would occasionally raise some questions to clarify her understanding of the technique.

As they discussed and conversed on how to make an inner demon materialize, time swiftly passed.

Before they knew it, the sun had already wandered across the sky and began to set toward the west.

Another day was coming to an end.

The scholarly faction paused the transportation of Heavenly City Fragments. The disciples who were moving the fragments needed some rest, new Heavenly City Fragments needed to be brought over from other academies of the scholarly faction, and the formations that were used to compress the fragments needed maintenance.

Song Shuhang and the others were still in the middle of discussing how to materialize an inner demon.

After an entire day of discussion, they had already modified the ?Inner Demon Clone Technique?, making a huge step forward.

This was thanks to the contributions of the black-skinned Soft Feather.

Just over half an hour ago, the black-skinned Soft Feather suddenly entered a state of pseudo-enlightenment and proposed many innovative solutions.

It could be said that she alone had greatly pushed forward the progress of the modification plan.

“Okay, let’s take a rest first. I’ll sort out and organize the ideas that were proposed just now. Later on, we can do some experimentation and see which works the best.” Song Shuhang raised his head and said, “We really have to thank Soft Feath— Holy Shi... Heavens!”

Song Shuhang had to stop himself mid-sentence because he discovered that, beside the black-skinned Soft Feather, there was another Soft Feather.

Initially, as the figures of the two Soft Feathers overlapped, Song Shuhang had not noticed the new Soft Feather at all. It was only at the end of the discussion that he realized that there were suddenly two Soft Feathers.

Hmm, I’ll go by exclusion.

The new Soft Feather had white skin. She did not look like a twin or a split of the black-skinned Soft Feather. Inside the Inner Demon Cave, the inner demon that had been drawn out from Young Master Hai’s body was still intact, and nothing had really happened to it yet.

She was clearly not Soft Feather’s main body, either. Soft Feather’s main body had followed Sage Monarch Spirit Butterfly back to Spirit Butterfly Island to enter into seclusion. It was impossible for her to have suddenly come over from Spirit Butterfly Island.

So... She must be the Heavenly Emperor.

Song Shuhang got in touch with his Inner World, discovering that he could still open it.

Additionally, Senior White’s clone was still around, albeit a little distracted.

Overall, things did not seem like they were too bad for him.

“Hi, Senior Song.” The Soft Feather who Song Shuhang suspected to be the Heavenly Emperor waved at him.

“Heavenly Emperor,” said Song Shuhang in a deep voice.

The virtuous lamia, Fairy Creation, and the black-skinned Soft Feather quickly moved behind Song Shuhang, arranging themselves according to their height.

No wonder Soft Feather suddenly put forward so many creative and highly feasible suggestions; it turned out to be the Heavenly Emperor all along!

“Oh, Senior Song, there’s no need to be afraid. I didn’t come here today to target you.” The Soft Feather possessed by the Heavenly Emperor said with a smile.

“Did you come for the Heavenly City Fragments?” Song Shuhang asked rhetorically.

He quickly came to this conclusion because the only thing in the scholarly faction that could attract the Heavenly Emperor were the Heavenly City Fragments.

The Heavenly Emperor smiled slightly and said, “Yes, I just want to take back the things that belong to me. So, Senior Song, you have no reason to stop me, right?”

Retrieving one’s own things was a matter of course.

Song Shuhang: “...”

In his Inner World, there were quite a number of fragments.

“However, I’m not in much of a hurry to retrieve the fragments. So I came to have a chat with you first, Senior Song. After all, we haven’t seen each other for a while,” said the Heavenly Emperor with a smile.

“Nonsense. You were also there when we were eating the Braised Heavenly Tribulation on Heavenly Field Island,” said Song Shuhang. She had even taken the Eastern Spring Pavilion Fragment that he was supposed to get from the Almighty Merchant!

Speaking of which, what had happened to the Almighty Merchant? Didn’t he say that he was going to chase the Heavenly Emperor to get back the fragments? The Heavenly Emperor was here, so where was the Almighty Merchant?

Should he use one of the tickets to summon him?

“Hehehe.” The Heavenly Emperor glanced at Song Shuhang and said meaningfully, “Don’t even bother trying to contact Fellow Daoist Almighty Merchant; he won’t come over. At least for a short while, he won’t be appearing again.”

Song Shuhang was shocked.

What happened to the Almighty Merchant? Was he done in by the Heavenly Emperor? Since she said that he won’t be appearing for a while, was he sealed somewhere?

How unreliable!

Back on the Heavenly Field, the Almighty Merchant said that he was confident that his fists were harder than the Heavenly Emperor’s, and that he would definitely face no problem in collecting what the Heavenly Emperor owed him. Yet, he was cheated in the end.

The next time we meet, should I use this to ridicule the Almighty Merchant and rend his heart?

It seemed likely that it was because of the ?Steel Hands Technique? that he inherited the Heavy Metal Sect’s hobby of rending others’ hearts. Song Shuhang felt that ever since he reached the master level in the ?Steel Hands Technique?, he always felt the urge to rend others’ hearts.

For example, right now, he really wanted to see the distressed, regretful, and heartbroken expression on the face of the Almighty Merchant.

Although he knew it was wrong to think so, his thoughts were like a car driven by Senior White, and he could not stop them at all.

Eh... Why am I having such thoughts?

Song Shuhang shook his head, throwing this strange thought out of his head.

This is not the normal me. I must have been secretly affected by something...

When he thought of this, Song Shuhang glanced at the Inner Demon Cave, and then at the Heavenly Emperor beside him.

[Could it be that the Heavenly Emperor is secretly using this Inner Demon Cave to influence my thoughts?]

The Inner Demon Cave was the personal laboratory of the Heavenly Emperor. She definitely had various means set up to control the Inner Demon Cave.

However, she underestimated him too much.

Although the time that he had cultivated was very short, his will was extremely strong; it was what he was the proudest of after his pain tolerance.

The Heavenly Emperor glanced at Shuhang’s proud expression, discovering that she could not read Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s thoughts from his facial expressions alone.

She really had no clue what the inexplicable pride on his face meant.

Did Tyrannical Song finally learn how to hide his thoughts with awkward expressions?

“It’s almost time. My people are here.” The Heavenly Emperor stood up. “Senior Song, just stay here and don’t roam about. I’m just getting my things back from the scholarly faction. As for this Inner Demon Cave... It no longer has any value to me. Originally, it was meant to be used to study inner demons to find a strange guy, but now it’s useless.”

In addition, she had already retrieved the remnant “path” from the Inner Demon Cave.

After saying that, the Heavenly Emperor left the Inner Demon Cave.

As soon as the Heavenly Emperor left, Song Shuhang shouted, “Contact Senior Eternal Fire!”

The scholarly faction had a lot of uninvited guests today.

As soon as the demonic bear was sent away, the even more troublesome Heavenly Emperor arrived—and it seemed like the Heavenly Emperor had come with a large group of people.

Sixteen raised her head and said, “I just sent a message to Senior Eternal Fire. He has already received it.”

Senior Eternal Fire replied to her with a wryly smiling emoji.

“I’m afraid that there’s nobody in the scholarly faction that can stop the Heavenly Emperor. Moreover, the Heavenly Emperor brought reinforcements,” said Sister White Dragon.

Of course, that was unless the owner of that powerful aura made a move.

“Fairy Creation.” Song Shuhang looked at Fairy Creation. “At a time like this, you should activate any hidden means that the scholarly faction has.”

As a direct disciple of the Scholarly Sage, Fairy Creation had been left responsible for guarding the Sage’s eye.

Now that she was in the stronghold of the scholarly faction, there should be some measures that she could take, right?

Fairy Creation replied, “Song~ Stupid.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

Fairy Creation’s personality A was completely unreliable. If it was Fairy Creation’s personality B that was present, she may have still come in handy.

However, her personality B almost never showed up.

Song Shuhang said, “Sister White Dragon, are we going to make a move?”

“And whose side should I take?” Sister White Dragon said. “Although I am with Sixteen now, don’t forget that I used to be the Ancestral Golden Dragon of the Heavenly City.”

Her feelings for the Heavenly City were very complicated. Although she used her death to separate herself from the Heavenly City, it was purely because she did not want to be constrained by the Heavenly Emperor’s path.

She still had many beautiful memories of the Ancient Heavenly City, and most of the time she had spent with Slow-Witted Song was in the Heavenly City.

Her attitude towards the Heavenly City was very similar to that of the Great Northern Emperor.

“Furthermore, in my current state, I can only resist the Heavenly Emperor for a short time. I can probably only give you enough time to retreat. If you want me to fight her head-on... Well, I simply do not have the energy for such an ordeal. After a while, I’d just end up being smashed to pieces and forced to regather in Sixteen’s body,” Sister White Dragon added.

“Don’t worry, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.” At this time, an ordinary-looking man stepped forward. “You’ve already done a lot for the scholarly faction. You can leave the rest to me.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Who are you, Uncle?”

“I’m the one who drove you guys here.” The uncle wiped his face, and the aura emanating from him changed into that of a refined gentleman.

“It’s you!” Song Shuhang once again linked the man in front of him to the blurred figure in his memory.

“You don’t have to worry. You’ve already helped the scholarly faction a great deal; we owe you for all the help that you have provided us.” The uncle stretched out his hand and gave Song Shuhang a volume of the ?Writing of the Sage?.

This was a scripture written by the Scholarly Sage when he was still alive.

Song Shuhang still felt worried. “The Heavenly Emperor has companions. I’m afraid that none of them are going to be weak. Are you sure you’re going to be alright, uncle?”

The driver uncle smiled and said, “Don’t worry, I also have a companion.”

Then, another figure emerged from the crowd.

It was a buddhist monk whose entire body seemed to have been cast from gold, and his muscles were exceptionally well-built. When he looked at him, Song Shuhang had the illusion as if all the muscles in the world were “growing” on this monk’s body

This buddhist monk put his palms together, revealing a faint smile. This smile was especially warm.

Song Shuhang’s eyes made contact with him.

Afterward, he sensed a sense of intimacy with this buddhist monk. It was the kind where the cultivation techniques they practiced resonated with one another.

Song Shuhang subconsciously asked, “Are you from the Jingang Temple?”

The buddhist monk’s smile grew brighter and he nodded gently.

On the top of Song Shuhang’s head, a seven-meter-long strand of hair suddenly appeared. It was another one of Pavilion Master Chu’s strands of hair.

The strand of hair quickly moved towards the buddhist monk, and the tip of the hair was like a spike as it directly shot toward the monk’s eyes.

The buddhist monk remained motionless, his hands still clasped together.

Pavilion Master Chu’s hair paused right in front of the monk.

After a while, the long hair slowly retracted.

Pavilion Master Chu said, “It’s not him.”

Previously, when the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion collapsed, Slow-Witted Song had appeared before her in a form very similar to the form of this great master from the Jingang Temple.

But the buddhist monk in front of them was not Slow-Witted Song.

This buddhist monk was a genuine great master from the Jingang Temple. In addition, the path to immortality that he walked was the buddhist path of the Jingang Temple.

Nevertheless, one thing was certain. This great master of the Jingang Temple and the driver uncle should have something to do with Slow-Witted Song.

However, this information could not be shared with White Dragon. So, Pavilion Master Chu did not reveal anything.

Pavilion Master Chu asked directly, “What is your goal?”

The Jingang Temple great master smiled slightly and replied, “We want to prevent the Heavenly Emperor from reclaiming the Heavenly City Fragments and delay her rebuilding of the Heavenly City. What follows after... Is the ultimate goal of our alliance, and that cannot be shared to the public for the time being.”

When Song Shuhang heard this, a series of clues appeared in his mind. He thought of [Wielder of the Will Liquid Metal Ball], the Heavenly Emperor, the fragment of the first ghost spirit ever, Cheng Lin, and so on.

[Wielder of the Will Liquid Metal Ball] had a plan—it wanted to use the path of the Heavenly Emperor to complete its body.

However, this plan had failed in the past.

But now, with the return of the Heavenly Emperor, the plan became feasible again.

With the driver uncle and the buddhist monk having formed an alliance that aimed to prevent the Heavenly Emperor from rebuilding the Heavenly City, their ultimate goal was already evident.

Everything suddenly became clear.

??????

“Anyway, thank you, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song.” The driver uncle flung his robe handsomely and strode to the Heavenly Emperor in the distance. “If we ever happen to meet in the future, I will definitely teach you a set of combat techniques that will satisfy you.”

Song Shuhang reminded, “I want those from the scholarly faction!”

The Jingang Temple great master paused slightly. Then, he turned around and smiled. “If you want to learn combat techniques of the scholarly faction, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song can come and learn them from me.”

Song Shuhang: “???”

I learned a lost technique of the Jingang Temple from an expert from the scholarly faction who drove us over. And now, I’m being told to go to a great master from the Jingang Temple if I want to learn techniques of the scholarly faction? Did you two change souls or something? Or perhaps you accidentally swapped scripts?

The Jingang Temple’s great master laughed out loud before heading toward the Heavenly Emperor in the distance with the driver uncle.

The driver uncle said, “Let’s move the location of the battle to outside the scholarly faction.”

The great master nodded slightly and said, “No problem, leave it to me. That is what I’m good at.”

??????

The two seniors who appeared to be very powerful had left just like that.

Sister White Dragon said slowly, “If it’s only the two of them, I doubt that they have what it takes to deal with the Heavenly Emperor.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Is the Heavenly Emperor that strong? She hasn’t fully recovered to her peak state. Actually, she hasn’t even restored her path.”

Sister White Dragon said, “Back during the era of the Ancient Heavenly City, in addition to the Great Emperors of the Four Cardinal Directions, there were several other hidden Immortal-level existences.”

Song Shuhang said, “Are you referring to those like you, Cheng Lin, and that Immortal monster hunter whose arms are filled with eyes? Did Fairy White Bone also reach this level towards the end?”

When Shuhang mentioned the monster hunter whose arms were filled with eyes, Pavilion Master Chu’s hair, which was on his head, shook slightly.

Sister White Dragon asked, “Have you done a lot of research on the Heavenly City?”

Song Shuhang replied, “A bit. However, among the Great Emperors of the Four Cardinal Directions, the Great Northern Emperor has already left the Heavenly City, and the Great Southern Emperor had a fight with Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven not long ago. Now that I mention that, I wonder how they’re currently doing. Anyway, you and Cheng Lin have also left the Heavenly City. Meanwhile, that Immortal whose arms are filled with eyes was caught by ‘Beep-Beep-Beep~ and ended up being locked up. He would likely not be able to do anything for quite some time. Does the Heavenly Emperor have any other Immortal-level companions?”

Sister White Dragon said, “It is extremely difficult to kill off someone who has already stepped into the Immortal Realm. Therefore, the Heavenly Emperor is likely to have 3 or 4 Immortal-level companions with full combat strength... This is still only the information I can gather using my memories. In the worst possible case, there is a chance that some of those who survived the collapse of the Heavenly City managed to take that final step and reach the Immortal Realm during the long time that has passed then.”

“That’s really scary.” Song Shuhang scratched his head.

He stared into the distance in dismay.

Even though the Heavenly Emperor seemed to be very talkative recently, she had always been at the top of Song Shuhang’s list of people he least wanted to meet.

Even if there came a day when the Heavenly Emperor jokingly stabbed him in the back, he would not be surprised at all.

The current “truce” between them was the result of the Heavenly Emperor borrowing Soft Feather’s face, and Song Shuhang knew this very well.

After all, if the Heavenly Emperor had used the face of a grown man to approach him, it would have been useless.

Song Shuhang said, “I’ve been considering some things. Should I go fight as well?”

“How are you planning to fight?” asked the black Scarlet Heaven Sword. “Otherwise, how about I find a way to contact my main body and ask Scarlet Heaven to give me some energy? That way, you’ll be able to let out a slash or two.”

“Let’s see if Senior White has any treasures that can contain inner demons first,” said Song Shuhang. “If he does, then it’s time for my demonic cooking skills to shine.”

??????

The Heavenly Emperor placed her hands behind her back, smiling like an ordinary girl as she walked through the scholarly faction.

“Haha, go ahead.” She smiled happily and said, “Come and fight me. I can’t wait to see what other interesting tricks you have.”

Song Shuhang asked the dazed Senior White softly, “Senior White, have you found anything that can contain an inner demon yet?”

He was afraid that if he spoke too loudly, Senior White might be startled and fall to the ground accidentally.

Shuhang no longer had the “decent luck” that he had yesterday. As such, there was nothing wrong with being cautious.

After hearing someone call him, Senior White finally came back to his senses and said, “Hm, I found a few items that might come in handy. I’ll try them out later to see if any of them work.”

After saying that, he used his spatial abilities to reach his arm into his treasure trove, and took out the five items that he thought might be useful.

There was a metal box that gave off a very techy feeling, a white jade bottle, a bag made of silk, a crystal ball-shaped magical treasure, and a simple pot.

“What are you going to do next?” Senior White handed all five magical treasures over to Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang could not hold so many magical treasures with only two hands, so he had to use his psychic energy to keep them suspended in the air around him—ever since he learned to use psychic energy, Song Shuhang discovered that he could not live without it anymore.

“From a purely rational perspective, I’ve been thinking of taking advantage of the chaos to launch an attack on the Heavenly Emperor. In the end, the two of us are enemies,” said Song Shuhang.

The revived Heavenly Emperor belonged to the camp of the ball of liquid metal.

Senior White’s clone said, ??”A purely rational perspective?”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword guessed, “Is it because the Heavenly Emperor has Soft Feather’s face, so from an emotional point of view, you can’t bring yourself to hit her?”

Song Shuhang replied, “No, I mean that thinking from an emotional point of view, it really isn’t right for me, a weakling, to be fighting big shots like her all the time. Against opponents of such a level, it would be much smarter for me to run as far away as I can.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword looked at Song Shuhang in shock. “So you have some self-knowledge. I always thought that you were so full of yourself that you forgot that you were a weakling.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

I’m not that reckless.

Senior White’s clone said, “Speaking of which, you’re talking about attacking the Heavenly Emperor while in her Inner Demon Cave. Are you not afraid that she will discover your plan?”

Song Shuhang’s face stiffened, but he quickly regained his composure, “It’s okay, Senior White. I’m just going to conspire openly.”

Regardless of whether the Heavenly Emperor could hear him or not, he would start by talking big. When betting while being broke, you barely risked anything and even had a chance of making money if you were lucky.

When it came to launching attacks, using psychological attacks first was the key.

Senior White asked, “Alright, what are you going to do?”

Song Shuhang replied, “I’m going to cook up the inner demon and then slice it up into inner demon sashimi.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, “Do you plan to lure the Heavenly Emperor over for an inner demon banquet? Are you thinking of making her give up on her designs on the scholarly faction by doing that?”

Sixteen smiled and said, “Senior, Shuhang’s plan definitely isn’t that ridiculous.”

“Yep,” Song Shuhang said, “just watch.”

Then, he entered the Inner Demon Cave with the five magical treasures that Senior White gave him floating around him.

The inner demon drawn from Young Master Hai’s clone was still in mid-air; it was crumpled into a ball and rolled around repeatedly.

Senior White and the others followed behind Shuhang.

“Huh?” Sister White Dragon suddenly exclaimed.

She felt that something was missing from this Inner Demon Cave, similar to when other fragments were licked by Song Shuhang’s Inner World.

Senior White mused, “There’s something missing from this fragment.”

“The things that’s missing should have been recovered by the Heavenly Emperor,” Su Clan’s Sixteen guessed.

The Heavenly Emperor had been in the Inner Demon Cave for quite a while. If there was something missing from this Heavenly City Fragment, it should have been taken by her.

“If that’s the case...” Sister White Dragon glanced at Song Shuhang.

Shuhang has been snatching the food from the Heavenly Emperor’s mouth and licking away whatever she wanted to retrieve.

If things were to continue developing in this manner, there would definitely be a battle between Song Shuhang and the Heavenly Emperor in the future.

??????

Senior White’s clone said, “Forget it, as long as the Inner Demon Cave is still here, its other functions should still be available.”

Song Shuhang nodded, heading toward the inner demon.

In his mind, he began to recall the several suggestions and plans that everybody had come up with during their discussion on inner demon materialization just now.

The black-skinned Soft Feather asked, “Which plan is Senior Song going to use?”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword seized the opportunity to say, “I still feel like my initial suggestion was very good. I don’t have the ability to eat, but the black-skinned Soft Feather does.”

The black-skinned Soft Feather said firmly, “I have a name, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword. Besides, I would never agree to going through with that plan of yours.”

“I’ll try each of the plans we discussed before,” replied Song Shuhang calmly. As long as you kept your calm, everything would go well.

He would absolutely not let Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword continue to deceive him on using the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? on it.

This was a good way of teaching it a lesson.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword had been provoking him all this time and rending his heart. The best he could do when faced with these provocations was to remain as calm as possible. Over time, he would definitely develop the character of a reliable and stable senior by doing so.

He believed that this was the correct way to make use of the black Scarlet Heaven Sword.

“Let’s get started,” said Song Shuhang. By using his will, he transferred out a set of kitchen utensils from the Ancient Heavenly City’s Canteen No. 111 back in the Inner World.

Inner demons were generally invisible. If it was not for the Scholarly Sage’s eye, Song Shuhang would not have been able to see them. Moreover, inner demons, which were abstract and illusory, could not be touched under normal circumstances.

At this time, it was time for the five magical treasures that Senior White had given him to show their worth.

Song Shuhang used the five magical treasures to capture the inner demon in mid-air. Out of the five magical treasures, two of them worked.

The silk bag and that simple pot could both contain the inner demon.

Song Shuhang thought for a moment and chose the bag. He returned the remaining four magical treasures to Senior White’s clone.

The soft silk bag was much more suited for what he was planning to do.

“Now, time to try out the first plan.”

Song Shuhang pressed the bag containing the inner demon onto the chopping board and attempted to process the invisible inner demon through the bag.

After a while, plan one failed.

The volume of the inner demon in the bag had also shrunk slightly.

“Time for plan two. I hope that this inner demon won’t be consumed before I finish processing it,” Song Shuhang said.

Sixteen thought for a while, then turned to Senior White and said, “Senior White, we thought of a total of seven plans a while ago, which one do you think is the best?”

Senior White’s clone said, “Huh? I was in a daze before, so I didn’t hear any of them.”

Sixteen said, “Senior White can pick any number you want.”

“Wonderful!” Song Shuhang praised.

Sixteen is really resourceful.

Senior White said, “Then how about... six?”

“Understood. I’m skipping straight to plan six.” Song Shuhang began using the sixth plan they had thought up for the inner demon materialization.

Soon enough, the inner demon in the bag materialized successfully.

Great!

Next, it’s time to slice this inner demon up and prepare the seasoning.

After that, all I need to do is to summon Senior Ruler of Shadows using the little cup...

Senior White asked, “Did it work?”

“Yup,” said Song Shuhang with a laugh. He stretched out his hand and pressed it down on the bag; the inner demon inside the bag began squirming around.

“Can you open it up and let us see what this inner demon looks like?” the black Scarlet Heaven Sword asked curiously—normally, inner demons did not have a fixed form as they were ever-changing.

However, since the inner demon had now materialized, it should have a pshysical form.

Was it going to take the form of what the cultivator was most afraid of? If so, then would Young Master Hai’s inner demon be... Song Shuhang?

If an inner demon that looked just like him came out of the bag, would Song Shuhang still be able to cut it into slices?

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword began to look forward to the next few moments.

Sixteen, Senior White, Sister White Dragon, and the others all came closer, also curious.

Song Shuhang said, “When I used the sixth plan to materialize the inner demon, I injected the concept of ‘fish’ into it. Therefore, it should have taken the form of a fish. This way, it will perfectly fit a dish like ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices?.”

After saying that, he stretched out his hand and reached into the silk bag before slowly pulling the inner demon out.

“Fwap~ Fwap~”

It really did look like a big fish. The tail of the fish was constantly flapping around. The inner demon seemed to know the fate that it was about to face and was struggling in the face of death.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said with some disappointment, “It really is just a fish...”

In the end, it was also an inner demon. How could seeing its brethren face such an unfortunate fate make it happy?

While it was still dwelling in its thoughts, Song Shuhang had already exerted some force with his right, dragging the big fish halfway out of the bag.

But then, a small waist appeared before everyone’s eyes.

Song Shuhang’s arm stiffened when he caught sight of this.

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “A mermaid?”

Song Shuhang said doubtfully, “Strange. When I was making it materialize, I injected the concept of an ordinary big fish into it. I didn’t have any thoughts of making it turn into a mermaid.”

Sister White Dragon guessed, “Although this kind of low-level inner demon doesn’t have much intelligence, it can still do some things instinctively. As an inner demon, it should have perceived the thoughts of the surrounding creatures. By using its innate talents, it combined these thoughts and assumed the form of a mermaid.”

In a way, it was similar to the protective coloring of a chameleon. The inner demon had changed itself according to the surrounding environment.

“If it is in the form of a mermaid, slicing it will be a bit more difficult,” said Song Shuhang. After all, ordinary people would have some psychological barriers when faced with something humanoid.

If he really could not bring himself to do it, he would have it take another shape.

Song Shuhang pulled the mermaid inner demon out of the bag. He wanted to see what the inner demon had turned into.

Above the inner demon’s waist was a mini human body. Perhaps due to the inner demon being too weak, it had not been able to emulate the gender of the human it had taken as a reference. Therefore, the human body reminded one of that of a genderless mannequin.

However, what surprised everyone was its head.

The inner demon had copied Senior White’s head.

It was a merman version of Senior White!

It was absolutely flawless in terms of appearance.

Song Shuhang: “...”

Sixteen: “...”

Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

Sister White Dragon smiled and said, “It can be said that this inner demon’s will to survive is very strong.”

If one were to ponder its actions, it had actually made a very reasonable choice.

Among the many characters at the scene, it was by taking from Sage White’s looks that it would be able to minimize its chance of dying.

True Monarch White Crane could not help but say, “Shuhang, sell it to me!”

“It isn’t for sale.” Senior White’s clone rejected True Monarch White Crane’s request.

Afterward, he reached out his hand to Song Shuhang and said, “Shuhang, lend me your phone.”

Song Shuhang unlocked his phone and handed it over to Senior White.

Senior White took several pictures of this Merman White. Then, he opened Song Shuhang’s chat software and sent the photos he took to Soft Feather.

Song Shuhang was stunned the entire time.

It was an absolutely shocking scene to see.

He even began to doubt whether Senior White’s clone had been swapped out at some point.

“Good,” Senior White’s clone said calmly. “This way, the next clone will suffer for sure.”

“...” Song Shuhang asked, “Senior White, are you okay? Is it possible that you’re tired and need some rest?”

Senior White’s clone replied, “I’m fine. It’s just that I don’t have much energy left, and my head feels a little dizzy. It’s like when you drink too much and get light-headed, but this feeling does feel quite good.”

Following that, he grabbed a kitchen knife and cut down the Merman White with a single slash.

Merman White was cut right at the middle.

If it had been someone else, they would have probably hesitated when faced with the Merman White, but Senior White’s clone was not so soft-hearted. He did not hesitate to backstab his main body and the next clone that was to come.

But even after being cut into two, the inner demon did not die.

Instead, its severed upper body began to transform wildly.

It transformed into Su Clan’s Sixteen.

Senior White’s clone did not hesitate in the slightest to slice it once again.

It then transformed to Soft Feather.

Senior White’s clone still showed no mercy.

It then transformed into the virtuous lamia, Fairy Creation, Sister White Dragon, True Monarch White Crane, and Song Shuhang one after the other.

But none of them worked.

“If you were to turn into a normal fish, I would not feel any sense of accomplishment from cutting you. The more you change into other people’s appearance, the more fun it is for me to slice you apart,” murmured Senior White’s clone.

While saying that, he cut the inner demon’s upper body in half once more.

The inner demon seemed to understand Senior White’s words, or perhaps it had inferred the meaning of Senior White’s words after sensing his thoughts.

A moment later, it transformed into a normal fish... And with that, it had used up its remaining bit of energy.

Senior White said, “It really turned into a fish.”

Senior White stretched out his hand and handed both the fish and the knife to Song Shuhang. “I’ll leave the rest to you.”

“Okay!” Song Shuhang took the kitchen knife, activated his demonic chef heart, and extracted the Demon Emperor’s cooking experience and insights from his memories.

His spiritual energy wrapped around the kitchen knife along with a strand of saber intent.

Then, he urged the power of the demonic chef heart to its full capabilities.

Bright lights flashed as Shuhang swung the knife around. Each one of his swings contained the power of the chef heart and saber intent; what he was doing was not merely some simple slicing.

In the blink of an eye, the fish-like inner demon was cut into neat slices and placed onto a plate.

And that was the end for the inner demon.

Song Shuhang wiped his hands, and then prepared the sauce according to Demon Emperor Hezhi’s menu. When he browsed his memory, he discovered that he could make use of some of the leftover ingredients from when he made the ?Braised Heavenly Tribulation?.

He asked, “Who wants to be the first to taste the ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices??”

This time, nobody went up to take Song Shuhang on his offer. Instead, all of their gazes moved to look at the small black cup that Song Shuhang had brought out.

Unlike the ?Braised Heavenly Tribulation?, when they saw this inner demon sashimi, they all felt that it would be for the better to look for someone else to try it out first.

It was an inner demon, after all.

The ?Braised Heavenly Tribulation? had gone through several complicated steps; it was fragrant, and the smell made people drool when it was finished. On the other hand, the inner demon had been sliced raw, so they were worried about suffering adverse reactions when consuming it.

True Monarch White Crane said, “If possible, it would be better to smoke the inner demon to make it more appetizing.”

“Time is tight. We don’t have the time to smoke the inner demon,” Song Shuhang replied.

Sixteen said, “Then let’s wait for Senior Ruler of Shadows to come over and have a taste of it first.”

Song Shuhang grabbed the little black cup and began to summon the Ruler of Shadows.

Shortly after the signal was sent, a bucket-sized spatial gate appeared above the small black cup. Then, dark shadows drilled out of the spatial gate, filling the entire Inner Demon Cave in the blink of an eye.

The Ruler of Shadows said, “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, we meet again.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Yes, Senior, we meet again. The space where I summoned Senior this time is rather small, would you like to go out to have a talk?”

After being covered by the body of the Ruler of Shadows, the entire Inner Demon Cave had become pitch black.

The Ruler of Shadows said with a smile, “This space is indeed too small. Next time, please summon me in a wider place. After all, my body is very large, and it is uncomfortable when I’m in such a tight space.”

After saying that, most of its shadows began to withdraw into the spatial gate, revealing only enough of itself to cover half of the Inner Demon Cave.

This big shot who had a soft spot for the dishes of the ?Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet? had surprisingly a very approachable personality.

“Oh, this is the scholarly faction. No wonder I felt uncomfortable. The attributes of the scholarly faction are opposite to mine.” The Ruler of Shadows then asked with a smile, “Anyway, seeing as Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song has summoned me, have you made a new dish for me to try out?”

Song Shuhang nodded and replied, “This is the ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices?. Senior, please taste it. Also, the repice I got was missing the steps to materialize the inner demon, so the taste might be different from the original one.”

“Is this ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices? of yours another modified dish?” The Ruler of Shadows laughed and said, “I like the ?Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet?, and I also like innovation. As long as the modifications are positive, and the dish tastes better than the original or has its own specialty, I have no problems with it.”

Song Shuhang handed over a plate of sashimi slices and served it along with three different sauces.

The Ruler of Shadows condensed five arms, two of which took the plate, one of which took the sauces, and the last two holding onto a knife and fork.

Under the gaze of Song Shuhang and the others, the Ruler of Shadows tasted one of the slices of Inner Demon Sashimi.

After a short while, the Ruler of Shadows said in a voice filled with satisfaction, “Mm, the taste is beyond my expectations. It tastes delicious.”

While saying that, he tried the three flavors of sauce.

“Senior, how does its taste compare to the original?” Song Shuhang tried asking. He wanted to know how effective the sixth plan that he discussed with the others was.

The Ruler of Shadows said, “How should I say this... There is absolutely no comparison.”

Song Shuhang: “?”

Was the version I made that bad?

“The ingredients are completely different,” said the Ruler of Shadows. “I was wondering why you were talking about inner demon materialization earlier. Now, it seems you directly turned the inner demon into an ingredient. Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, this is the first time I’ve seen such a technique. You were able to draw the inner demon out of a cultivator’s body, materialize it, and then slice it apart to make a dish. If you master this technique, I’m afraid that cultivators all over the universe would be frantically making requests to you.”

Sixteen immediately understood the meaning behind the Ruler of Shadows’ words. “Senior, are you saying that an inner demon tribulation was used for the original ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices??”

The Ruler of Shadows said slowly, “Yes. Although I don’t know how the fellow daoist who created the ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices? did it, he did seal the inner demon tribulation of a cultivator who was transcending their tribulation. During the inner demon tribulation, there is a short period of time in which the inner demon materializes.”

Song Shuhang said, disappointed, “So I failed.”

The Ruler of Shadows said, “Given our previous agreement, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song has indeed failed this time. You did not make the ?Inner Demon Tribulation Sashimi Slices?. However, this ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices? of yours happened to satisfy my appetite. So, I’ll still allow you to request something from me. Of course, the value you’ll get out of it is not equal to a dish of the ?Heavenly Tribulation Grand Banquet?.”

Then, he added, “One more thing, I do not recommend you to directly consume this version of the ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices?. These are the slices of a pure inner demon, and it is not good for your body when you consume them directly.”

“Hm... It’s delicious.” While the Ruler of Shadows was saying that, Senior White’s voice came from the side.

Song Shuhang hurriedly turned his head. “Senior White, don’t eat that! These ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices? are not suitable for us to eat.”

The Ruler of Shadows laughed and said, “Sage White’s body is a clone, right? If it is a clone, then it’s fine to have a taste of it. It won’t hurt the main body anyway.”

Hearing this, Song Shuhang let out a sigh of relief.

“So, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song, is there anything you want?” the Ruler of Shadows asked while eating.

Song Shuhang said, “Yes. In fact, I summoned Senior because I needed to ask you something.”

The Ruler of Shadows said, “Fellow Daoist, please speak.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Is Senior interested in fighting the Heavenly Emperor?”

The Ruler of Shadows replied, “This is not an equivalent exchange, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song. Although the Heavenly Emperor has yet to recover her strength, if I attack her, I’ll have to deal with many troubles in the future. Moreover, if I take action against the Heavenly Emperor now, it will imply that I am someone who takes advantage of others while they’re in a weakened state. If I really have to fight her, it would only be after she returns to her peak.”

The pride and confidence of a powerhouse exuded from the Ruler of Shadows.

“However, I can lend Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song an interesting item. Since we’re in the scholarly faction, this item should work quite well. This item is very precious, and when Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song uses it, the effects will by no means be lackluster,” said the Ruler of Shadows.

Song Shuhang asked, “Precious... How much is it worth?”

The Ruler of Shadows replied, “Hm, converted into Eighth Stage or Ninth Stage spirit stones, it should be enough to exchange for a small mountain of them.”

Doesn’t that mean that it’s a treasure of the same level as the virtuous lamia’s flat imperial hat? As long as the flat imperial hat has sufficient energy, the virtuous lamia can exert combat power at the level of the Ninth Stage!

The Ruler of Shadows handed over a bracelet. “Its name is Shadow Sanctum. It can draw out the obsession left by a powerhouse in a certain place, and transform that obsession into a shadow clone. The stronger the powerhouse, the stronger the obsession they are likely to have left behind, thereby increasing the power that Shadow Sanctum is able to display. We’re in the scholarly faction, a place where the Scholarly Sage and the 13 Tribulation Transcenders of the scholarly faction once lived. I can sense that there’s a lot of residual obsession left here that has yet to be consumed. If you activate the item, I can assure you that its effects will not disappoint you.”

Sister White Dragon asked, “Is this Fellow Daoist Shadow’s path?”

The Ruler of Shadows replied, “Of course not.”

Sister White Dragon said, “Oh, I was just asking casually.”

Song Shuhang squeezed the bracelet and said, “What if the ‘obsession’ that was left in this area isn’t activated?”

“As long as you use it, there will definitely be ‘obsession’ that is activated,” said the Ruler of Shadows. “But how strong that activated ‘obsession’ is depends on you.”

Song Shuhang nodded and looked at Senior White. “Senior White, how about you do another divination for me?”

Senior White’s clone turned around and an expression of confusion was visible on his face.

His deadpan face actually showed an expression!

Song Shuhang asked hurriedly, “Senior White, are you really okay?”

Senior White rubbed his temples and said, “Eating the ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices? had a certain effect on me, a rather hallucinogenic effect. Earlier, my body was slightly empty due to the lack of energy, but after eating the ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices?, I felt like floating. Initially, it only felt like I was tipsy, but now it feels like I’m completely drunk.”

“Senior White, let me help you.” True Monarch White Crane took the opportunity to step forward and support Senior White.

Rumble!

At that moment, there was thunderous rumbling that came from the distance.

The rumbling had come from the collision of powerful forces, and the earth shook as if there was an earthquake.

“The driver uncle and the great master from the Jingang Temple must have run into the Heavenly Emperor’s camp,” explained Sister White Dragon. “Those guys are really crazy.”

Due to the imminent change of the Wielder of the Heaven’s Will, those at the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm and the Immortal Realm had all gone into hiding.

Even if they really wanted to go out and do some activities, they would use various means that would allow them to stay safe when doing so.

They would typically have their body replaced, possess someone or something, or seal their strength.

On the other hand, the Heavenly Emperor’s camp and the driver uncle’s camp, who were in the sky above the scholarly faction, displayed their full strength without reservation.

Song Shuhang said, “Having a battle directly above the scholarly faction should be unfavorable for the driver uncle and the Jingang Temple’s great master.”

Sister White Dragon replied, “They are trying to shift the battlefield elsewhere. They should be moving to some other dimension soon.”

Previously, the Jingang Temple’s great master had mentioned that he excelled in shifting the battlefield to other places.

With his powerful physical strength, combined with the supernatural powers of the Jingang Temple, he should indeed have the ability to forcefully shift the battlefield elsewhere.

Song Shuhang asked, “Has the Heavenly Emperor been taken away?”

Sister White Dragon replied, “Mm-hm, the Heavenly Emperor’s aura has disappeared. She must have been their focus.”

Pavilion Master Chu’s hair emerged from the top of Song Shuhang’s head and said, “I can still sense the aura of an Immortal somewhere close. They’re likely to be someone that the Heavenly Emperor arranged as a backup.”

In the past, the scholarly faction and the Ancient Heavenly City both possessed the power to suppress the entire universe.

However, the way the two forces were established was very different.

The scholarly faction was single-handedly created by the Scholarly Sage. He took in some disciples and trained them until 13 of them became the 13 Tribulation Transcenders of the scholarly faction.

On the other hand, the Heavenly Emperor had gathered a group of like-minded companions at the Immortal level to establish the Heavenly City. Then, they recruited powerful people from all over the universe, making them join the city.

After losing the Sage, the scholarly faction suffered greatly in terms of the number of Immortals they could count on.

Pavilion Master Chu continued, “After both the Heavenly Emperor’s and driver uncle’s camp moved to another battlefield, the scholarly faction has lost their top experts. If that hidden Immortal makes a move now, they can easily take away all the Heavenly City Fragments in the scholarly faction, unless the scholarly faction has some tricks up its sleeve.”

During the several calamities that the scholarly faction had faced, most of its 13 Tribulation Transcenders were either killed or severely injured. Anyway, some of them still lived as felling a Tribulation Transcender was no easy task. If there were three or four of them who were still alive to this day, then with the talent and aptitude that they had, there was a high chance that they had already stepped onto their own path, becoming Immortals a long time ago.

If there were any of the 13 Tribulation Transcenders hidden among the disciples of the scholarly faction, then there was nothing to worry about when it came to the raiding conducted by the Heavenly City.

Song Shuhang thought for a while and said, “I’ll ask Senior Eternal Fire to send people over. We have to hurry up and transfer the Heavenly City Fragments to the world of the golden lotus. We should transport as much as we can at the fastest speed.”

As long as they entered the world of the golden lotus, it would not be so easy for the Heavenly Emperor to recover the fragments.

He quickly sent a message to Senior Eternal Fire as they needed all the time they could get.

“I have some bad news,” said Pavilion Master Chu slowly. “Chu Two has sent me a message. She was able to take care of the demonic bear and some of its companions by using her Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion, but the demonic bear has other companions who are heading over to the scholarly faction with their forces as we speak.”

Song Shuhang touched the Sage’s eye in his left eye socket and looked at the Ruler of Shadows. “Senior, how do I activate Shadow Sanctum?”

“Just pour your spiritual energy into it. In addition, if you have enough time, you can look for the place with the strongest obsession in the scholarly faction and activate Shadow Sanctum there. It’s best to perform some rituals that can enhance your luck before activating it,” replied the Ruler of Shadows.

Song Shuhang asked, “Would that allow me to display its effect to the fullest?”

The Ruler of Shadows replied, “Extra luck always helps, especially if you’re someone with not-so-good luck.”

Song Shuhang sighed, hoping that the Sage’s eye could enhance the power of the obsession. “It seems I’ll have to postpone my fight with the Heavenly Emperor.”

If Shadow Sanctum could play a significant role, then it would be best to save it for the incoming evil demons of the Netherworld.

[No Tyrannical Song, Buzzz~ No Tyrannical Song, please reply when you receive this message.] All of a sudden, the electronic voice of Little Sun ‘You’re Busy T233’ sounded in Song Shuhang’s ears.

However, the signal seemed to be a little choppy as its voice was rather difficult to hear.

Song Shuhang replied, [I’m here.]

The Little Sun said, [No Tyrannical Song, my master is asking you: Where are you right now?]

Song Shuhang replied, [I am in the scholarly faction.]

[Buzzzz, sure enough. Please be careful, the scholarly faction’s signal has some obstructions,] said the Little Sun said. [In addition, the fat ball is on its way to the main world, so prepare yourself mentally.]

Song Shuhang asked, [The fat ball is coming too? Doesn’t it still need some more time?]

Little Sun replied, [According to the data we gathered, the fat ball has received some critical information from its subordinates and changed its plans. The information involved the scholarly faction. Please be careful.]

Could it be because of the demonic bear?

Song Shuhang had a terrible headache as he learned of this new information.

The only thing that he could be thankful for at the moment was that the fat ball had Senior White Two constantly watching it.

Although its strength was the highest among Song Shuhang’s ‘list of people he least wanted to meet’, since Senior White Two did not allow the fat ball to bully the weak, it did not have much of a direct threat to Shuhang.

Song Shuhang said, “Pavilion Master Chu, please find a way to notify Chu Two to be more careful. The boss of the demonic bear is going to be making a move. The level of danger just skyrocketed.”

For some reason, he felt especially insecure today.

He turned his head down and looked at Shadow Sanctum, touching the Sage’s eye in his left eye socket. Suddenly, a bold thought appeared in his mind.

Could there be any obsession left by the Scholarly Sage in the scholarly faction? If there is, then can I make use of it?

For example, he could try throwing Senior Skylark’s head over at a place where the Scholarly Sage’s obsession was relatively stronger.

He could also add Fairy Creation to the mix to strengthen the effect.

If he did all that, there was a chance he might ignite the Scholarly Sage’s obsession.

If this bold plan worked, as long as the power of the Scholarly Sage lasted for a decent time, Shuhang might be able to play a key role during this event.

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior Ruler of Shadows, after this Shadow Sanctum is activated, how long can it last?”

The Ruler of Shadows replied, “It depends on the number of obsessions you activate. The quality of the obsession is related to the amount of power that can be exerted after activating Shadow Sanctum. If the quality is about the same, the number of the obsession is what determines the amount of time the technique can work.”

Song Shuhang nodded, “I see. I’m going to take a walk around the scholarly faction and have a look at the area with the strongest obsession.”

With evil demons of the Netherworld, the Heavenly Emperor, and the fat ball appearing one after the other, it would do him good to be ready to ignite those obsessions before the enemy appeared.

Sixteen said, “Shuhang, do you know how to sense obsessions?”

The hand that Song Shuhang was using to hold Shadow Sanctum froze—Right, how do I sense obsessions?

He turned his head to look at the Ruler of Shadows and asked, “Senior, how can I sense obsessions?”

“There are several methods that you can use. One of these methods is to infer the location through historical records. If you want to summon a certain big shot, you can look through historical records and check where they stayed most of the time, and where major events related to them took place. Through this method, we can speculate the locations of the obsession of that big shot. However, this can only speculate approximate locations. In addition, such history is recorded by people, and that means that it is very likely to have errors,” said the Ruler of Shadows.

Song Shuhang nodded. “What are the other methods?”

The Ruler of Shadows said, “Another method is to find someone who is born with the talent to sense obsessions and ask them for help.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

The Ruler of Shadows said, “And another method that you can use is to use a set of magical techniques I have called ?Obsession True Sight?. By using this magical technique, the obsessions would look like flames to your eyes. The place where the flames are denser is where the obsession is most concentrated in both quality and quantity.”

Song Shuhang’s eyes shone brightly.

That’s perfect!

“However, that is a secret technique of mine, so I don’t intend on spreading it around,” the Ruler of Shadows added. “It’s useless no matter how bright your eyes shine.”

Song Shuhang: “...”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword suggested, “Fellow Daoist Ruler of Shadows, how about you take him in as your adoptive son?”

The Ruler of Shadows replied decisively, “No.”

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword turned to Song Shuhang and said, “There’s only so much I can do to help you.”

Song Shuhang sighed and said, “In other words, I can only use the first option.”

“Actually, there is still another option,” Senior White’s clone said. “Fellow Daoist Shadow, do you have the time to help us check where the flames of obsession burn the strongest in the scholarly faction?”

After the Ruler of Shadows gave Song Shuhang the treasure, he had not immediately left for the Shadow Realm, and had instead stayed behind to watch how things played out. Since that was the case, it would be reasonable to think that he might have the intention to help them out.

Anyway, it was just a matter of asking. Asking a question did not cost any money, at least not in this case.

“No problem,” the Ruler of Shadows said happily. He then turned to Song Shuhang and said, “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, your mind is not nimble enough, and your face is not thick enough.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword hurriedly said, “No, no, the thickness of his face is just right. Anyway, it’s not that his mind isn’t nimble enough, rather that he’s slightly overcautious toward a big senior like you.”

Song Shuhang’s way of thinking had already become one with that of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, and it was very jumpy.

When chatting with him, it was almost certain that the topic would stray from its original path and there was no knowing where the discussion would end up.

If he continued like this, his way of thinking would soon become something similar to Sage White’s or Soft Feather’s, and that was honestly not that favorable.

The Ruler of Shadows asked curiously, “Am I too intimidating? I honestly think that I’m a rather kind and gentle senior.”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “It’s exactly because you’re kind that Tyrannical Song is much more cautious towards you.”

If you were a hostile Immortal-level senior, Song Shuhang would have long since started bothering you like a nasty flea, not showing any of the reluctance he’s showing right now.

“Is that so? I actually like Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s character.” The Ruler of Shadows laughed and said, “Anyway, let me see where obsession is the strongest here in the scholarly faction.”

After saying that, a portion of the Ruler of Shadows’ body floated out of the Inner Demon Cave before activating the ?Obsession True Sight? and taking a look around the entire scholarly faction.

The Ruler of Shadows said, “I’ve found the place where the flames of obsession are burning the brightest. It’s an area on the eastern edge of the scholarly faction, inside a large rift valley. It’s quite an unexpected location. I initially thought that the flames of obsession would be most concentrated in places such as the residences of the 13 Tribulation Transcenders or the Scholarly Sage. I did not expect that it would instead be this inconspicuous location.”

Song Shuhang replied, “A large rift valley on the eastern edge of the scholarly faction... Understood. Thank you, Senior, I’ll be heading there right away.”

The Ruler of Shadows said, “No problem. Right, if none of you are going to be eating these ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices?, I’ll finish them.”

“Feel free to do so, Fellow Daoist,” Senior White’s clone said. “We can’t eat them anyway.”

Could the main reason as to why the Ruler of Shadows stayed behind be these ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices??

??????

Song Shuhang flew on his saber and rushed eastward.

Sixteen, Senior White, and True Monarch White Crane followed right behind him.

Soon enough, they found themselves in a large rift valley.

Sixteen looked around and said, “It feels as if someone cut out this rift valley using a saber or their palm.”

Song Shuhang said, “Perhaps these are the signs of a battle that the Scholarly Sage had with someone. However, who could have fought the Scholarly Sage for him to have left such a powerful obsession behind?”

Senior White asked, “How do you intend to proceed?”

Song Shuhang replied, “Senior White, I would like you to stand by my side to support me. Sister White Dragon and Sixteen, please take care; there may be a giant turtle of disaster that will be appearing shortly.”

“Alright,” Sixteen said.

Song Shuhang took a deep breath and mumbled something at Senior White.

After doing that, he brought out an incomplete head of Senior Skylark from his Inner World.

Fairy Creation held Skylark’s head and followed Song Shuhang’s instructions, heading to the center of the large rift valley.

True Monarch White Crane: “!!!”

Why does Song Shuhang have Senior Skylark’s head in his hands?

When Skylark’s head appeared, the temperature in this large rift valley suddenly rose.

Has the obsession been successfully drawn over?

“Sage’s obsession, ignite!” Song Shuhang took this opportunity to activate Shadow Sanctum.

Inside the Inner Demon Cave.

The portion of the Ruler of Shadow’s body that was still in the cave had condensed six human-like arms and sat at the entrance of the cave.

Using his six hands, he held a plate of ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices?, savoring it with gusto.

While Song Shuhang was activating the obsessions in the scholarly faction, the Ruler of Shadows raised its head and glanced toward the large rift valley with interest.

“What a powerful obsession, and he had actually been able to activate it in a single breath. As expected of the first Sage in a thousand years; Profound Sage Tyrannical Song’s means are indeed remarkable. However, the power generated by such a powerful obsession is not something that the body of an ordinary Eighth Stage Profound Sage can withstand... Well, I did remind him discreetly, he should have noticed, right? I pointed out that the quality of the obsession is directly related to the time it can be summoned. As the first Sage in a thousand years, he should at least have this level of understanding, right?” The Ruler of Shadows picked up a piece of sashimi with a fork, poured the sauce onto it, and stuffed it into his mouth, chewing it slowly.

Although it isn’t the ?Inner Demon Tribulation Sashimi Slices?, this ?Inner Demon Sashimi Slices? is very original and has a novel taste. If Profound Sage Tyrannical Song is able to neutralize the negative influence that this dish has on cultivators, it might become a better dish than the ?Inner Demon Tribulation Sashimi Slices?.

I truly hope that Profound Sage Tyrannical Song can advance further as an immortal chef.

Whether it’s the ?Braised Heavenly Tribulation? or the ?Inner Demon Tribulation Sashimi Slices?, he’s been able to make a different version of them; he’s very talented in cooking the heavenly tribulation.

??????

Meanwhile in the large rift valley.

Although he could not see the obsession, Song Shuhang could sense that the temperature in the large rift valley was getting higher and higher. He guessed that it should be because the Scholarly Sage’s flame of obsession had been ignited.

He began to activate Shadow Sanctum. “Fairy Creation, come back. The giant turtle of disaster is about to appear.”

After Fairy Creation put down Skylark’s head, she raised both of her hands above her head, stood on the tips of her toes, and then swan-danced all the way back to Song Shuhang.

The dance was beautiful, pleasing to the eye, and simply amazing to watch!

Just as Fairy Creation’s figure left, a large mouth opened in the air and swallowed Skylark’s head.

After swallowing Skylark’s head, the mouth stopped abruptly.

[God damn it, it’s you again, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song! My father and I were chased down by tentacle monsters for several days the last time you baited us over! Are you trying to trick us again today?] the giant turtle of disaster said in an angry voice. [I’m going to tell my dad to beat you up!]

Song Shuhang: “...”

Heavens, it’s you again? It’s the turtle sister that took off her shell last time.

Why are you always the one appearing no matter where I throw out a part of Skylark?

Is there some fate between us?

Anyway, the father of this turtle sister is very powerful, and it is very likely to be an Immortal-level existence. With the scholarly faction being in the current mess it is, if her father also intervenes... that will make things much worse and much harder to deal with.

“You’re misunderstanding!” Song Shuhang shouted. “I’m not trying to trick you this time, trust me. You can leave after taking back Senior Skylark’s head. I’m trying to summon something else this time.”

The lady giant turtle of disaster roared, [There are no misunderstandings in this world, only wicked fate. Today, my dad is definitely going to be beating the shit out of you—Dad, come here!]

[Dear daughter, can you wait a bit? Daddy will be there in 20 minutes— No, 30 minutes.] A voice sounded from the void. [Can you go into hiding for now? Your parents are trying to make some cute little siblings for you. After half an hour, daddy will make sure to do you justice.]

The lady giant turtle of disaster was left speechless.

Now, everyone knew that her father and mother were making little turtles!

Well, that was awkward.

The lady giant turtle of disaster gnashed her teeth and said, [Just you wait, Profound Sage Tyrannical Song! In half an hour, my dad is definitely going to come over and beat the shit out of you!]

Then, her figure disappeared into the void.

“You really are a sinful man, Tyrannical Song. That was a lady turtle,” the black Scarlet Heaven Sword said with a strange smile.

Song Shuhang: “...”

He could not help but press his hand onto the black Scarlet Heaven Sword and use three instances of the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique?.

“Aaahhh~ So refreshing~” After the familiar cool sensation coursed through its body, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword added, “Actually, if the father of that lady giant turtle of disaster does come over, it might be a good thing. Evil demons of the Netherworld, powerhouses from the Heavenly City, the Heavenly Emperor, and many other guys are going to make an appearance. At that time, if the father of that giant turtle of disaster really does come over and get involved in the chaotic battle, it would be a lot more interesting.”

“That makes sense,” Sister White Dragon said. “If her father comes over, we can just drag him into the battle with some tricks.”

Senior White’s clone asked, ?”Did Shadow Sanctum work?”

“We’ll know in a bit.” Song Shuhang held up Shadow Sanctum.

He could feel that Shadow Sanctum was resonating with the obsession in the rift valley, and was transforming this obsession into a shadow clone.

While holding Shadow Sanctum up high, Song Shuhang used three instances of the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? on it. Probably because he had just used the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? for Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, his hands were feeling a little itchy and had involuntarily slid onto the magical treasure.

“Buzz~”

Shadow Sanctum vibrated excitedly, and after the three instances of the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique?, it displayed its full power.

In the next moment, all the obsession in the large rift valley was mobilized.

It really worked!?Song Shuhang was overjoyed and wanted to use the ?Saber-Nurturing Technique? again.

Fortunately, at the critical moment, his rationality prevailed. Shadow Sanctum was a very precious item, and it could not be stimulated so carelessly. If he broke it, it would be a disaster.

This thought immediately calmed Song Shuhang down.

“Woosh~”

The sound of waves came from Shadow Sanctum’s body.

In the next moment, the shadow clone began to condense.

A huge shadow appeared. It was so big that it covered the entire sky above the scholarly faction.

Sister White Dragon said, “This... doesn’t look like the Sage, does it?”

Although she had not met the Scholarly Sage before, she knew that he was a human.

Song Shuhang looked confused. “If it’s not the Sage, then who is it?”

I brought out Senior Skylark’s head, as well as Fairy Creation, yet I failed to summon the Scholarly Sage?

As soon as his voice faded, the shadow in the sky quickly poured into Song Shuhang’s body.

However, because the shadow was a bit too large, the process lasted for quite a while.

After about five minutes...

“It still isn’t over?” Song Shuhang felt that his body was melting, and he felt that he might even be assimilated by the power of this “shadow”!

At the same time, as this shadow continued to enter his body, information emerged in his mind, allowing him to know whose obsession he had just summoned.

This was the power that belonged to the Indestructible Lord.

The Indestructible Lord, a terrifying existence born in the primordial era.

During the primordial era, the Indestructible Lord fell into an eternal slumber as it had tried to access truths beyond its comprehension. While the Indestructible Lord was slumbering, its demonic thoughts had turned into tentacles, and acted in the place of its will, exploring the laws of eternity.

Song Shuhang had fought the Indestructible Lord before, and he knew all this very well.

After summoning its obsession, Song Shuhang had a bad premonition.

It’s over. Ever since my “decent luck” ran out yesterday, all kinds of bad things have been happening to me.

I’m going to die, am I not?

Actually, it wasn’t too strange that the Indestructible Lord’s obsession was attracted after Senior Skylark’s head was brought out, as the Indestructible Lord’s obsession for eternity was no weaker than the Scholarly Sage’s obsession with Senior Skylark.

What a tragedy.

Even with the protection of Senior White, I wasn’t able to prevent my bad luck from taking over. Just how bad is my luck today?

Song Shuhang’s liver ached.

The shadow of the Indestructible Lord’s obsession was still pouring into his body. If this continued, he would be overwhelmed by the power inside the shadow before Shadow Sanctum could even properly take effect.

Under normal circumstances, if the power of the obsession was a bit too strong, Song Shuhang would have turned on his pseudo-eternity smoke mode before his body exploded.

However, what he summoned this time was the obsession of the Indestructible Lord. Song Shuhang had experienced for himself just how strong the Indestructible Lord’s desire for eternity was, and he did not want to experience it a second time.

Therefore, it was best for him to avoid entering the pseudo-eternity state unless it was absolutely necessary. If not, he might just draw over the demonic heads formed from the demonic will of the Indestructible Lord and cause the situation in the scholarly faction to become even messier.

When his thoughts reached this point, not only was his liver aching, but his stomach also began cramping.

Behind his waist, the black Scarlet Heaven Sword encouraged him, “You got this, Song Shuhang. You can definitely do it. Believe in yourself!”

Song Shuhang gritted his teeth and circulated his three top-tier body-tempering techniques to bear the power of the obsession.

The Holy Apes holding Scholarly Scriptures in their hands began chanting loudly, while the ?Variant Steel Hands Technique? turned Song Shuhang’s skin black. As soon as the three body-tempering techniques began operating, the pressure he was feeling from the obsession pouring into him decreased significantly.

At this time, the virtuous lamia appeared and suddenly began singing, “Believe in yourself, ooh~ You will win and create miracles~ Believe in yourself, ooh~”

The “ooh~” in the song was very magical, and Song Shuhang almost sang along with her.

But after the virtuous lamia sang those few lines, she stopped. She was only playing around a little, and she was strangely reliable when it came to life and death situations.

She stretched out her hand and placed it on Song Shuhang’s body, circulating the ?Dual System Virtue Technique? to relieve some of the pressure on Song Shuhang with the power of virtue.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword remained behind Song Shuhang’s waist. It could not relieve the pressure on Song Shuhang like the virtuous lamia, but what it could do was absorb and store the power that leaked out of Song Shuhang. As long as it accumulated enough energy, it could also assist Song Shuhang by slashing out a Heaven Burning Flaming Saber like its main body.

At the same time, it added, “Even if you die, you will go out with a bang!”

“Life is as gorgeous as summer flowers, and death is as quiet and beautiful as autumn leaves,” said Pavilion Master Chu’s hair as it swayed in the wind, also silently absorbing some of the power that leaked out.

“Don’t put up flags for me, Seniors.” Song Shuhang concentrated on absorbing the energy, and all of the hairs on his body stood on end. An incomparably vast amount of spiritual energy enveloped him, and the primordial power of the Indestructible Lord came to him from all directions.

Everyone around him got some information from this primordial power. As long as one encountered and managed to experience the power of an Immortal with their body, they would find themselves with some comprehension of it. In particular, when it came to an existence from the primordial era like the Indestructible Lord, they would come in contact with a taboo-like energy.

Senior White’s clone said, “Hm? This energy feels quite familiar.”

Song Shuhang nodded. “We fought this guy on Heavenly Field Island last week. The power of the Indestructible Lord, the wisps of its demonic will turned into the demonic heads, and its obsession turned into tentacles. At that time, a large portion of the demonic heads had been taken down by Senior Creation’s singing... and the obsession of the Indestructible Lord was drawn away by the giant turtle of disaster.”

“Oh, so that’s what it was.” Senior White finally understood why he had felt the energy to be quite familiar.

The main body of the Indestructible Lord was in deep slumber. Its demonic will and obsession had replaced it to collect information about “eternity” across the universe. Then, when they broke into the main world to pursue Skylark, they were destroyed by the Scholarly Sage.

The Sage also left behind a lot of backups, including the voice of Dharma King Creation, which specialized in restraining the Indestructible Lord’s demonic will.

At this moment, the black-skinned Soft Feather said, “Senior Song, your body is breaking.”

Song Shuhang replied, “Ah, I can see that, Soft Feather.”

There were small cracks all over Song Shuhang’s body.

“Sure enough, I still can’t bear this power. If this continues, my body will explode soon.” Song Shuhang waved his hand and opened the Inner World. “Everyone, enter my Inner World and hide. Senior White, do you have a way to transfer me to a remote and uninhabited place? I’m going to activate my smoke mode.”

Senior White’s clone said, “Sure, just give me a few moments.”

Then, he raised his sleeve, revealing his white forearm.

On the arm of Senior White’s clone was a tattoo that looked like a little snake.

Senior White reached out and grabbed the tattoo, removing it with a forceful pull.

He shook it lightly, and the tattoo inflated, turning into a long rope.

Senior White’s clone grasped both ends of the long rope and skillfully turned it into a short, fancy jump rope.

“The embodiment of the Indestructible Lord’s demonic will.” Song Shuhang finally remembered what it was.

This was the fragment of the Indestructible Lord’s demonic will that had parasitized Song Shuhang’s body on Heavenly Field Island. Later on, it had been pulled out by Senior White’s clone and changed from 3D to 2D, and then into a long rope.

“Yup,” Senior White’s clone said. “I placed it on my arm for a few days and purified it thoroughly. Although it is still a wisp of demonic will of the Indestructible Lord, it belongs to me now.”

After saying that, Senior White’s clone threw the wisp of demonic will at Song Shuhang.

The demonic will was like a long snake as it wrapped around Song Shuhang’s neck.

“It won’t burrow into my body again, right?” Song Shuhang already had some trauma from this thing.

Senior White said, “Don’t worry, that won’t happen. It will just stick to you like a tattoo—”

In the next moment, the virtuous fat whale that the lamia was riding jumped up and swallowed the Indestructible Lord’s demonic will in a single go.

Then, it leaned against Song Shuhang’s back, returning to his body.

A tattoo appeared on Song Shuhang’s back.

It was of a huge whale with its mouth open, a snake sticking out of it.

The tattoo actually looked quite good.

As soon as the tattoo appeared, Song Shuhang felt that the connection between him and the obsession above his head had become stronger.

The terrifying power no longer continued to pour into his body. Instead, a black hole condensed above Song Shuhang’s head.

The Indestructible Lord’s obsession had begun to manifest.

The sudden increase in power gave Song Shuhang an illusion of invincibility.

He clenched his fists slightly, wanting to let out an emotional sigh.

The virtuous lamia snatched his line, “Please call me Song ‘Super Awesome’ Shuhang.”

Song Shuhang said, “Can you let me say my line every now and then?”

The virtuous lamia blinked. “Can you let me say my line every now and then?”

The virtuous lamia’s library had been updated again.

Song Shuhang: “...”

At this moment, Sister White Dragon asked, “What are you going to do next?”

Once Shadow Sanctum was activated, the materialized obsession wouldn’t last long.

When the Indestructible Lord’s obsession that had taken possession of—or in this case, attached itself to—Song Shuhang’s body was completely consumed, Shadow Sanctum’s effect would also come to an end.

From this point onward, every minute and every second was very precious to Song Shuhang.

Above Song Shuhang’s head, Pavilion Master Chu’s hair voiced out, “That Immortal has made their move. They are already plundering the Heavenly City Fragments.”

She was like a radar, keeping an eye on everything that was happening in the scholarly faction.

Song Shuhang asked, “Can Sister White Dragon sense who the other party is?”

Intelligence was of the utmost importance in modern warfare.

Sister White Dragon shook her head. “Their aura is concealed very well. Anyway, it shouldn’t be someone I know.”

Song Shuhang pondered for a few seconds and said, “Since the fat ball has yet to arrive, let’s go to meet this Immortal from the Ancient Heavenly City.”

Pavilion Master Chu’s hair said, “You don’t need to go looking for them... They’re coming here.”

When Song Shuhang activated Shadow Sanctum, it caused quite the commotion, so it was natural that other people noticed what was going on.

Soon after, the sky above their heads was torn apart by a pair of black arms.

These black arms were covered with endless demonic energy and red eyes.

“Eh?” Song Shuhang’s heart thumped when he saw this familiar scene.

It’s that Immortal whose arms are covered in eyes.

I remember that he was showing off in front of Striped Dragon Two the last time, even refusing to forgive Cheng Lin... After that, he was caught and locked up in a small black room for a thousand years.

How come he’s out already?

Has Striped Dragon Two become so unreliable?

You shouldn’t change your mind after saying that you were going to lock him up for a thousand years!

No matter what, this Immortal is an enemy who killed your daughter, Empress Cheng Lin, at least once! So why not just imprison him until he dies?

The next time I meet Fairy Cheng Lin, should I tip her off on this Immortal being set free?

Thoughts flashed through Song Shuhang’s mind, with bold ideas appearing one after the other
