“Crack, crack, crack.”

The spatial gate opened, and the Immortal with arms covered with eyes stepped out, glancing around.

The Light Wheel of an Immortal shone brightly behind his head.

The Immortal then crossed his arms and said solemnly, “Are you the trump card that the scholarly faction has prepared to deal with me?”

Song Shuhang felt his eyes hurt when he saw the Immortal’s posture—it wasn’t that he had any problem with someone crossing their arms, but with the Immortal’s arms being covered in eyes, wouldn’t this posture hurt those poor eyes?

Suddenly, the Immortal with arms covered with eyes glared at Song Shuhang, and said through clenched teeth, “It’s you!”

Seeing an old enemy, his eyes became bloodshot.

The virtuous lamia went to protect Song Shuhang like an old hen protecting her chick. She spread her arms wide open, while her beautiful eyes stared at the Immortal with vigilance.

“@#%×,” the Immortal paused slightly before bitterly calling out the virtuous lamia’s name. The bitterness in his tone was very obvious... Even though there was a distance of over a thousand meters between them, the bitterness was still loud and clear.

But if you were to carefully listen to his tone, you would discover that along with the bitterness, there was also a hint of tenderness.

“Are you still going to protect him?” asked the Immortal.

The virtuous lamia blinked, and her red lips parted slightly. “Goddamn it, it’s you again... I’m going to tell my dad to beat you up!”

The Immortal with arms covered with eyes was baffled

In the next moment, he looked at Song Shuhang again. This time, his eyes were even redder.

On the top of Song Shuhang’s head, Pavilion Master Chu’s hair stood upright.

“Shuhang.” Her voice was deep, very deep, and it contained an unresolved resentment.

There had been an inner demon in her body that had stayed with her from the Seventh Stage Realm all the way until she reached the Immortal Realm. Resentment had formed from the destruction of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion, and the pain had been tormenting her ever since... It had only been temporarily stopped when Chu Two had split apart from her.

“Although I don’t know how he got out, I know what must be done,” Song Shuhang said. “Senior Chu, please summon Chu Two back. We can’t let her continue wasting time on those evil demons of the Netherworld.”

She did not need to use words. She directly sent Chu Two the image of the Immortal with arms covered with eyes.

Song Shuhang reached out and unsheathed Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword.

“Swoosh~”

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber issued a phoenix cry as it drilled out of the Inner World, happily landing in Song Shuhang’s left hand.

A saber in the left hand, and a sword in the right.

“I might know what’s going on,” Sister White Dragon said suddenly. “It’s not his main body. It’s more like a clone.”

As an Immortal-level existence, it was not strange for the other party to possess one or two powerful clones.

The main body of the Immortal with arms covered with eyes was probably still locked in Stripe Dragon Two’s small black room. However, this clone could move around freely.

A clone was definitely not as strong as the main body. However, with a special secret technique like one that was used for this clone, it was possible for it to possess combat power at the Immortal level.

Nevertheless, it was also because it was a clone that Sister White Dragon had not recognized its aura previously.

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “Control the power of the Indestructible Lord and use the Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique on him.”

Song Shuhang asked, “Senior, can your body handle it?”

The black Scarlet Heaven Sword replied, “Don’t worry about me. Just go ahead and do it!”

Song Shuhang activated the energy of the Indestructible Lord and poured it into Scarlet Heaven Sword.

He spun his wrist and dark flames erupted from the sword.

Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique—Indestructible Lord Edition.

The flaming saber, powered by the energy of the Indestructible Lord, erupted with different flames from the original version. This flame did not appear to be as domineering as the original version, but it did seem to have several strange attributes and debuffs such as hallucinations, poison, demonic sounds, and so on.

Song Shuhang raised his hand and sent a slash toward the sky.

The Immortal with arms covered with eyes snorted and waved his hands.

As soon as he did that, several rays of light shot out from his arms.

The rays aimed at the black Heaven Burning Flaming Saber.

There was no contest, and the domineering rays of light smashed the black Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique into pieces.

The Immortal said solemnly, “That’s it?”

In the next moment, he began descending from the air.

He wanted to pinch Profound Sage Tyrannical Song to death, just like how he did with Cheng Lin back then.

Song Shuhang chuckled. “Do you really think that was all there was to it?”

The Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique, which had been broken up and annihilated, suddenly took shape again, swallowing the Immortal with arms covered with eyes.

The nature of the Indestructible Lord’s power was like the name suggested, indestructible.

After being neutralized, his attacks would form again and continue to attack. This kind of attack method was very unscientific.

People who did not know the Indestructible Lord could easily be fooled and get killed when fighting him.

The pitch-black Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique struck the body of the Immortal with arms covered with eyes.

The virtuous lamia dubbed the scene for him, “Ahhh~ Ah~”

While screaming, she also threw a few blades of light toward him—each of these attacks of virtue was close to the Seventh Stage in strength.

Although attacks of this level could not even hurt a strand of hair of the Immortal, their emotional damage was immeasurable.

“Keep attacking! The opponent is an Immortal. Even if it’s just a clone, it won’t be easy to kill him,” above his head, Pavilion Master Chu’s hair reminded him.

“I don’t want to stop either, but the techniques I know are limited,” said Song Shuhang with a stifled heart. Then, he used his psychic energy to hold up Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword and pointed his palm toward the place where the Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique had exploded.

?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment?!

He had learned this secret technique of the Jingang Temple only recently.

He had read the text of the secret technique and mastered the theory, but he had never gotten to use it.

But now that the Indestructible Lord’s obsession was attached to his body, information and laws were unceasingly pouring into Song Shuhang’s mind. It was the knowledge he was receiving after being possessed by the Indestructible Lord’s obsession.

In this state, Song Shuhang’s mind was extremely active.

The ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment?, of which he only knew the theory, had become integral part of his arsenal. It was similar, in a way, to when he used Young Master Phoenix Slayer’s CPU.

During this time when he was borrowing the CPU of the Indestructible Lord’s obsession, the saber techniques, sword techniques, magical techniques, and secret techniques he did not know too well—as well as those that he could barely understand—were being revised anew.

In the next moment, a huge Buddha’s palm appeared in the air.

Under the blessing of the Indestructible Lord’s power, this Buddha’s palm came to have an area of ??nearly 100 square meters. When the palm slammed down, it was accompanied by the power of lightning.

Unfortunately, he was in a hurry, and Song Shuhang had been unable to combine the ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? and the ?Lightning Palm?.

“Boom!”

The ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? shot toward the location of the explosion.

Song Shuhang stared at the blast zone using the Scholarly Sage’s eye. The Immortal with arms covered in eyes did not dodge the attack. He was still resisting the inextinguishable fire and saber intent of the Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique.

The ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? landed on his back with perfect timing.

It was a pity that the Impregnating Gaze had no effect on enemies at the Immortal Realm. Otherwise, this would have been the perfect time to add the Impregna— Expert’s Appraisal to the combo!

At the same time, Song Shuhang made a hand seal and shouted, “Five Thunder Strikes!”

“Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom!”

Five thick bolts of lightning were summoned, and under the blessing of the Indestructible Lord’s power, these ordinary-looking lightning bolts came to possess a might beyond the Ninth Stage.

This was also the first time that Song Shuhang had ever used the complete version of the Five Thunder Strikes.

It felt great to be able to use magical techniques!

“Are you underestimating me?!” the Immortal with arms covered in eyes roared angrily. At the same time, the eye on his forehead shone with a vicious light.

The flames, saber intent, and lightning that surrounded him were all dispelled.

Other than the Heaven Burning Flaming Saber Technique at the beginning, all the other techniques that Tyrannical Song had been using were small magical techniques that could not hurt him in the slightest.

“Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom!”

“Sbam!”

The ?Buddha’s Giant Palm of Punishment? and the five lightning bolts that had been dispelled recondensed, attacking the Immortal one more time. However, they still barely did anything to him.

The Immortal let out an enraged roar. He ignored the attacks, moved through space, and appeared in front of Song Shuhang directly.

His pitch-black hands grabbed Song Shuhang’s neck, and the eyes between his palms emitted fifty different kinds of light at the same time.

Those lights could cause petrification, paralysis, weakness, hallucinations, apply curses, and ignore defenses.

A single move that was equivalent to a full set.

Even if it were an Immortal who was grabbed, they would not be able to resist the attack easily.

The Immortal said furiously, “Die, you who are surnamed Song.”

He held Song Shuhang’s neck with both of his hands and raised him up in the air. His strong fingers tightly locked Song Shuhang’s neck in place.

[Wait, isn’t this too easy...]

A strange feeling suddenly welled up in the heart of the Immortal with arms covered in eyes.

During the whole process, Song Shuhang had not resisted, allowing him to grab his neck. It was similar to when he had strangled Cheng Lin back then.

The eyes of Song Shuhang, who was being held by his neck, rolled up.

And then, his body softened like a boiled noodle.

“Ahhh~ Ah~” The virtuous lamia screamed in cooperation.

It’s a fake!

The Immortal threw away Song Shuhang’s body instinctively.

However, while it was easy for him to grab Song Shuhang, the Immortal soon discovered that it was difficult to get rid of him.

Song Shuhang, whose eyes were rolled up, seemed to be glued to his hands. He could not shake him off at all.

“Why are you throwing me away? Weren’t you going to strangle me?” Song Shuhang, who was being swung around like a noodle, suddenly let out a strange sound.

His voice sounded just like what one would make when in the middle of a dream.

“Come on. Strangle me,” the dreamy voice continued. “If you don’t strangle me, I will slice you up!”

“Go to hell.” The Immortal focused on Song Shuhang’s body, and shot all kinds of lights once again.

Song Shuhang, who was stuck to both of his hands, was blown up. His body was shattered by the power of the attack.

However, the flesh and blood that had splattered everywhere seemed to come alive a moment later. It turned into what looked like bloody mud and then crawled over and wrapped around the Immortal’s arms. Shortly after, all of the eyes were covered with flesh and blood.

Soon, Shuhang’s flesh and blood began to corrode the eyes on the Immortal’s arms.

The Immortal launched another attack with his eyes, blasting the flesh and blood apart.

Meanwhile...

In the sky, Song Shuhang’s real body walked out of the black hole formed from the materialized obsession.

At this moment, Song Shuhang was in a wonderful state.

There was a “shell” on his body, which was a combination of the power of the Indestructible Lord’s obsession and the Indestructible Lord’s demonic will that had been purified by Senior White.

With this shell, Song Shuhang could fully exert the energy of the Indestructible Lord’s obsession, and even use some of the secret techniques and skills of the Indestructible Lord.

If he had to describe this state...

It was like playing a VR game. Through this “shell,” he controlled the Immortal-level account of the Indestructible Lord.

That skill he had used just now was called “Declaration of Death,” and it was a substitution-type skill. In addition, only half of the skill had taken effect yet.

Song Shuhang’s real body approached the Immortal, but the other party seemed to be completely oblivious to his presence.

As soon as Song Shuhang arrived next to the Immortal, he swung Scarlet Heaven Sword and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber at him.

Declaration of Death: If you don’t strangle me, I will slice you up.

The Indestructible Lord did as he said. If he said that he would slice you up, he would slice you up. He would absolutely not stab you instead!

The saber and the sword mercilessly slashed down at the Immortal.

Two gashes were left on his body, and copious amounts of blood began gushing out of the wounds. There were dark flames that remained in the wounds, constantly burning him and preventing his wounds from healing.

The Immortal clenched his teeth after receiving the attack, but he did not let out a single sound.

He had a strange feeling. Tyrannical Song was completely different from before, whether it was the power of his attacks or the way he used the laws.

Earlier, it seemed he had been intentionally using those small tricks to draw his ire.

Sure enough, nobody with the surname Song is anything good.

The Immortal with arms covered in eyes issued out a long cry, and a tattoo-like huge eye appeared on his chest.

When this eye appeared, it deciphered the Declaration of Death that Song Shuhang was using, and the Immortal was finally able to see Song Shuhang’s real body.

He turned around to block Song Shuhang’s attack, and a beam of light shot out from the eye on his chest.

“Fwoosh~”

Above Song Shuhang’s head, energy came pouring out from the black hole, and a giant shell condensed around Shuhang. This shell easily blocked the light. This was the Indestructible Lord’s powerful defensive skill, Giant King’s Robe.

Unfortunately, both Declaration of Death and Giant King’s Robe were moves unique to the Indestructible Lord’s obsession. As such, Song Shuhang could not learn them himself. Once the obsession was consumed, he would no longer be able to use these skills.

Song Shuhang, who was on the defensive, glanced at the tattoo-like eye on the chest of the Immortal. “Nipple-beams sure are dangerous.”

The Immortal with arms covered in eyes said calmly, “Wrong, this eye grew in the middle of my chest.”

Then, he placed his hands together and pushed them toward Song Shuhang, a terrifying rune condensing from the two eyes in the middle of his palms. The destructive power contained in this rune was enough to wipe the scholarly faction off of the earth.

This attack is something that Tyrannical Song has no choice but to block. Otherwise, everyone below in the scholarly faction will perish!

At this moment, Song Shuhang called out calmly, “You’re finally here.”

A girl’s voice sounded. “Yes, I’m here.”

The Immortal with arms covered in eyes froze.

Behind him, a black-haired girl had appeared. She was barefoot as she stood in the air, and a jewel was hanging from her waist.

Then, the world changed.

A world with an ancient architectural style appeared, sucking him and Tyrannical Song into it.

This was the world of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion.

The Immortal with arms covered in eyes looked at Pavilion Master Chu, and his heart suddenly thumped. “It’s you.”

“Yes, it’s me,” replied Pavilion Master Chu Two slowly.

“This is just a clone. Let’s kill him quickly,” Song Shuhang said. “I’m very tight on time. I’m consuming a large amount of energy every second.”

Although it was only a clone, it could ease the anger in Pavilion Master Chu and Chu Two by a little bit.

Then, Song Shuhang made his move.

A sword in his left hand, and a saber in the right one. He attacked with both at the same time.

Moreover, he was not using some ordinary techniques when he attacked. By taking advantage of the Indestructible Lord’s huge library of skills, he could choose from a plethora of sword-saber combination secret techniques.

Song Shuhang wished that he used his brain to copy these skills... Unfortunately, some dreams were bound to remain dreams.

When he unleashed one of the secret techniques, the projection of a woman appeared on Song Shuhang’s left, supporting Scarlet Heaven Sword, while the projection of a man appeared on his right, supporting the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

Song Shuhang merely waved his hands, and the projections rushed forward in unison.

The man and the woman each used a sword technique and a saber technique that contained the laws of the Great Way. When they attacked in unison, the might of the attack increased by four times. In addition, Scarlet Heaven Sword and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber were both top-notch divine weapons, which only served to add to the power of the combo.

The Immortal with arms covered in eyes wanted to dodge, but he was already caught in the domain of the sword-saber attack. No matter where he ran to, he would still be slashed by the attack.

He wanted to escape by using his spatial abilities, but this was the world of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion, and the space had long since been blocked. The only way he would be able to use his spatial abilities to escape was if he managed to break the spatial blockade of Pavilion Master Chu Two.

“Heavenly City’s Immortal Beheading Flag!” All of the eyes on the Immortal’s body shot out rays of light, which then converged to resist the combined strike of the sword and the saber. At the same time, a magical treasure appeared in his hand.

This flag was a treasure that his main body possessed during the era of the Ancient Heavenly City.

As the Immortal waved the battle flag, his body turned into a blinding light that shot straight through the attack, heading toward Song Shuhang.

As the Immortal shot through the attack, the sword and saber attack left nearly a hundred bloody wounds on his body. During that instant, most of the eyes on his arms had also been slashed.

However, he continued to rush straight for Song Shuhang before fiercely slamming down the immortal beheading flag in his hand.

Song Shuhang said, “Haha, it’s good that you’ve come closer.”

The Giant King’s Robe had yet to expire, and the sleeves of the robe rose to block the attack.

“Clang!”

During a confrontation between Immortals, terrifying energy fluctuations would scatter in all directions. If they were in the main world, the shock wave would have been enough to flatten the scholarly faction.

Fortunately, Pavilion Master Chu Two had summoned the world of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion.

Space was blocked, and Pavilion Master Chu Two was also present, so the shock waves were limited to an area of ten meters around them.

However, in this manner, the shock waves became even more violent.

“Crack, crack, crack~”

The defenses of the Giant King’s Robe started to break down.

Song Shuhang manipulated the shell around him to welcome the attack of the Immortal, unleashing the might of the Indestructible Lord to the greatest extent.

The two fought frantically at close quarters. In the blink of an eye, they had nearly exchanged a thousand blows.

Countless secret techniques, innate abilities, magical techniques, curses, and martial arts were used, targeting the enemy’s body, soul, mind, and will.

Immortal-level attacks were very varied as these powerhouses were proficient in countless fields.

??????

This was the coolest fight that Song Shuhang had ever participated in.

It could be seen from this fight just how terrifying and powerful the Indestructible Lord was.

Despite there being only a remnant of his obsession in the scholarly faction, once it was materialized by Shadow Sanctum, it allowed Song Shuhang to possess the power to confront an Immortal.

If the real body of the Indestructible Lord were to appear, it was unimaginable what kind of power it could unleash...

The clone of the Immortal and Song Shuhang fought to a stalemate.

The space around them began to distort as they continued to fight, and the spatial blockade arranged by Pavilion Master Chu Two was gradually collapsing.

To be honest, Pavilion Master Chu Two really did not expect Song Shuhang to be able to accomplish such a feat. He was fighting head-on with the clone of an Immortal without falling into a disadvantage, and he was even faintly suppressing the other party.

“Surnamed Song, die!” Suddenly, the Immortal seized an opportunity.

The battle flag got past Song Shuhang’s sword-saber defense, stabbing violently toward his stomach.

This was the end.

Song Shuhang suffered from a lack of combat experience, especially when it came to battles at the Immortal level. While he might be fine for a short while, more and more flaws would appear as time passed.

“Rip!”

Then, the sound of a spear stabbing into the flesh echoed.

The Immortal, who was firmly holding onto the battle flag, lowered his head slightly.

In his abdomen, he saw the tip of a spear glowing with a seven-colored light

The colorful spear tip was, in truth, the tip of his Immortal Beheading Flag!

However, he could remember stabbing the flag toward the young man surnamed Song, so how did it end up in his own stomach?

“Are you surprised?” Song Shuhang said. “Hehe, I won’t be explaining what happened to you, though.”

I’ll just let you waste your brain cells trying to figure out what happened!

And more importantly... Song Shuhang, himself, did not know the principles behind that move of the Indestructible Lord.

The Immortal with arms covered in eyes firmly gripped the battle flag and pulled it out. With that, the spear tip that had pierced into his abdomen was removed. Now, the Immortal Beheading Flag was tainted with the blood of an Immortal, and it was his own blood.

The Immortal yelled, “Karma— Ah!”

Before he could finish, another spear had pierced through his stomach.

It was a colorful spear tip once again, and the tip of the spear was dyed with Immortal blood. It was a very familiar scene.

Agonizing pain that even an Immortal would be unable to endure was transmitted from his abdomen to his soul.

He could sense that this spear had been specially made to target him. The energy on the spear countered and suppressed the origin energy of a monster hunter inside his body.

When the spear entered his body, he felt his entire body go weak. The feeling of weakness that reached all the way to his bones made it difficult for him to even lift a finger.

Behind him, Pavilion Master Chu Two was holding a spear with a calm expression on her face. She had thrust the spear with both of her hands, calmly piercing the waist of the Immortal.

The Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion was her domain, and she could do a lot of incredible things in this place... Such as concealing her aura completely.

This was especially so with Song Shuhang present and attracting the attention of the Immortal. With him attracting all the attention, she only needed to leave a projection in the distance, and then step by step move to the side of the Immortal and thrust the spear.

Pavilion Master Chu Two said slowly, “This is a move that I’ve played millions of times in my mind.”

During the long period since their last encounter, she had repeatedly thought of what she would do if she were to meet the monster hunter that had destroyed the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion again.

She had collected information about this monster hunter through every possible method, so she knew that he had become an Immortal and was one of the founders of the Ancient Heavenly City. She then went to collect a large number of his battle records. Whether it was his duels in the Heavenly City or his numerous battles with experts all over the universe, she collected them all, though most of them had come from Slow-Witted Song.

Anyway, both Pavilion Master Chu and Pavilion Master Chu Two had a database on this monster hunter. After repeated simulations, they had come up with nearly 10,000 ways to deal with this monster hunter while in the domain of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion.

Pavilion Master Chu Two said calmly, “It’s a pity this isn’t your main body.”

In the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion below, a metal column rose to form a giant tree. Behind the metal tree, there was a projection of the Thriving and Withering Trees, which then attached themselves to the giant metal tree, forming a powerful seal.

The giant metal tree rose up and swallowed the Immortal monster hunter.

Killing an Immortal-level powerhouse was never easy, even if it was just a clone. As such, Pavilion Master Chu Two’s plan was to seal the Immortal monster hunter and grind him to death slowly.

[She played that single move millions of times in her mind... A woman’s drive to seek revenge is truly terrifying.] The monster hunter tried to restore his energy, but his origin energy seemed to have been completely sealed.

Still, you’re too naive if you think I can be dealt with so easily...

He was an Immortal, and even a clone of his would not be dealt with so easily.

You have paid too much attention to my identity as a monster hunter... While I have lost the origin energy of a monster hunter, I can use other forms of energy just fine,?the monster hunter said in his mind.

In addition to the origin energy of a monster hunter, there was another form of energy hidden in his body. This energy was energy that he was born with. He, himself, did not know where this energy had come from, but it was undoubtedly a terrifying and powerful form of energy.

Moreover, even though this was a clone, he could still summon this energy.

As the giant metal tree reached his body, it tried to swallow him.

After switching up his origin energy, the Immortal monster hunter began to struggle. His body slowly squirmed its way out of the seal of the giant metal tree, like an evil ghost crawling its way out of hell.

At the same time, all of the eyes that covered his body shot beams of light unceasingly, preventing Song Shuhang and Pavilion Master Chu Two from approaching and giving him some time to break free from the seal of the giant metal tree.

While he was crawling out of the seal, his right hand grabbed at the spear that had pierced him through the back and tried pulling it out as he wanted to unseal his origin monster hunter energy.

Song Shuhang summoned the Giant King’s Robe again and said, “I’ll block these beams. Senior Chu, you can go and stab him again.”

“Don’t worry, this is the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion,” Pavilion Master Chu Two said confidently.

“It’s too late! Hahaha.” The monster hunter struggled with all his might, and most of his body had already emerged from the metal tree.

Just as his body was about to break out of the metal tree, Song Shuhang appeared before his eyes.

It was a version of Song Shuhang made of steel. It had appeared out of nowhere, dodging all of the light beams that had filled the sky.

This steel manifestation of Song Shuhang seemed to be in a different dimension; the beams of light simply passed through his body, as if it wasn’t even there.

The steel Song Shuhang said, “Have a good rest.”

He then brought out a short blade and stabbed it right into the forehead of the monster hunter.

The monster hunter roared, “Tyrannical... Song...!!!”

He raised his hand to stop the other party, but the steel Song Shuhang’s arm passed right through his defenses, inserting the short blade right into his forehead.

This short blade had the same effect as the spear that Pavilion Master Chu Two had used; it seemed to have been specially made for this monster hunter. The spear sealed his monster hunter origin energy, while the short blade sealed his hidden reserve of origin energy.

The monster hunter roared, “Impossible! How and why do you know about my hidden reserve of origin energy?”

No, this isn’t a Tyrannical Song...

The monster hunter howled, “Who are you?!”

The steel Song Shuhang placed his finger against his lips. “Shh~”

Afterward, he raised his foot, stepped on the face of the monster hunter, and sent him back into the seal of the giant metal tree.

“You who’s surnamed... Song...” The monster hunter’s voice trailed off mid-sentence, becoming softer and softer until it could no longer be heard. During this time, his body had been swallowed back into the metal tree, getting sealed for good.

As for the steel Song Shuhang, when the light beams disappeared, so did he. There was not a single trace of evidence that he had even been there.

He had appeared out of nowhere, disappearing in the same manner.

??????

“The seal worked?” Song Shuhang looked puzzled.

“Mm-hm.” Pavilion Master Chu Two nodded after confirming that the Immortal monster hunter had been sealed in the giant metal tree. Then, she asked, “By the way... that steel version of you just now, was that your clone?”

“The steel version of me?” Song Shuhang immediately remembered his poor steel manifestation.

Nowadays, all big shots liked to “borrow” things from newbies.

There were some who borrowed ghost spirits, some who borrowed clones or manifestations, and some who borrowed heads.

Back then, Song Shuhang’s poor steel manifestation had just been born, yet before he could even establish a deep connection with it, it had been taken away by the Heavenly Emperor along with the Sun Boat of the Black Dragon World.

Pavilion Master Chu Two replied, “Yes, that steel version of yours appeared all of a sudden, inserting a short blade into the forehead of the monster hunter. In doing so, the other kind of energy in his body was sealed. Then, your steel-self kicked him back into my seal.”

The steel Song Shuhang appeared under the cover of the beam attacks of the monster hunter, and disappeared alongside the beams. However, the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion was her world, and nothing that happened inside this world could escape her senses.

Song Shuhang said, “No, that doesn’t make sense.”

Pavilion Master Chu Two asked, “What? Why?”

Song Shuhang replied, “If it really was a steel version of me, then it should have been my steel manifestation. However, my steel manifestation is under the control of the Heavenly Emperor. She stole it and took control over it using a secret technique, and I can’t summon it back.”

If it was really his steel manifestation, then didn’t that mean that the Heavenly Emperor had just controlled it to assist Pavilion Master Chu Two in sealing the Immortal monster hunter?

But the problem with that scenario was that the monster was a subordinate of the Heavenly Emperor, and a loyal one at that. After the Ancient Heavenly City was destroyed, he had hunted down Cheng Lin frantically.

Why would the Heavenly Emperor help her enemy seal off her number one fan?

Unless... She was crazy.

It was also possible that what appeared just now was not Shuhang’s steel manifestation.

......

This matter truly made one think.

[Ding~ Your “Buddy,” the Heavenly Emperor, has remotely transferred you 10 seconds’ worth of strength. The cost of this transfer is 90% of this energy. Please check the transaction carefully.]

[Attached message: Yo, Senior Song. First of all, congratulations. You have sealed the clone of my Heavenly City’s Pioneer General. You fought very well in that battle, and you had the momentum of an Immortal. However, I still managed to recover a large portion of the Heavenly City Fragments outside the scholarly faction.]

It was the QR code Golden Core’s friend function.

The thing that annoyed Song Shuhang the most about this friend function was that Fairy Cheng Lin and other big shots could use all kinds of different sub-features of this ability of his, but he could only read the messages due to his low strength.

Song Shuhang: “...”

It really was the Heavenly Emperor!

Has her brain finally gone haywire?

No, with the character of the Heavenly Emperor, she must be scheming something.

She deliberately trapped the monster hunter’s clone into Pavilion Master Chu Two’s seal. Was everything part of her scheme?

Wait...

Is she trying to use this clone to take the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion away from Pavilion Master Chu Two?

In the past, before Pavilion Master Chu stepped onto her path to immortality, there were survivors of the Ancient Heavenly City in the Beast Realm who wanted to seize her Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion and use it to rebuild the Heavenly City.

Now that the Heavenly Emperor was reborn and trying to rebuild the Heavenly City, it was very likely that she was eyeing the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion!

[Ding~ Your “Buddy,” the Heavenly Emperor, has transmitted another 10 seconds’ worth of strength, along with the message: Senior Song, let me guess. Are you thinking that my brain has gone haywire? Let me tell you this, I haven’t gone crazy and I’m completely fine. As for what I’m planning on doing, how about you guess? If you guess it right, I’ll give you a reward.]

Another message appeared in Song Shuhang’s mind.

“Senior Chu, can you check the seal again? Try looking for any loopholes or weaknesses in the seal,” urged Song Shuhang. “The steel version of me that appeared just now was indeed my steel manifestation, and it was the Heavenly Emperor who had been controlling it.”

Pavilion Master Chu Two nodded. She checked her seal repeatedly, carefully inspecting every single part of it. At the same time, Pavilion Master Chu’s hair had also come to Chu Two’s assistance, helping her inspect the seal.

After a while.

“There doesn’t seem to be any problem with the seal,” said Pavilion Master Chu Two.

The clone of the Immortal monster hunter had been sealed, and it would stay in that state all the way until it died. Moreover, with the spear in its abdomen and the short blade in its forehead sealing its origin energies, there was nothing it could do to escape.

Pavilion Master Chu added, “With the power of the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion, we can weaken the clone to its limit while it’s inside the seal and kill it within a year at most.”

Song Shuhang said, “The short blade in the clone’s forehead belongs to the Heavenly Emperor. Is it possible that she has a way to make the short blade ineffective and allow the monster hunter to break free from the seal?”

“Actually, I had some information on the second form of origin energy that the monster hunter possessed,” said Pavilion Master Chu Two slowly. “I had long considered this possibility when I designed the seal. Even if the short blade in the clone’s forehead were to lose its effect, it will not affect the seal.”

Song Shuhang rubbed his temples.

He really had no idea what the Heavenly Emperor was planning or thinking.

He was lacking information and clues.

Even if he were the reincarnation of the great detective Sherlock Holmes, he believed that he would have no way of figuring out the truth.

“I have to leave as I can’t stay in the main world for too long,” said Pavilion Master Chu Two. This was the price that she had to pay for fusing with Skylark’s head.

Song Shuhang said, “Be careful of the Ruler of the Netherworld Fat Ball.”

Pavilion Master Chu Two replied, “Don’t worry. I’m currently stuck in the Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion which lies between the Netherworld Realm and the main world. As long as I don’t go out on expeditions on my own, I shouldn’t face any problems.”

After saying that, the entire Crystal-Clear Water Pavilion disappeared along with her.

Song Shuhang found himself back in the rift valley.

“Senior, you were on an expedition today.” Song Shuhang sighed.

Pavilion Master Chu’s hair swayed gently. “Don’t worry about her, if she really gets in trouble... She can still rely on that other ruler.”

“That’s true.” Song Shuhang descended to the ground.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber returned to the Inner World, back to Lady Onion.

True Monarch White Crane asked, “Shuhang, where’s that big shot with arms covered in eyes?”

Song Shuhang replied, “He was sealed by me and Pavilion Master Chu.”

Sister White Dragon silently let out a sigh.

[By the way, Sister White Dragon, when we were sealing the clone of the monster hunter, the Heavenly Emperor appeared through my steel manifestation. She stabbed the monster hunter in the forehead, and kicked him into Pavilion Master Chu Two’s seal. Do you have any ideas on why she might have done that?] Song Shuhang transmitted his voice to Sister White Dragon.

Sister White Dragon: ∑(っ°Д°;)っ

This news was simply too staggering.

Sister White Dragon’s brain crashed.

The Immortal monster hunter was the vanguard of the Heavenly City, and he had contributed greatly to the expansion of the city. When the Heavenly City had to fight, he would be the first to go up and join the battle.

Among all the Immortals, he was the most loyal to the Heavenly Emperor.

Now, the Heavenly Emperor had backstabbed her most loyal general...

“Has she finally gone crazy?” After a long while, Sister White Dragon could only squeeze out these words.

Song Shuhang said, “That’s what I’m thinking too.”

Speaking of the Heavenly Emperor, where is she now?

Song Shuhang looked up at the black-hole-like obsession above his head. After checking it out, he estimated that the energy from the Indestructible Lord’s obsession could last a while longer.

Song Shuhang did not want to waste the materialized obsession.

What should I do with it?

The fat ball hasn’t arrived yet, and the same goes for that group of evil demons from the Netherworld that is supposed to head over to the scholarly faction.

I haven’t gotten any news from Senior White Two either.

Song Shuhang suddenly asked, “Sister White Dragon, you still haven’t added me as a friend through my QR code Golden Core Composition, right?”

Sister White Dragon waved her small claw and said, “Sixteen has already added you, so there’s no need for me to do that.”

Sixteen glanced at Song Shuhang and asked, “Shuhang, is there anything you’re having trouble with?”

Song Shuhang replied, “I wanted to ask the seniors how they’re able to impart their strength.”

Senior White’s clone, who was by the side, asked, “Doesn’t the Sage Seal have that function?”

Song Shuhang replied, “I’m not talking about the method where you use the Sage Seal. I’m more curious about how it’s done through the QR code Golden Core Composition’s friend function.”

If he could learn this trick, then even without the help of the Black Dragon World’s Dragon Network Assistant, he could send messages to others from afar.

“I don’t know anything about that. It doesn’t seem like I have any way of remotely transferring strength to you through the QR code Golden Core Composition.” Su Clan’s Sixteen pondered for a short moment, and then said, “Sister White Dragon, why don’t you add Song Shuhang as a friend and test this function?”

Sister White Dragon’s scratched her face with her little claws and said, “Alright.”

......

Song Shuhang willed it and projected the QR code Golden Core Composition from his Spirit Lake. “Sister White Dragon, try scanning this pattern with your mental energy.”

As soon as Song Shuhang finished speaking, he received a message.

[Beep~ The Indestructible Lord added you as a friend. Please select its group.]

Song Shuhang exclaimed, “F*ck!”

“What the heck? You startled me,” said Sister White Dragon. She had just gathered her mental energy and was about to scan the QR code Golden Core when Shuhang suddenly shouted, interrupting her.

Song Shuhang turned to look at the seniors and Sixteen. “The Indestructible Lord just added me as a friend.”

Senior White’s clone guessed, ??”It may be because the Indestructible Lord’s obsession is currently attached to you, which somehow drew over its mental energy.”

Sixteen asked worriedly, “What happens if the Indestructible Lord adds you as a friend? Will there be any problems?”

“From my previous experiences, I don’t think it’ll cause any problem,” replied Song Shuhang.

After all, the Heavenly Emperor was also there in his friend list, albeit under the “buddies” category. Still, Song Shuhang felt that such a label was much more fit for Doudou; after all, Doudou was a true buddy of his.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword said, “Then just ignore it for now. The Indestructible Lord has always been in a dormant state. Besides its obsession for objects that carry the aura of eternity, it has basically had no contact with the outside world.”

[Beep~ Ten seconds have passed. Do you want to include the Indestructible Lord in the list of unfamiliar friends?]

“Right, there was this function as well.” Song Shuhang nodded and replied, “Then place it inside the list of unfamiliar friends for now.”

[Beep~ The Indestructible Lord has added you as a friend, and has been included in the ‘unfamiliar friends’ list.]

[Beep~ The Indestructible Lord has perceived the aura of eternity, triggering a reaction.]

Song Shuhang blurted out, “Huh?”

What is going on?

In the next moment, Song Shuhang’s body swiftly rose into the air.

The obsession that possessed him began to act on its own.

Song Shuhang looked at Shadow Sanctum in his hand. At this time, the bracelet was covered with black and red patterns.

Shadow Sanctum could activate an obsession, transform it into a shadow, and then have it attached to a host who could use it as a source of energy. However, if the shadow were to encounter the very object of its obsession, there was a certain chance of it entering a violent and uncontrollable state.

“What is this kid doing?” Sister White Dragon picked up Sixteen and chased after Song Shuhang.

True Monarch White Crane brought out its immortal boat and took Senior White’s clone, who was in an energy-saving state, with it as it followed after them.

??????

Song Shuhang’s body flew upward at an increasingly faster rate.

Then, his figure suddenly disappeared.

Su Clan’s Sixteen wondered, “Was it a spatial teleportation?”

Senior White’s clone said, “It’s a hidden passage that leads to the Netherworld.”

In the sky above the scholarly faction, there was a hidden passage that led to the Netherworld. It seemed to be a new passage that had opened just recently.

“Should we chase after him?” asked True Monarch White Crane.

Senior White’s clone said, “No. I’ll contact someone, and we’ll wait for Shuhang near the passage.”

After saying that, Senior White’s clone tried to contact the person who Song Shuhang called Senior White Two. Its main body had once communicated with White Two and they had exchanged contact information.

Since there was a passage that led to the Netherworld Realm right here, then he should be able to contact White Two.

It was more suitable to leave matters related to the Netherworld to him.

Sister White Dragon’s little claw patted Sixteen’s head lightly. She could see that Sixteen was very anxious, so she tried calming her down.

At this moment, Sixteen’s phone rang.

It was Song Shuhang who was calling. His phone still managed to get a bit of signal even when he was inside the passage that led to the Netherworld.

Sixteen quickly answered the call.

“Sixteen, don’t follow me in,” Song Shuhang said from the other side. “Wait for me at the entrance of the passage. If I come out, catch me and run.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “What happened to you?”

Song Shuhang said, “I saw... some parts of Senior Skylark.”

These were parts of Skylark that had not been recycled by the giant turtles of disaster.

Seeing these parts, he wondered how Senior Skylark was doing.

The Indestructible Lord’s obsession continued to take him deeper into the passage.

After reaching a certain depth, his phone finally lost signal.

As such, Song Shuhang could only put away his phone. “Senior Skylark is still wandering in the Netherworld Realm all by herself...”

“It fits her character very well,” said the black Scarlet Heaven Sword. “But the question is, who is attacking her, and why haven’t those giant turtles of disaster come?”

Song Shuhang speculated, “It might be because there isn’t any aura of eternity on these body parts.”

Since the bone of eternity was still with the fat ball, the new parts of Senior Skylark’s body probably did not carry the aura of eternity, thus holding no attraction to the giant turtles of disaster.

As for who might have attacked her...

In the worst case, it could be the fat ball as Skylark had been aiming to mess with it.

“Be careful of what’s ahead.” The black Scarlet Heaven Sword gave Song Shuhang a reminder after sensing a strange aura ahead of them.

The obsession that was wrapped around Song Shuhang let out a strange cry and recklessly rushed forward.

At the end of the passage, a figure could vaguely be seen.

The Indestructible Lord’s obsession, which had become a “shell” around Song Shuhang, condensed what appeared to be a mouth, and spewed out flames.

These flames were extremely powerful.

But after spewing out those scary flames for a short while, the Indestructible Lord’s obsession calmed down.

Song Shuhang regained control.

Song Shuhang: “...”

The Indestructible Lord had recklessly rushed to an unknown place, provoking an enemy.

Then, it retreated and left the provoked enemy for Tyrannical Song to deal with...
